91void LeabraContextLayerSpec::Compute_Context(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
92 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::PLUS_PHASE) {
93 u->ext = u->act_m; // just use previous minus phase value!
94 }
95 else {
96 LeabraRecvCons* cg = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.SafeEl(0);
97 if(TestError(!cg, "Compute_Context", "requires one recv projection!")) {
98 return;
99 }
100 LeabraUnit* su = (LeabraUnit*)cg->Un(0);
101 if(TestError(!su, "Compute_Context", "requires one unit in recv projection!")) {
102 return;
103 }
104 u->ext = updt.fm_prv * u->act_p + updt.fm_hid * su->act_p; // compute new value
105 }
106 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
107 u->Compute_HardClamp(net);
108}
109
110void LeabraContextLayerSpec::Compute_HardClamp(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
111 lay->hard_clamped = true; // cache this flag
112 lay->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
113 bool do_update = lay->GetUserDataDef(do_update_key, false).toBool();
114 if (do_update) {
115 lay->SetUserData(do_update_key, false); // reset
116 } else { // not explicit triger, so try other conditions
117 switch (update_criteria) {
118 case UC_TRIAL:
119 do_update = true;
120 break;
121 case UC_MANUAL: break; // weren't triggered, so that's it
122 case UC_N_TRIAL: {
123 // do modulo the trial, adding offset -- add 1 so first trial is not trigger
124 do_update = (((net->trial + n_spec.n_offs + 1) % n_spec.n_trials) == 0);
125 } break;
126 }
127 }
128 if (!do_update) return;
129
130 lay->Inhib_SetVals(inhib.kwta_pt); // assume 0 - 1 clamped inputs
131
132 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
133 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
134 Compute_Context(lay, u, net);
135 }
136 Compute_CycleStats(lay, net);
137}
138
139void LeabraContextLayerSpec::TriggerUpdate(LeabraLayer* lay) {
140 if (!lay) return;
141 if (TestError((lay->spec.spec.ptr() != this),
142 "TriggerUpdate", "Spec does not belong to the layer passed as arg"))
143 return;
144 lay->SetUserData(do_update_key, true);
145}
146
147void LeabraLayer::TriggerContextUpdate() {
148 LeabraContextLayerSpec* cls = dynamic_cast<LeabraContextLayerSpec*>
149 (spec.spec.ptr());
150 if (cls) {
151 cls->TriggerUpdate(this);
152 }
153}

176
177void DeepContextLayerSpec::Compute_Context(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
178 LeabraRecvCons* cg = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.SafeEl(0);
179 if(TestError(!cg, "Compute_Context", "requires one recv projection!")) {
180 return;
181 }
182 LeabraUnit* su = (LeabraUnit*)cg->Un(0);
183 if(TestError(!su, "Compute_Context", "requires one unit in recv projection!")) {
184 return;
185 }
186 LeabraUnitSpec* rus = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
187 if(net->phase_no >= 2) {
188 u->act = u->act_p; // just use last plus phase state
189 }
190 else {
191 u->act = su->act_eq;
192 }
193 u->act_eq = u->act_nd = u->act;
194 u->da = 0.0f; // I'm fully settled!
195 u->AddToActBuf(rus->syn_delay);
196}
197
198void DeepContextLayerSpec::Compute_CycleStats(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
199 lay->Inhib_SetVals(inhib.kwta_pt); // assume 0 - 1 clamped inputs
200 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
201 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
202 Compute_Context(lay, u, net);
203 }
204 inherited::Compute_CycleStats(lay, net);
205}

210void LeabraMultCopyLayerSpec::Initialize() {
211 one_minus = false;
212 mult_gain = 1.0f;
213}
214
215bool LeabraMultCopyLayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
216 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
217 bool rval = inherited::CheckConfig_Layer(lay, quiet);
218
219 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
220 if(lay->CheckError(u == NULL__null, quiet, rval,
221 "leabra mult copy layer doesn't have any units:", lay->name)) {
222 return false; // fatal
223 }
224
225 if(lay->CheckError(u->recv.size != 2, quiet, rval,
226 "leabra mult copy layer must have exactly 2 recv prjns, first = act to copy, second = act to multiply:", lay->name)) {
227 return false; // fatal
228 }
229
230 LeabraRecvCons* copy_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(0);
231 if(lay->CheckError(copy_gp->size != 1, quiet, rval,
232 "leabra mult copy layer first prjn (copy act source) must have exactly 1 connection to copy from:", lay->name)) {
233 return false; // fatal
234 }
235 LeabraRecvCons* mult_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(1);
236 if(lay->CheckError(mult_gp->size != 1, quiet, rval,
237 "leabra mult copy layer second prjn (mult act source) must have exactly 1 connection to get mult act from:", lay->name)) {
238 return false; // fatal
239 }
240 return rval;
241}
242
243void LeabraMultCopyLayerSpec::Compute_MultCopyAct(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
244 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
245 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
246 if(u->recv.size < 2) continue;
247
248 LeabraRecvCons* copy_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(0);
249 LeabraRecvCons* mult_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(1);
250
251 if(copy_gp->size != 1) continue;
252 if(mult_gp->size != 1) continue;
253
254 LeabraUnitSpec* rus = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
255
256 LeabraUnit* copy_un = (LeabraUnit*)copy_gp->Un(0);
257 LeabraUnit* mult_un = (LeabraUnit*)mult_gp->Un(0);
258
259 float mult_eff = mult_gain * mult_un->act_eq;;
260 if(mult_eff > 1.0f) mult_eff = 1.0f;
261 float new_act;
262 if(one_minus)
263 new_act = copy_un->act_eq * (1.0f - mult_eff);
264 else
265 new_act = copy_un->act_eq * mult_eff;
266 u->act = new_act;
267 u->act_eq = u->act_nd = u->act;
268 u->da = 0.0f; // I'm fully settled!
269 u->AddToActBuf(rus->syn_delay);
270 }
271}
272
273void LeabraMultCopyLayerSpec::Compute_CycleStats(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
274 Compute_MultCopyAct(lay, net);
275 inherited::Compute_CycleStats(lay, net);
276}

287void LeabraLinUnitSpec::Initialize() {
288 SetUnique("act_fun", true);
289 SetUnique("act_range", true);
290 SetUnique("clamp_range", true);
291 SetUnique("act", true);
292 act_fun = LINEAR;
293 act_range.max = 20;
294 act_range.min = 0;
295 act_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
296 clamp_range.max = 1.0f;
297 clamp_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
298 act.gain = 2;
299}
300
301void LeabraLinUnitSpec::Compute_ActFmVm(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net) {
302 float new_act = u->net * act.gain; // use linear netin as act
303
304 u->da = new_act - u->act;
305 if((noise_type == ACT_NOISE) && (noise.type != Random::NONE) && (net->cycle >= 0)) {
306 new_act += Compute_Noise(u, net);
307 }
308 u->act = u->act_nd = u->act_eq = act_range.Clip(new_act);
309}

327bool XCalSRAvgConSpec::CheckConfig_RecvCons(RecvCons* cg, bool quiet) {
328 bool rval = true;
329 if((learn_rule == CTLEABRA_CAL) || (learn_rule == CTLEABRA_XCAL)) {
330 if(cg->prjn) {
331 if(cg->prjn->CheckError(!cg->prjn->con_type->InheritsFrom(&TA_LeabraSRAvgCon), quiet, rval,
332 "does not have con_type = LeabraSRAvgCon -- required for CTLEABRA_CAL or _XCAL learning to hold the sravg connection-level values -- I just fixed this for you in this projection, but must do Build to get it to take effect")) {
333 cg->prjn->con_type = &TA_LeabraSRAvgCon;
334 }
335 }
336 }
337 return rval;
338}

389//////////////////////////////////
390// CycleSynDepConSpec //
391//////////////////////////////////
392
393void CycleSynDepSpec::Initialize() {
394 rec = 0.002f;
395 asymp_act = 0.4f;
396 depl = rec * (1.0f - asymp_act); // here the drive is constant
397}
398
399void CycleSynDepSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
400 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
401
402 if(rec < .00001f) rec = .00001f;
403 // chg = rec * (1 - cur) - dep * drive = 0; // equilibrium point
404 // rec * (1 - cur) = dep * drive
405 // dep = rec * (1 - cur) / drive
406 depl = rec * (1.0f - asymp_act); // here the drive is constant
407 depl = MAX(depl, 0.0f)(((depl) > (0.0f)) ? (depl) : (0.0f));
408}
409
410void CycleSynDepConSpec::Initialize() {
411 min_obj_type = &TA_CycleSynDepCon;
412}
413
414void CycleSynDepConSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
415 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
416 syn_dep.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
417}

581void LeabraXCALSpikeConSpec::GraphXCALSpikeSim(DataTable* graph_data,
582 LeabraUnitSpec* unit_spec,
583 float rate_min, float rate_max, float rate_inc,
584 float max_time, int reps_per_point,
585 float lin_norm) {
586 taProject* proj = GET_MY_OWNER(taProject)(taProject *) GetOwner(&TA_taProject);
587 if(!graph_data) {
588 graph_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(name + "_XCALSpikeSim", true);
589 }
590
591 bool local_us = false;
592 if(!unit_spec) {
593 unit_spec = new LeabraUnitSpec;
594 local_us = true;
595 }
596
597 StringtaString sim_data_name = name + "_XCALSpikeSim_Tmp";
598 DataTable* sim_data = proj->GetNewAnalysisDataTable(sim_data_name, true);
599
600 sim_data->StructUpdate(true);
601// graph_data->ResetData();
602 int idx;
603
604// DataTable sim_data;
605// taBase::Ref(sim_data);
606 DataCol* sim_r_rate = sim_data->FindMakeColName("r_rate", idx, VT_FLOAT);
607 DataCol* sim_s_rate = sim_data->FindMakeColName("s_rate", idx, VT_FLOAT);
608 DataCol* sim_ca_avg = sim_data->FindMakeColName("ca_avg", idx, VT_FLOAT);
609 DataCol* sim_sravg_ss = sim_data->FindMakeColName("sravg_ss", idx, VT_FLOAT);
610 DataCol* sim_sravg_s = sim_data->FindMakeColName("sravg_s", idx, VT_FLOAT);
611 DataCol* sim_sravg_m = sim_data->FindMakeColName("sravg_m", idx, VT_FLOAT);
612 DataCol* sim_srprod_s = sim_data->FindMakeColName("srprod_s", idx, VT_FLOAT);
613 DataCol* sim_srprod_m = sim_data->FindMakeColName("srprod_m", idx, VT_FLOAT);
614 DataCol* sim_sravg_lin = sim_data->FindMakeColName("sravg_lin", idx, VT_FLOAT);
615
616 float s_rate, r_rate;
617 for(r_rate = rate_min; r_rate <= rate_max; r_rate += rate_inc) {
618 for(s_rate = rate_min; s_rate <= rate_max; s_rate += rate_inc) {
619 for(int rep=0; rep < reps_per_point; rep++) {
620 float nmda = 0.0f;
621 float ca = 0.0f;
622 float ca_avg = 0.0f;
623 float ca_sum = 0.0f;
624 float vmd = 0.0f;
625 float r_p = r_rate / 1000.0f;
626 float s_p = s_rate / 1000.0f;
627 float time = 0.0f;
628 bool s_act = false;
629 bool r_act = false;
630 float s_avg = 0.0f;
631 float r_avg = 0.0f;
632 float s_lin = 0.0f;
633 float r_lin = 0.0f;
634 float s_avg_s = 0.15f;
635 float s_avg_m = 0.15f;
636 float r_avg_s = 0.15f;
637 float r_avg_m = 0.15f;
638 float sravg_ss = 0.15f;
639 float sravg_s = 0.15f;
640 float sravg_m = 0.15f;
641 for(time = 0.0f; time < max_time; time += 1.0f) {
642 s_act = (bool)Random::Poisson(s_p);
643 r_act = (bool)Random::Poisson(r_p);
644 if(r_act) {
645 vmd += unit_spec->spike_misc.vm_dend;
646 r_avg += 1.0f;
647 }
648 vmd -= vmd / unit_spec->spike_misc.vm_dend_dt;
649 float dnmda = -nmda * xcal_spike.nmda_rate;
650 float dca = (nmda * (xcal_spike.ca_v_nmda * vmd + xcal_spike.ca_nmda))
651 - (ca * xcal_spike.ca_rate);
652 if(s_act) { s_avg += 1.0f; dnmda += xcal_spike.k_ca / (xcal_spike.k_ca + ca); }
653 if(r_act) { dca += xcal_spike.ca_vgcc; }
654 nmda += dnmda;
655 ca += dca;
656 ca_sum += ca;
657
658 float sr = (ca - xcal_spike.ca_off); if(sr < 0.0f) sr = 0.0f;
659 sravg_ss += unit_spec->act_avg.ss_dt * (sr - sravg_ss);
660 sravg_s += unit_spec->act_avg.s_dt * (sravg_ss - sravg_s);
661 sravg_m += unit_spec->act_avg.m_dt * (sravg_s - sravg_m);
662
663 r_avg_s += unit_spec->act_avg.s_dt * ((float)r_act - r_avg_s);
664 r_avg_m += unit_spec->act_avg.m_dt * (r_avg_s - r_avg_m);
665 s_avg_s += unit_spec->act_avg.s_dt * ((float)s_act - s_avg_s);
666 s_avg_m += unit_spec->act_avg.m_dt * (s_avg_s - s_avg_m);
667 }
668 ca_avg = ca_sum / max_time;
669 s_lin *= lin_norm;
670 r_lin *= lin_norm;
671 float sravg_lin = s_avg * r_avg;
672
673 float srprod_s = r_avg_s * s_avg_s;
674 float srprod_m = r_avg_m * s_avg_m;
675
676 sim_data->AddBlankRow();
677 sim_r_rate->SetValAsFloat(r_rate, -1);
678 sim_s_rate->SetValAsFloat(s_rate, -1);
679 sim_ca_avg->SetValAsFloat(ca_avg, -1);
680 sim_sravg_ss->SetValAsFloat(sravg_ss, -1);
681 sim_sravg_s->SetValAsFloat(sravg_s, -1);
682 sim_sravg_m->SetValAsFloat(sravg_m, -1);
683 sim_srprod_s->SetValAsFloat(srprod_s, -1);
684 sim_srprod_m->SetValAsFloat(srprod_m, -1);
685 sim_sravg_lin->SetValAsFloat(sravg_lin, -1);
686 }
687 }
688 }
689
690 if(local_us) {
691 delete unit_spec;
692 }
693
694 sim_data->StructUpdate(false);
695
696 DataGroupSpec dgs;
697 taBase::Ref(dgs);
698 dgs.append_agg_name = false;
699 // dgs.SetDataTable(sim_data);
700 dgs.AddAllColumns(sim_data);
701 dgs.ClearColumns();
702
703 ((DataGroupEl*)dgs.ops[0])->agg.op = Aggregate::GROUP; // r_rate
704 ((DataGroupEl*)dgs.ops[1])->agg.op = Aggregate::GROUP; // s_rate
705 for(int i=2; i< dgs.ops.size; i++)
706 ((DataGroupEl*)dgs.ops[i])->agg.op = Aggregate::MEAN;
707
708 taDataProc::Group(graph_data, sim_data, &dgs);
709 dgs.ClearColumns();
710 taDataAnal::Matrix3DGraph(graph_data, "s_rate", "r_rate");
711
712 DataCol* gp_r_rate = graph_data->FindMakeColName("r_rate", idx, VT_FLOAT);
713 gp_r_rate->SetUserData("X_AXIS", true);
714 DataCol* gp_s_rate = graph_data->FindMakeColName("s_rate", idx, VT_FLOAT);
715 gp_s_rate->SetUserData("Z_AXIS", true);
716 DataCol* gp_sravg_m = graph_data->FindMakeColName("sravg_m", idx, VT_FLOAT);
717 gp_sravg_m->SetUserData("PLOT_1", true);
718 DataCol* gp_sravg_s = graph_data->FindMakeColName("sravg_s", idx, VT_FLOAT);
719 gp_sravg_s->SetUserData("PLOT_2", true);
720 DataCol* gp_srprod_m = graph_data->FindMakeColName("srprod_m", idx, VT_FLOAT);
721 gp_srprod_m->SetUserData("PLOT_3", true);
722 DataCol* gp_srprod_s = graph_data->FindMakeColName("srprod_s", idx, VT_FLOAT);
723 gp_srprod_s->SetUserData("PLOT_4", true);
724
725 graph_data->FindMakeGraphView();
726
727 proj->data.RemoveLeafName(sim_data_name); // nuke it
728}

749
750void ScalarValSpec::Initialize() {
751 rep = LOCALIST;
752 un_width = .3f;
753 norm_width = false;
754 clamp_pat = false;
755 clip_val = true;
756 send_thr = false;
757 init_nms = true;
758
759 min = val = 0.0f;
760 range = incr = 1.0f;
761 un_width_eff = un_width;
762
763 Defaults_init();
764}
765
766void ScalarValSpec::Defaults_init() {
767 min_sum_act = 0.2f;
768}
769
770void ScalarValSpec::InitRange(float umin, float urng) {
771 min = umin; range = urng;
772 un_width_eff = un_width;
773 if(norm_width)
774 un_width_eff *= range;
775}
776
777void ScalarValSpec::InitVal(float sval, int ugp_size, float umin, float urng) {
778 InitRange(umin, urng);
779 val = sval;
780 incr = range / (float)(ugp_size - 2); // skip 1st unit, and count end..
781 // incr -= .000001f; // round-off tolerance..
782}
783
784// rep 1.5. ugp_size = 4, incr = 1.5 / 3 = .5
785// 0 .5 1
786// oooo111122222 = val / incr
787
788// 0 .5 1 val = .8, incr = .5
789// 0 .4 .6
790// (.4 * .5 + .6 * 1) / (.6 + .4) = .8
791
792// act = 1.0 - (fabs(val - cur) / incr)
793
794
795float ScalarValSpec::GetUnitAct(int unit_idx) {
796 int eff_idx = unit_idx - 1;
797 if(rep == GAUSSIAN) {
798 float cur = min + incr * (float)eff_idx;
799 float dist = (cur - val) / un_width_eff;
800 return taMath_float::exp_fast(-(dist * dist));
801 }
802 else if(rep == LOCALIST) {
803 float cur = min + incr * (float)eff_idx;
804 if(fabs(val - cur) > incr) return 0.0f;
805 return 1.0f - (fabs(val - cur) / incr);
806 }
807 return 0.0f; // compiler food
808}
809
810float ScalarValSpec::GetUnitVal(int unit_idx) {
811 int eff_idx = unit_idx - 1;
812 float cur = min + incr * (float)eff_idx;
813 return cur;
814}
815
816void ScalarValBias::Initialize() {
817 un = NO_UN;
818 un_shp = VAL;
819 un_gain = 1.0f;
820 wt = NO_WT;
821 val = 0.0f;
822 wt_gain = 1.0f;
823}
824
825void ScalarValLayerSpec::Initialize() {
826 Defaults_init();
827}
828
829void ScalarValLayerSpec::Defaults_init() {
830 SetUnique("kwta", true);
831 SetUnique("gp_kwta", true);
832 SetUnique("inhib", true);
833 if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
834 kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
835 kwta.k = 3;
836 gp_kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
837 gp_kwta.k = 3;
838 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB;
839 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.25f;
840
841 unit_range.min = -0.5f; unit_range.max = 1.5f;
842 unit_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
843 scalar.InitRange(unit_range.min, unit_range.range); // needed for un_width_eff
844 val_range.min = unit_range.min + (.5f * scalar.un_width_eff);
845 val_range.max = unit_range.max - (.5f * scalar.un_width_eff);
846 }
847 else if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::LOCALIST) {
848 kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
849 kwta.k = 1;
850 gp_kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
851 gp_kwta.k = 1;
852 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
853 inhib.kwta_pt = .9f;
854
855 unit_range.min = 0.0f; unit_range.max = 1.0f;
856 unit_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
857 val_range.min = unit_range.min;
858 val_range.max = unit_range.max;
859
860 scalar.min_sum_act = .2f;
861 }
862 val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
863}
864
865void ScalarValLayerSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
866 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
867 unit_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
868 scalar.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
869 if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
870 scalar.InitRange(unit_range.min, unit_range.range); // needed for un_width_eff
871 val_range.min = unit_range.min + (.5f * scalar.un_width_eff);
872 val_range.max = unit_range.max - (.5f * scalar.un_width_eff);
873 }
874 else {
875 val_range.min = unit_range.min;
876 val_range.max = unit_range.max;
877 }
878 val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
879}
880
881void ScalarValLayerSpec::HelpConfig() {
882 StringtaString help = "ScalarValLayerSpec Computation:\n\
883 Uses distributed coarse-coding units to represent a single scalar value. Each unit\
884 has a preferred value arranged evenly between the min-max range, and decoding\
885 simply computes an activation-weighted average based on these preferred values. The\
886 current scalar value is displayed in the first unit in the layer, which can be clamped\
887 and compared, etc (i.e., set the environment patterns to have just one unit and provide\
888 the actual scalar value and it will automatically establish the appropriate distributed\
889 representation in the rest of the units). This first unit is only viewable as act_eq,\
890 not act, because it must not send activation to other units.\n\
891 \nScalarValLayerSpec Configuration:\n\
892 - The bias_val settings allow you to specify a default initial and ongoing bias value\
893 through a constant excitatory current (GC) or bias weights (BWT) to the unit, and initial\
894 weight values. These establish a distributed representation that represents the given .val\n\
895 - A self connection using the ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec can be made, which provides a bias\
896 for neighboring units to have similar values. It should usually have a fairly small wt_scale.rel\
897 parameter (e.g., .1)";
898 taMisc::Confirm(help);
899}
900
901bool ScalarValLayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
902 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
903 bool rval = inherited::CheckConfig_Layer(lay, quiet);
904
905 if(lay->CheckError(lay->un_geom.n < 3, quiet, rval,
906 "coarse-coded scalar representation requires at least 3 units, I just set un_geom.n")) {
907 if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::LOCALIST) {
908 lay->un_geom.n = 4;
909 lay->un_geom.x = 4;
910 }
911 else if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
912 lay->un_geom.n = 12;
913 lay->un_geom.x = 12;
914 }
915 }
916
917 if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::LOCALIST) {
918 kwta.k = 1; // localist means 1 unit active!!
919 gp_kwta.k = 1;
920 }
921
922 if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::GC) {
923 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
924 if(lay->CheckError(us->hyst.init, quiet, rval,
925 "bias_val.un = GCH requires UnitSpec hyst.init = false, I just set it for you in spec:", us->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
926 us->SetUnique("hyst", true);
927 us->hyst.init = false;
928 }
929 if(lay->CheckError(us->acc.init, quiet, rval,
930 "bias_val.un = GC requires UnitSpec acc.init = false, I just set it for you in spec:", us->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
931 us->SetUnique("acc", true);
932 us->acc.init = false;
933 }
934 }
935
936 // check for conspecs with correct params
937 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
938 if(lay->CheckError(u == NULL__null, quiet, rval,
939 "scalar val layer doesn't have any units:", lay->name)) {
940 return false; // fatal
941 }
942
943 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
944 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
945 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL__null) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL__null)) continue;
946 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
947 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec)) {
948 if(lay->CheckError(cs->wt_scale.rel > 0.5f, quiet, rval,
949 "scalar val self connections should have wt_scale < .5, I just set it to .1 for you (make sure this is appropriate for all connections that use this spec!)")) {
950 cs->SetUnique("wt_scale", true);
951 cs->wt_scale.rel = 0.1f;
952 }
953 if(lay->CheckError(cs->lrate > 0.0f, quiet, rval,
954 "scalar val self connections should have lrate = 0, I just set it for you in spec:", cs->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
955 cs->SetUnique("lrate", true);
956 cs->lrate = 0.0f;
957 }
958 }
959 else if(cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
960 continue;
961 }
962 }
963 return rval;
964}
965
966void ScalarValLayerSpec::ReConfig(Network* net, int n_units) {
967 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, net->layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay
= (LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
968 if(lay->spec.SPtr() != this) continue;
969
970 if(n_units > 0) {
971 lay->un_geom.n = n_units;
972 lay->un_geom.x = n_units;
973 }
974
975 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
976 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
977
978 if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::LOCALIST) {
979 scalar.min_sum_act = .2f;
980 kwta.k = 1;
981 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
982 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.9f;
983 us->g_bar.h = .03f; us->g_bar.a = .09f;
984 us->act_fun = LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_LINEAR;
985 us->act.thr = .17f;
986 us->act.gain = 220.0f;
987 us->act.nvar = .01f;
988 us->dt.vm = .05f;
989 bias_val.un = ScalarValBias::GC;
990 bias_val.wt = ScalarValBias::NO_WT;
991 unit_range.min = 0.0f; unit_range.max = 1.0f;
992
993 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
994 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
995 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL__null) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL__null)) continue;
996 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
997 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
998 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
999 continue;
1000 }
1001 cs->lmix.err_sb = false; // false: this is critical for linear mapping of vals..
1002 cs->rnd.mean = 0.1f;
1003 cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
1004 cs->wt_sig.gain = 1.0; cs->wt_sig.off = 1.0;
1005 }
1006 }
1007 else if(scalar.rep == ScalarValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
1008 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB;
1009 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.25f;
1010 us->g_bar.h = .015f; us->g_bar.a = .045f;
1011 us->act_fun = LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_XX1;
1012 us->act.thr = .25f;
1013 us->act.gain = 600.0f;
1014 us->act.nvar = .005f;
1015 us->dt.vm = .2f;
1016 bias_val.un = ScalarValBias::GC;
1017 bias_val.wt = ScalarValBias::NO_WT;
1018 unit_range.min = -.5f; unit_range.max = 1.5f;
1019
1020 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1021 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1022 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL__null) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL__null)) continue;
1023 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1024 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
1025 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
1026 continue;
1027 }
1028 cs->lmix.err_sb = true;
1029 cs->rnd.mean = 0.1f;
1030 cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
1031 cs->wt_sig.gain = 1.0; cs->wt_sig.off = 1.0;
1032 }
1033 }
1034 us->UpdateAfterEdit();
1035 }
1036 UpdateAfterEdit();
1037}
1038
1039// todo: deal with lesion flag in lots of special purpose code like this!!!
1040
1041void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_WtBias_Val(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md,
1042 int gpidx, float val) {
1043 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1044 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
1045 scalar.InitVal(val, nunits, unit_range.min, unit_range.range);
1046 for(int i=1;i<nunits;i++) {
1047 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1048 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1049 float act = .03f * bias_val.wt_gain * scalar.GetUnitAct(i);
1050 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1051 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1052 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1053 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
1054 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) continue;
1055 for(int ci=0;ci<recv_gp->size;ci++) {
1056 LeabraCon* cn = (LeabraCon*)recv_gp->PtrCn(ci);
1057 cn->wt += act;
1058 if(cn->wt < cs->wt_limits.min) cn->wt = cs->wt_limits.min;
1059 if(cn->wt > cs->wt_limits.max) cn->wt = cs->wt_limits.max;
1060 }
1061 recv_gp->Init_Weights_post(u);
1062 }
1063 }
1064}
1065
1066void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_UnBias_Val(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md,
1067 int gpidx, float val) {
1068 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1069 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
1070 scalar.InitVal(val, nunits, unit_range.min, unit_range.range);
1071 for(int i=1;i<nunits;i++) {
1072 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1073 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1074 float act = bias_val.un_gain * scalar.GetUnitAct(i);
1075 if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::GC)
1076 u->vcb.g_h = act;
1077 else if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::BWT)
1078 u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt = act;
1079 }
1080}
1081
1082void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_UnBias_NegSlp(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md,
1083 int gpidx) {
1084 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1085 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
1086 float val = 0.0f;
1087 float incr = bias_val.un_gain / (float)(nunits - 2);
1088 for(int i=1;i<nunits;i++) {
1089 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1090 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1091 if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::GC)
1092 u->vcb.g_a = val;
1093 else if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::BWT)
1094 u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt = -val;
1095 }
1096}
1097
1098void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_UnBias_PosSlp(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md,
1099 int gpidx) {
1100 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1101 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
1102 float val = bias_val.un_gain;
1103 float incr = bias_val.un_gain / (float)(nunits - 2);
1104 for(int i=1;i<nunits;i++) {
1105 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1106 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1107 if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::GC)
1108 u->vcb.g_h = val;
1109 else if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::BWT)
1110 u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt = val;
1111 }
1112}
1113
1114void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_BiasVal(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1115 if(bias_val.un != ScalarValBias::NO_UN) {
1116 if(bias_val.un_shp == ScalarValBias::VAL) {
1117 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Compute_UnBias_Val(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.val);)if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; Compute_UnBias_Val(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.val); } } else
{ Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; Compute_UnBias_Val
(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.val); };
1118 }
1119 else if(bias_val.un_shp == ScalarValBias::NEG_SLP) {
1120 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Compute_UnBias_NegSlp(lay, acc_md, gpidx);)if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; Compute_UnBias_NegSlp(lay, acc_md, gpidx); } } else { Layer
::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; Compute_UnBias_NegSlp
(lay, acc_md, gpidx); };
1121 }
1122 else if(bias_val.un_shp == ScalarValBias::POS_SLP) {
1123 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Compute_UnBias_PosSlp(lay, acc_md, gpidx);)if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; Compute_UnBias_PosSlp(lay, acc_md, gpidx); } } else { Layer
::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; Compute_UnBias_PosSlp
(lay, acc_md, gpidx); };
1124 }
1125 }
1126 if(bias_val.wt == ScalarValBias::WT) {
1127 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Compute_WtBias_Val(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.val);)if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; Compute_WtBias_Val(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.val); } } else
{ Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; Compute_WtBias_Val
(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.val); };
1128 }
1129}

1131void ScalarValLayerSpec::BuildUnits_Threads_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1132 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1133 LeabraNetwork* net) {

1135 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {

1140 net->units_flat.Add(un);
1141 }

gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; BuildUnits_Threads_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); } } else {
Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; BuildUnits_Threads_ugp
(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); };

1157void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_AvgMaxVals_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1158 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1159 AvgMaxVals& vals, ta_memb_ptr mb_off) {
1160 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1161 vals.InitVals();
1162 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
1163 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1164 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1165 if(i == 0) { continue; } // skip first unit
1166 float val = *((float*)MemberDef::GetOff_static((void*)u, 0, mb_off));
1167 vals.UpdtVals(val, i);
1168 }
1169 vals.CalcAvg(nunits);
1170}
1171
1172void ScalarValLayerSpec::ClampValue_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1173 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1174 LeabraNetwork*, float rescale) {
1175 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1176 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
1177 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx);
1178 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
1179 if(!clamp.hard)
1180 u->UnSetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
1181 else
1182 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
1183 float val = u->ext;
1184 if(scalar.clip_val)
1185 val = val_range.Clip(val); // first unit has the value to clamp
1186 scalar.InitVal(val, nunits, unit_range.min, unit_range.range);
1187 for(int i=1;i<nunits;i++) {
1188 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1189 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1190 float act = rescale * scalar.GetUnitAct(i);
1191 if(act < us->opt_thresh.send)
1192 act = 0.0f;
1193 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
1194 u->ext = act;
1195 }
1196}
1197
1198float ScalarValLayerSpec::ClampAvgAct(int ugp_size) {
1199 if(ugp_size < 3) return 0.0f;
1200 float val = val_range.min + .5f * val_range.Range(); // half way
1201 scalar.InitVal(val, ugp_size, unit_range.min, unit_range.range);
1202 float sum = 0.0f;
1203 for(int i=1;i<ugp_size;i++) {
1204 float act = scalar.GetUnitAct(i);
1205 sum += act;
1206 }
1207 sum /= (float)(ugp_size - 1);
1208 return sum;
1209}
1210
1211float ScalarValLayerSpec::ReadValue_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1212 LeabraNetwork* net) {
1213 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1214 if(nunits < 3) return 0.0f; // must be at least a few units..
1215
1216 scalar.InitVal(0.0f, nunits, unit_range.min, unit_range.range);
1217 float avg = 0.0f;
1218 float sum_act = 0.0f;
1219 for(int i=1;i<nunits;i++) {
1220 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1221 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1222 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
1223 float cur = scalar.GetUnitVal(i);
1224 float act_val = 0.0f;
1225 if(!scalar.send_thr || (u->act_eq >= us->opt_thresh.send)) // only if over sending thresh!
1226 act_val = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->act_eq) / us->clamp_range.max; // clipped & normalized!
1227 avg += cur * act_val;
1228 sum_act += act_val;
1229 }
1230 sum_act = MAX(sum_act, scalar.min_sum_act)(((sum_act) > (scalar.min_sum_act)) ? (sum_act) : (scalar.
min_sum_act));
1231 if(sum_act > 0.0f)
1232 avg /= sum_act;
1233 // set the first unit in the group to represent the value
1234 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx);
1235 u->act_eq = u->act_nd = avg;
1236 u->act = 0.0f; // very important to clamp act to 0: don't send!
1237 u->da = 0.0f; // don't contribute to change in act
1238 return u->act_eq;
1239}
1240
1241void ScalarValLayerSpec::ReadValue(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1242 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); } } else { Layer::AccessMode
acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md
, gpidx, net); };
1243}
1244
1245void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_ExtToPlus_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1246 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1247 LeabraNetwork*) {
1248 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1249 if(nunits < 3) return;
1250 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->GetUnitSpec();
1251 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
1252 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1253 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1254 if(i > 0) u->act_p = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->ext);
1255 else u->act_p = u->ext;
1256 u->act_dif = u->act_p - u->act_m;
1257 // important to clear ext stuff, otherwise it will get added into netin next time around!!
1258 u->ext = 0.0f;
1259 u->ext_flag = Unit::NO_EXTERNAL;
1260 }
1261}
1262
1263void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_ExtToAct_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1264 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1265 LeabraNetwork*) {
1266 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1267 if(nunits < 3) return;
1268 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->GetUnitSpec();
1269 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
1270 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1271 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
1272 if(i > 0) u->act_eq = u->act = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->ext);
1273 else u->act_eq = u->ext;
1274 u->ext = 0.0f;
1275 u->ext_flag = Unit::NO_EXTERNAL;
1276 }
1277}

1342void ScalarValLayerSpec::Settle_Init_Layer(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1343 inherited::Settle_Init_Layer(lay, net);
1344
1345 Settle_Init_Unit0(lay, net);
1346
1347 if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::BWT) {
1348 // if using bias-weight bias, keep a constant scaling (independent of layer size)
1349 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
1350 LeabraConSpec* bspec = (LeabraConSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec()->bias_spec.SPtr();
1351 u->bias_scale = bspec->wt_scale.abs; // still have absolute scaling if wanted..
1352 u->bias_scale /= 100.0f;
1353 }
1354 }

1357void ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_HardClamp(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1358 if(scalar.clamp_pat) {
1359 inherited::Compute_HardClamp(lay, net);
1360 return;
1361 }
1362 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT)) {
1363 lay->hard_clamped = false;
1364 return;
1365 }
1366 // allow for soft-clamping: translates pattern into exts first
1367 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, ClampValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; ClampValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); } } else { Layer::
AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; ClampValue_ugp
(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); };
1368 // now check for actual hard clamping
1369 if(!clamp.hard) {
1370 lay->hard_clamped = false;
1371 return;
1372 }
1373 HardClampExt(lay, net);
1374}

1380
1381float ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_SSE_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1382 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx, int& n_vals) {
1383 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx);
1384 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
1385 // only count if target value is within range -- otherwise considered a non-target
1386 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP) && val_range.RangeTestEq(u->targ)) {
1387 n_vals++;
1388 float uerr = u->targ - u->act_m;
1389 if(fabsf(uerr) < us->sse_tol)
1390 return 0.0f;
1391 return uerr * uerr;
1392 }
1393 return 0.0f;
1394}
1395
1396float ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_SSE(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*,
1397 int& n_vals, bool unit_avg, bool sqrt) {
1398 n_vals = 0;
1399 if(!(lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP))) return 0.0f;
1400 lay->sse = 0.0f;
1401 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals); )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals);
} } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx
= 0; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals
); };
1402 float rval = lay->sse;
1403 if(unit_avg && n_vals > 0)
1404 lay->sse /= (float)n_vals;
1405 if(sqrt)
1406 lay->sse = sqrtf(lay->sse);
1407 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
1408 (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE))) {
1409 rval = 0.0f;
1410 n_vals = 0;
1411 }
1412 return rval;
1413}
1414
1415float ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr_ugp(LeabraLayer* lay,
1416 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1417 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1418 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx);
1419 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
1420 // only count if target value is within range -- otherwise considered a non-target
1421 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP) && val_range.RangeTestEq(u->targ)) {
1422 float uerr = u->targ - u->act_m;
1423 if(fabsf(uerr) < us->sse_tol)
1424 return 0.0f;
1425 return fabsf(uerr);
1426 }
1427 return 0.0f;
1428}
1429
1430float ScalarValLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1431 lay->norm_err = -1.0f; // assume not contributing
1432 if(!lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP)) return -1.0f; // indicates not applicable
1433
1434 float nerr = 0.0f;
1435 float ntot = 0;
1436 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
1437 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
1438 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
1439 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
1440 ntot += unit_range.range;
1441 }
1442 }
1443 else {
1444 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
1445 ntot += unit_range.range;
1446 }
1447 if(ntot == 0.0f) return -1.0f;
1448
1449 lay->norm_err = nerr / ntot;
1450 if(lay->norm_err > 1.0f) lay->norm_err = 1.0f;
1451
1452 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
1453 (lay->HasExtFlag(Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE)))
1454 return -1.0f; // no contributarse
1455
1456 return lay->norm_err;
1457}

1460//////////////////////////////////
1461// Scalar Value Self Prjn //
1462//////////////////////////////////
1463
1464void ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
1465 init_wts = true;
1466 width = 3;
1467 wt_width = 2.0f;
1468 wt_max = 1.0f;
1469}
1470
1471void ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec::Connect_UnitGroup(Layer* lay,
1472 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
1473 Projection* prjn) {
1474// float neigh1 = 1.0f / wt_width;
1475// float val1 = expf(-(neigh1 * neigh1));
1476// float scale_val = wt_max / val1;
1477
1478 int n_cons = 2*width + 1;
1479 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
1480
1481 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
1482 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
1483 LeabraUnit* ru = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
1484
1485 if(!alloc_loop)
1486 ru->RecvConsPreAlloc(n_cons, prjn);
1487
1488 int j;
1489 for(j=-width;j<=width;j++) {
1490 int sidx = i+j;
1491 if((sidx < 0) || (sidx >= nunits)) continue;
1492 LeabraUnit* su = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, sidx, gpidx);
1493 if(!self_con && (ru == su)) continue;
1494 ru->ConnectFromCk(su, prjn);
1495 }
1496 }
1497 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
1498 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
1499 }
1500 }
1501}
1502
1503void ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
1504 if(!prjn->from) return;
1505 if(TestError(prjn->from.ptr() != prjn->layer, "Connect_impl", "must be used as a self-projection!")) {
1506 return;
1507 }
1508
1509 Layer* lay = prjn->layer;
1510 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Connect_UnitGroup(lay, acc_md, gpidx, prjn); )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; Connect_UnitGroup(lay, acc_md, gpidx, prjn); } } else { Layer
::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; Connect_UnitGroup
(lay, acc_md, gpidx, prjn); };
1511}
1512
1513void ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection*, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
1514 float neigh1 = 1.0f / wt_width;
1515 float val1 = expf(-(neigh1 * neigh1));
1516 float scale_val = wt_max / val1;
1517
1518 int ru_idx = ru->idx; // index within owning group
1519
1520 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
1521 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
1522 int su_idx = su->idx;
1523 float dist = (float)(ru_idx - su_idx) / wt_width;
1524 float wtval = scale_val * expf(-(dist * dist));
1525 cg->PtrCn(i)->wt = wtval;
1526 }
1527}
1528
1529//////////////////////////////////
1530// MotorForceLayerSpec //
1531//////////////////////////////////
1532
1533void MotorForceSpec::Initialize() {
1534 pos_width = .2f;
1535 vel_width = .2f;
1536 norm_width = true;
1537 clip_vals = true;
1538
1539 cur_pos = cur_vel = 0.0f;
1540 pos_min = vel_min = 0.0f;
1541 pos_range = vel_range = 1.0f;
1542
1543 pos_width_eff = pos_width;
1544 vel_width_eff = vel_width;
1545}
1546
1547void MotorForceSpec::InitRanges(float pos_min_, float pos_range_, float vel_min_, float vel_range_) {
1548 pos_min = pos_min_;
1549 pos_range = pos_range_;
1550 vel_min = vel_min_;
1551 vel_range = vel_range_;
1552 pos_width_eff = pos_width;
1553 vel_width_eff = vel_width;
1554 if(norm_width) {
1555 pos_width_eff *= pos_range;
1556 vel_width_eff *= vel_range;
1557 }
1558}
1559
1560void MotorForceSpec::InitVals(float pos, int pos_size, float pos_min_, float pos_range_,
1561 float vel, int vel_size, float vel_min_, float vel_range_) {
1562 InitRanges(pos_min_, pos_range_, vel_min_, vel_range_);
1563 cur_pos = pos;
1564 pos_incr = pos_range / (float)(pos_size-1);
1565 cur_vel = vel;
1566 vel_incr = vel_range / (float)(vel_size-1);
1567}
1568
1569float MotorForceSpec::GetWt(int pos_gp_idx, int vel_gp_idx) {
1570 float ug_pos = pos_min + pos_incr * (float)pos_gp_idx;
1571 float pos_dist = (ug_pos - cur_pos) / pos_width_eff;
1572 float ug_vel = vel_min + vel_incr * (float)vel_gp_idx;
1573 float vel_dist = (ug_vel - cur_vel) / vel_width_eff;
1574 return taMath_float::exp_fast(-(pos_dist * pos_dist + vel_dist * vel_dist));
1575}
1576
1577void MotorForceLayerSpec::Initialize() {
1578 pos_range.min = 0.0f;
1579 pos_range.max = 2.0f;
1580 vel_range.min = -.1f;
1581 vel_range.max = .1f;
1582 add_noise = true;
1583 force_noise.type = Random::GAUSSIAN;
1584 force_noise.var = .01f;
1585}
1586
1587void MotorForceLayerSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
1588 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
1589 pos_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1590 vel_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1591 force_noise.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1592}
1593
1594bool MotorForceLayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
1595 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
1596 bool rval = inherited::CheckConfig_Layer(lay, quiet);
1597 if(!rval) return rval;
1598
1599 if(lay->CheckError(!lay->unit_groups, quiet, rval,
1600 "requires unit groups -- I just set it for you")) {
1601 lay->unit_groups = true;
1602 }
1603 if(lay->CheckError(lay->gp_geom.x < 3, quiet, rval,
1604 "requires at least 3 unit groups in x axis -- I just set it for you")) {
1605 lay->gp_geom.x = 5;
1606 }
1607 if(lay->CheckError(lay->gp_geom.y < 3, quiet, rval,
1608 "requires at least 3 unit groups in y axis -- I just set it for you")) {
1609 lay->gp_geom.y = 5;
1610 }
1611 return rval;
1612}
1613
1614float MotorForceLayerSpec::ReadForce(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net, float pos, float vel) {
1615 if(motor_force.clip_vals) {
1616 pos = pos_range.Clip(pos);
1617 vel = vel_range.Clip(vel);
1618 }
1619 motor_force.InitVals(pos, lay->gp_geom.x, pos_range.min, pos_range.range,
1620 vel, lay->gp_geom.y, vel_range.min, vel_range.range);
1621
1622 float force = 0.0f;
1623 float wt_sum = 0.0f;
1624 for(int y=0; y<lay->gp_geom.y; y++) {
1625 for(int x=0; x<lay->gp_geom.x; x++) {
1626 float wt = motor_force.GetWt(x,y);
1627 int gpidx = y * lay->gp_geom.x + x;
1628 LeabraUnit* un0 = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(Layer::ACC_GP, 0, gpidx);
1629 force += wt * un0->act_eq;
1630 wt_sum += wt;
1631 }
1632 }
1633 if(wt_sum > 0.0f)
1634 force /= wt_sum;
1635 if(add_noise)
1636 force += force_noise.Gen();
1637 return force;
1638}
1639
1640void MotorForceLayerSpec::ClampForce(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net, float force, float pos, float vel) {
1641 if(motor_force.clip_vals) {
1642 pos = pos_range.Clip(pos);
1643 vel = vel_range.Clip(vel);
1644 }
1645 motor_force.InitVals(pos, lay->gp_geom.x, pos_range.min, pos_range.range,
1646 vel, lay->gp_geom.y, vel_range.min, vel_range.range);
1647
1648 for(int y=0; y<lay->gp_geom.y; y++) {
1649 for(int x=0; x<lay->gp_geom.x; x++) {
1650 float wt = motor_force.GetWt(x,y);
1651 int gpidx = y * lay->gp_geom.x + x;
1652 LeabraUnit* un0 = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(Layer::ACC_GP, 0, gpidx);
1653 un0->ext = force;
1654 ClampValue_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, gpidx, net, wt);
1655 }
1656 }
1657 lay->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
1658 lay->hard_clamped = clamp.hard;
1659 HardClampExt(lay, net);
1660 scalar.clamp_pat = true; // must have this to keep this clamped val
1661 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay,if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx
); u->ext = 0.0f; } } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer
::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->
UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx); u->ext = 0.0f; }
1662 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx);if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx
); u->ext = 0.0f; } } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer
::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->
UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx); u->ext = 0.0f; }
1663 u->ext = 0.0f; // must reset so it doesn't contribute!if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx
); u->ext = 0.0f; } } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer
::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->
UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx); u->ext = 0.0f; }
1664 )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP

); u->ext = 0.0f; } } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer
::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->
UnitAccess(acc_md, 0, gpidx); u->ext = 0.0f; };
1665}
1666
1667void MotorForceLayerSpec::Compute_BiasVal(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
1668 float vel_mid = .5f * (float)(lay->gp_geom.y-1);
1669 float pos_mid = .5f * (float)(lay->gp_geom.x-1);
1670 for(int y=0; y<lay->gp_geom.y; y++) {
1671 float vel_dist = -((float)y - vel_mid) / vel_mid;
1672 for(int x=0; x<lay->gp_geom.x; x++) {
1673 float pos_dist = -((float)x - pos_mid) / pos_mid;
1674 float sum_val = .5f * vel_dist + .5f * pos_dist;
1675 int gpidx = y * lay->gp_geom.x + x;
1676
1677 if(bias_val.un != ScalarValBias::NO_UN) {
1678 Compute_UnBias_Val(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, gpidx, sum_val);
1679 }
1680 if(bias_val.wt == ScalarValBias::WT) {
1681 Compute_WtBias_Val(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, gpidx, sum_val);
1682 }
1683 }
1684 }
1685}

1698
1699void TwoDValLeabraLayer::UpdateTwoDValsGeom() {
1700 TwoDValLayerSpec* ls = (TwoDValLayerSpec*)GetLayerSpec();
1701 if(!ls) return;
1702 if(ls->InheritsFrom(&TA_TwoDValLayerSpec)) {
1703 if(unit_groups)
1704 twod_vals.SetGeom(5, 2, TWOD_N, ls->twod.n_vals, gp_geom.x, gp_geom.y);
1705 else
1706 twod_vals.SetGeom(5, 2, TWOD_N, ls->twod.n_vals, 1, 1);
1707 }
1708}
1709
1710void TwoDValLeabraLayer::ApplyInputData_2d(taMatrix* data, Unit::ExtType ext_flags,
1711 Random* ran, const TwoDCoord& offs, bool na_by_range) {
1712 // only no unit_group supported!
1713 if(TestError(unit_groups, "ApplyInputData_2d",
1714 "input data must be 4d for layers with unit_groups: outer 2 are group dims, inner 2 are x,y vals and n_vals")) {
1715 return;
1716 }
1717 for(int d_y = 0; d_y < data->dim(1); d_y++) {
1718 int val_idx = offs.y + d_y;
1719 for(int d_x = 0; d_x < data->dim(0); d_x++) {
1720 int xy_idx = offs.x + d_x;
1721 Variant val = data->SafeElAsVar(d_x, d_y);
1722 if(ext_flags & Unit::EXT)
1723 twod_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, TWOD_EXT, val_idx, 0, 0);
1724 else
1725 twod_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, TWOD_TARG, val_idx, 0, 0);
1726 }
1727 }
1728}
1729
1730void TwoDValLeabraLayer::ApplyInputData_Flat4d(taMatrix* data, Unit::ExtType ext_flags,
1731 Random* ran, const TwoDCoord& offs, bool na_by_range) {
1732 // outer-loop is data-group (groups of x-y data items)
1733 if(TestError(!unit_groups, "ApplyInputData_Flat4d",
1734 "input data must be 2d for layers without unit_groups: x,y vals and n_vals")) {
1735 return;
1736 }
1737 for(int dg_y = 0; dg_y < data->dim(3); dg_y++) {
1738 for(int dg_x = 0; dg_x < data->dim(2); dg_x++) {
1739
1740 for(int d_y = 0; d_y < data->dim(1); d_y++) {
1741 int u_y = offs.y + dg_y * data->dim(1) + d_y; // multiply out data indicies
1742 for(int d_x = 0; d_x < data->dim(0); d_x++) {
1743 int u_x = offs.x + dg_x * data->dim(0) + d_x; // multiply out data indicies
1744 Unit* un = UnitAtCoord(u_x, u_y);
1745 if(un) {
1746 float val = data->SafeElAsVar(d_x, d_y, dg_x, dg_y).toFloat();
1747 un->ApplyInputData(val, ext_flags, ran, na_by_range);
1748 }
1749 }
1750 }
1751 }
1752 }
1753}
1754
1755void TwoDValLeabraLayer::ApplyInputData_Gp4d(taMatrix* data, Unit::ExtType ext_flags, Random* ran,
1756 bool na_by_range) {
1757 // outer-loop is data-group (groups of x-y data items)
1758 for(int dg_y = 0; dg_y < data->dim(3); dg_y++) {
1759 for(int dg_x = 0; dg_x < data->dim(2); dg_x++) {
1760
1761 for(int d_y = 0; d_y < data->dim(1); d_y++) {
1762 int val_idx = d_y;
1763 for(int d_x = 0; d_x < data->dim(0); d_x++) {
1764 int xy_idx = d_x;
1765 Variant val = data->SafeElAsVar(d_x, d_y, dg_x, dg_y);
1766 if(ext_flags & Unit::EXT)
1767 twod_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, TWOD_EXT, val_idx, dg_x, dg_y);
1768 else
1769 twod_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, TWOD_TARG, val_idx, dg_x, dg_y);
1770 }
1771 }
1772 }
1773 }
1774}

1779void TwoDValSpec::Initialize() {
1780 rep = GAUSSIAN;
1781 n_vals = 1;
1782 un_width = .3f;
1783 norm_width = false;
1784 clamp_pat = false;
1785 min_sum_act = 0.2f;
1786 mn_dst = 0.5f;
1787 clip_val = true;
1788
1789 x_min = x_val = y_min = y_val = 0.0f;
1790 x_range = x_incr = y_range = y_incr = 1.0f;
1791 x_size = y_size = 1;
1792 un_width_x = un_width_y = un_width;
1793}
1794
1795void TwoDValSpec::InitRange(float xmin, float xrng, float ymin, float yrng) {
1796 x_min = xmin; x_range = xrng; y_min = ymin; y_range = yrng;
1797 un_width_x = un_width;
1798 un_width_y = un_width;
1799 if(norm_width) {
1800 un_width_x *= x_range;
1801 un_width_y *= y_range;
1802 }
1803}
1804
1805void TwoDValSpec::InitVal(float xval, float yval, int xsize, int ysize, float xmin, float xrng, float ymin, float yrng) {
1806 InitRange(xmin, xrng, ymin, yrng);
1807 x_val = xval; y_val = yval;
1808 x_size = xsize; y_size = ysize;
1809 x_incr = x_range / (float)(x_size - 1); // DON'T skip 1st row, and count end..
1810 y_incr = y_range / (float)(y_size - 1); // DON'T skip 1st row, and count end..
1811 // incr -= .000001f; // round-off tolerance..
1812}
1813
1814float TwoDValSpec::GetUnitAct(int unit_idx) {
1815 int x_idx = unit_idx % x_size;
1816 int y_idx = (unit_idx / x_size);
1817 if(rep == GAUSSIAN) {
1818 float x_cur = x_min + x_incr * (float)x_idx;
1819 float x_dist = (x_cur - x_val) / un_width_x;
1820 float y_cur = y_min + y_incr * (float)y_idx;
1821 float y_dist = (y_cur - y_val) / un_width_y;
1822 float dist = x_dist * x_dist + y_dist * y_dist;
1823 return expf(-dist);
1824 }
1825 else if(rep == LOCALIST) {
1826 float x_cur = x_min + x_incr * (float)x_idx;
1827 float y_cur = y_min + y_incr * (float)y_idx;
1828 float x_dist = fabs(x_val - x_cur);
1829 float y_dist = fabs(y_val - y_cur);
1830 if((x_dist > x_incr) && (y_dist > y_incr)) return 0.0f;
1831
1832 return 1.0f - .5 * ((x_dist / x_incr) + (y_dist / y_incr)); // todo: no idea if this is right.
1833 }
1834 return 0.0f;
1835}
1836
1837void TwoDValSpec::GetUnitVal(int unit_idx, float& x_cur, float& y_cur) {
1838 int x_idx = unit_idx % x_size;
1839 int y_idx = (unit_idx / x_size);
1840 x_cur = x_min + x_incr * (float)x_idx;
1841 y_cur = y_min + y_incr * (float)y_idx;
1842}
1843
1844void TwoDValBias::Initialize() {
1845 un = NO_UN;
1846 un_gain = 1.0f;
1847 wt = NO_WT;
1848 wt_gain = 1.0f;
1849 x_val = 0.0f;
1850 y_val = 0.0f;
1851}
1852
1853void TwoDValLayerSpec::Initialize() {
1854 min_obj_type = &TA_TwoDValLeabraLayer;
1855
1856 SetUnique("kwta", true);
1857 kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
1858 kwta.k = 9;
1859 gp_kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
1860 gp_kwta.k = 9;
1861 SetUnique("inhib_group", true);
1862 inhib_group = ENTIRE_LAYER;
1863 SetUnique("inhib", true);
1864 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
1865 inhib.kwta_pt = .6f;
1866
1867 if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
1868 x_range.min = -0.5f; x_range.max = 1.5f; x_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1869 y_range.min = -0.5f; y_range.max = 1.5f; y_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1870 twod.InitRange(x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
1871 x_val_range.min = x_range.min + (.5f * twod.un_width_x);
1872 x_val_range.max = x_range.max - (.5f * twod.un_width_x);
1873 y_val_range.min = y_range.min + (.5f * twod.un_width_y);
1874 y_val_range.max = y_range.max - (.5f * twod.un_width_y);
1875 }
1876 else if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
1877 x_range.min = 0.0f; x_range.max = 1.0f; x_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1878 y_range.min = 0.0f; y_range.max = 1.0f; y_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1879 x_val_range.min = x_range.min; x_val_range.max = x_range.max;
1880 y_val_range.min = y_range.min; y_val_range.max = y_range.max;
1881 }
1882 x_val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui(); y_val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1883}
1884
1885void TwoDValLayerSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
1886 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
1887 x_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui(); y_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1888 twod.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1889 if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
1890 twod.InitRange(x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
1891 x_val_range.min = x_range.min + (.5f * twod.un_width_x);
1892 y_val_range.min = y_range.min + (.5f * twod.un_width_y);
1893 x_val_range.max = x_range.max - (.5f * twod.un_width_x);
1894 y_val_range.max = y_range.max - (.5f * twod.un_width_y);
1895 }
1896 else {
1897 x_val_range.min = x_range.min; y_val_range.min = y_range.min;
1898 x_val_range.max = x_range.max; y_val_range.max = y_range.max;
1899 }
1900 x_val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui(); y_val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
1901}
1902
1903void TwoDValLayerSpec::HelpConfig() {
1904 StringtaString help = "TwoDValLayerSpec Computation:\n\
1905 Uses distributed coarse-coding units to represent two-dimensional values. Each unit\
1906 has a preferred value arranged evenly between the min-max range, and decoding\
1907 simply computes an activation-weighted average based on these preferred values. The\
1908 current twod value is encoded in the twod_vals member of the TwoDValLeabraLayer (x1,y1, x2,y2, etc),\
1909 which are set by input data, and updated to reflect current values encoded over layer.\
1910 For no unit groups case, input data should be 2d with inner dim of size 2 (x,y) and outer dim\
1911 of n_vals size. For unit_groups, data should be 4d with two extra outer dims of gp_x, gp_y.\
1912 Provide the actual twod values in input data and it will automatically establish the \
1913 appropriate distributed representation in the rest of the units.\n\
1914 \nTwoDValLayerSpec Configuration:\n\
1915 - The bias_val settings allow you to specify a default initial and ongoing bias value\
1916 through a constant excitatory current (GC) or bias weights (BWT) to the unit, and initial\
1917 weight values. These establish a distributed representation that represents the given .val\n\
1918 - A self connection using the TwoDValSelfPrjnSpec can be made, which provides a bias\
1919 for neighboring units to have similar values. It should usually have a fairly small wt_scale.rel\
1920 parameter (e.g., .1)";
1921 taMisc::Confirm(help);
1922}
1923
1924bool TwoDValLayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
1925 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
1926 bool rval = inherited::CheckConfig_Layer(lay, quiet);
1927
1928 if(lay->CheckError(lay->un_geom.n < 3, quiet, rval,
1929 "coarse-coded twod representation requires at least 3 units, I just set un_geom.n")) {
1930 if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
1931 lay->un_geom.n = 9;
1932 lay->un_geom.x = 3;
1933 lay->un_geom.y = 3;
1934 }
1935 else if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
1936 lay->un_geom.n = 121;
1937 lay->un_geom.x = 11;
1938 lay->un_geom.y = 11;
1939 }
1940 }
1941
1942 if(lay->InheritsFrom(&TA_TwoDValLeabraLayer)) { // inh will be flagged above
1943 ((TwoDValLeabraLayer*)lay)->UpdateTwoDValsGeom();
1944 }
1945
1946 if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
1947 kwta.k = 1; // localist means 1 unit active!!
1948 gp_kwta.k = 1;
1949 }
1950
1951 if(bias_val.un == TwoDValBias::GC) {
1952 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
1953 if(lay->CheckError(us->hyst.init, quiet, rval,
1954 "bias_val.un = GCH requires UnitSpec hyst.init = false, I just set it for you in spec:", us->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
1955 us->SetUnique("hyst", true);
1956 us->hyst.init = false;
1957 }
1958 if(lay->CheckError(us->acc.init, quiet, rval,
1959 "bias_val.un = GC requires UnitSpec acc.init = false, I just set it for you in spec:", us->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
1960 us->SetUnique("acc", true);
1961 us->acc.init = false;
1962 }
1963 }
1964
1965 // check for conspecs with correct params
1966 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
1967 if(lay->CheckError(u == NULL__null, quiet, rval,
1968 "twod val layer doesn't have any units:", lay->name)) {
1969 return false; // fatal
1970 }
1971
1972 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
1973 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
1974 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL__null) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL__null)) continue;
1975 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
1976 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec)) {
1977 if(lay->CheckError(cs->wt_scale.rel > 0.5f, quiet, rval,
1978 "twod val self connections should have wt_scale < .5, I just set it to .1 for you (make sure this is appropriate for all connections that use this spec!)")) {
1979 cs->SetUnique("wt_scale", true);
1980 cs->wt_scale.rel = 0.1f;
1981 }
1982 if(lay->CheckError(cs->lrate > 0.0f, quiet, rval,
1983 "twod val self connections should have lrate = 0, I just set it for you in spec:", cs->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
1984 cs->SetUnique("lrate", true);
1985 cs->lrate = 0.0f;
1986 }
1987 }
1988 else if(cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
1989 continue;
1990 }
1991 }
1992 return rval;
1993}
1994
1995void TwoDValLayerSpec::ReConfig(Network* net, int n_units) {
1996 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, net->layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay
= (LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
1997 if(lay->spec.SPtr() != this) continue;
1998
1999 if(n_units > 0) {
2000 lay->SetNUnits(n_units);
2001 }
2002
2003 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
2004 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
2005
2006 if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
2007 twod.min_sum_act = .2f;
2008 kwta.k = 1;
2009 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
2010 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.9f;
2011 us->g_bar.h = .03f; us->g_bar.a = .09f;
2012 us->act_fun = LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_LINEAR;
2013 us->act.thr = .17f;
2014 us->act.gain = 220.0f;
2015 us->act.nvar = .01f;
2016 us->dt.vm = .05f;
2017 bias_val.un = TwoDValBias::GC; bias_val.wt = TwoDValBias::NO_WT;
2018 x_range.min = 0.0f; x_range.max = 1.0f;
2019 y_range.min = 0.0f; y_range.max = 1.0f;
2020
2021 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
2022 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
2023 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL__null) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL__null)) continue;
2024 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
2025 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
2026 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
2027 continue;
2028 }
2029 cs->lmix.err_sb = false; // false: this is critical for linear mapping of vals..
2030 cs->rnd.mean = 0.1f;
2031 cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
2032 cs->wt_sig.gain = 1.0; cs->wt_sig.off = 1.0;
2033 }
2034 }
2035 else if(twod.rep == TwoDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
2036 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB;
2037 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.25f;
2038 us->g_bar.h = .015f; us->g_bar.a = .045f;
2039 us->act_fun = LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_XX1;
2040 us->act.thr = .25f;
2041 us->act.gain = 600.0f;
2042 us->act.nvar = .005f;
2043 us->dt.vm = .2f;
2044 bias_val.un = TwoDValBias::GC; bias_val.wt = TwoDValBias::NO_WT;
2045 x_range.min = -.5f; x_range.max = 1.5f;
2046 y_range.min = -.5f; y_range.max = 1.5f;
2047
2048 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
2049 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
2050 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL__null) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL__null)) continue;
2051 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
2052 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
2053 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
2054 continue;
2055 }
2056 cs->lmix.err_sb = true;
2057 cs->rnd.mean = 0.1f;
2058 cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
2059 cs->wt_sig.gain = 1.0; cs->wt_sig.off = 1.0;
2060 }
2061 }
2062 us->UpdateAfterEdit();
2063 }
2064 UpdateAfterEdit();
2065}

2068
2069void TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_WtBias_Val(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2070 float x_val, float y_val) {
2071 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
2072 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
2073 twod.InitVal(x_val, y_val, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
2074 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2075 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
2076 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2077 float act = .03f * bias_val.wt_gain * twod.GetUnitAct(i);
2078 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
2079 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
2080 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
2081 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
2082 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) continue;
2083 for(int ci=0;ci<recv_gp->size;ci++) {
2084 LeabraCon* cn = (LeabraCon*)recv_gp->PtrCn(ci);
2085 cn->wt += act;
2086 if(cn->wt < cs->wt_limits.min) cn->wt = cs->wt_limits.min;
2087 if(cn->wt > cs->wt_limits.max) cn->wt = cs->wt_limits.max;
2088 }
2089 recv_gp->Init_Weights_post(u);
2090 }
2091 }
2092}

2094void TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_UnBias_Val(LeabraLayer* lay, Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2095 float x_val, float y_val) {
2096 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
2097 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
2098 twod.InitVal(x_val, y_val, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
2099 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2100 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
2101 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2102 float act = bias_val.un_gain * twod.GetUnitAct(i);
2103 if(bias_val.un == TwoDValBias::GC)
2104 u->vcb.g_h = act;
2105 else if(bias_val.un == TwoDValBias::BWT)
2106 u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt = act;
2107 }
2108}

gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; Compute_UnBias_Val(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val.x_val, bias_val

; int gpidx = 0; Compute_UnBias_Val(lay, acc_md, gpidx, bias_val

gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP

2123
2124void TwoDValLayerSpec::ClampValue_ugp(TwoDValLeabraLayer* lay,
2125 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2126 LeabraNetwork* net, float rescale) {
2127 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
2128 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
2129 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(gpidx);
2130 // first initialize to zero
2131 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->GetUnitSpec();
2132 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2133 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
2134 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2135 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
2136 u->ext = 0.0;
2137 }
2138 for(int k=0;k<twod.n_vals;k++) {
2139 float x_val = lay->GetTwoDVal(TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_X, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_EXT,
2140 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2141 float y_val = lay->GetTwoDVal(TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_Y, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_EXT,
2142 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2143 if(twod.clip_val) {
2144 x_val = x_val_range.Clip(x_val);
2145 y_val = y_val_range.Clip(y_val);
2146 }
2147 twod.InitVal(x_val, y_val, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
2148 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2149 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
2150 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2151 float act = rescale * twod.GetUnitAct(i);
2152 if(act < us->opt_thresh.send)
2153 act = 0.0f;
2154 u->ext += act;
2155 }
2156 }
2157}

2160 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); } } else { Layer::AccessMode
acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx = 0; ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md
, gpidx, net); };
2161}
2162
2163void TwoDValLayerSpec::ReadValue_ugp(TwoDValLeabraLayer* lay,
2164 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2165 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
2166 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
2167 twod.InitVal(0.0f, 0.0f, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
2168 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->GetUnitSpec();
2169 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(gpidx);
2170 if(twod.n_vals == 1) { // special case
2171 float x_avg = 0.0f; float y_avg = 0.0f;
2172 float sum_act = 0.0f;
2173 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2174 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
2175 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2176 float x_cur, y_cur; twod.GetUnitVal(i, x_cur, y_cur);
2177 float act_val = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->act_eq) / us->clamp_range.max; // clipped & normalized!
2178 x_avg += x_cur * act_val;
2179 y_avg += y_cur * act_val;
2180 sum_act += act_val;
2181 }
2182 sum_act = MAX(sum_act, twod.min_sum_act)(((sum_act) > (twod.min_sum_act)) ? (sum_act) : (twod.min_sum_act
));
2183 if(sum_act > 0.0f) {
2184 x_avg /= sum_act; y_avg /= sum_act;
2185 }
2186 // encode the value
2187 lay->SetTwoDVal(x_avg, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_X, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT,
2188 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2189 lay->SetTwoDVal(y_avg, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_Y, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT,
2190 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2191 }
2192 else { // multiple items
2193 // first find the max values, using sum of -1..+1 region
2194 static ValIdx_Array sort_ary;
2195 sort_ary.Reset();
2196 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2197 float sum = 0.0f;
2198 float nsum = 0.0f;
2199 for(int x=-1;x<=1;x++) {
2200 for(int y=-1;y<=1;y++) {
2201 int idx = i + y * lay->un_geom.x + x;
2202 if(idx < 0 || idx >= nunits) continue;
2203 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, idx, gpidx);
2204 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2205 float act_val = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->act_eq) / us->clamp_range.max; // clipped & normalized!
2206 nsum += 1.0f;
2207 sum += act_val;
2208 }
2209 }
2210 if(nsum > 0.0f) sum /= nsum;
2211 ValIdx vi(sum, i);
2212 sort_ary.Add(vi);
2213 }
2214 sort_ary.Sort();
2215 float mn_x = twod.mn_dst * twod.un_width_x * x_range.Range();
2216 float mn_y = twod.mn_dst * twod.un_width_y * y_range.Range();
2217 float mn_dist = mn_x * mn_x + mn_y * mn_y;
2218 int outi = 0; int j = 0;
2219 while((outi < twod.n_vals) && (j < sort_ary.size)) {
2220 ValIdx& vi = sort_ary[sort_ary.size - j - 1]; // going backward through sort_ary
2221 float x_cur, y_cur; twod.GetUnitVal(vi.idx, x_cur, y_cur);
2222 // check distance from all previous!
2223 float my_mn = x_range.Range() + y_range.Range();
2224 for(int k=0; k<j; k++) {
2225 ValIdx& vo = sort_ary[sort_ary.size - k - 1];
2226 if(vo.val == -1.0f) continue; // guy we skipped over before
2227 float x_prv, y_prv; twod.GetUnitVal(vo.idx, x_prv, y_prv);
2228 float x_d = x_cur - x_prv; float y_d = y_cur - y_prv;
2229 float dist = x_d * x_d + y_d * y_d;
2230 my_mn = MIN(dist, my_mn)(((dist) < (my_mn)) ? (dist) : (my_mn));
2231 }
2232 if(my_mn < mn_dist) { vi.val = -1.0f; j++; continue; } // mark with -1 so we know we skipped it
2233
2234 // encode the value
2235 lay->SetTwoDVal(x_cur, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_X, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT,
2236 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2237 lay->SetTwoDVal(y_cur, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_Y, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT,
2238 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2239 j++; outi++;
2240 }
2241 }
2242}

2245 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);

2299

2301 tdlay->UpdateTwoDValsGeom(); // quick, make sure no mismatch
2302

2304 // if using bias-weight bias, keep a constant scaling (independent of layer size)
2305 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr

2313void TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_HardClamp(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2314 if(twod.clamp_pat) {
2315 inherited::Compute_HardClamp(lay, net);
2316 return;
2317 }
2318 if(!(lay->ext_flag & Unit::EXT)) {
2319 lay->hard_clamped = false;
2320 return;
2321 }
2322 // allow for soft-clamping: translates pattern into exts first
2323 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, ClampValue_ugp((TwoDValLeabraLayer*)lay, acc_md, gpidx, net); )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; ClampValue_ugp((TwoDValLeabraLayer*)lay, acc_md, gpidx, net
); } } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx
= 0; ClampValue_ugp((TwoDValLeabraLayer*)lay, acc_md, gpidx,
net); };
2324 // now check for actual hard clamping
2325 if(!clamp.hard) {
2326 lay->hard_clamped = false;
2327 return;
2328 }
2329 HardClampExt(lay, net);
2330}
