2342
2343void TwoDValLayerSpec::PostSettle_ugp(TwoDValLeabraLayer* lay,
2344 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2345 LeabraNetwork* net) {
2346 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(gpidx);
2347
2348 bool no_plus_testing = false;
2349 if(net->no_plus_test && (net->train_mode == LeabraNetwork::TEST)) {
2350 no_plus_testing = true;
2351 }
2352
2353 for(int k=0;k<twod.n_vals;k++) {
2354 float x_val, y_val, x_m, y_m, x_p, y_p;
2355 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT,
2356 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2357 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_m, y_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2358 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2359 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_p, y_p, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2360 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2361
2362 switch(net->phase_order) {
2363 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS:
2364 if(no_plus_testing) {
2365 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2366 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2367 lay->SetTwoDVals(0.0f, 0.0f, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2368 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2369 }
2370 else {
2371 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
2372 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2373 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2374 }
2375 else {
2376 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2377 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2378 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2379 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2380 }
2381 }
2382 break;
2383 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_MINUS:
2384 if(no_plus_testing) {
2385 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2386 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2387 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2388 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2389 lay->SetTwoDVals(0.0f, 0.0f, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2390 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2391 }
2392 else {
2393 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
2394 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2395 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2396 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2397 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2398 }
2399 else {
2400 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2401 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2402 }
2403 }
2404 break;
2405 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_ONLY:
2406 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2407 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2408 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2409 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2410 lay->SetTwoDVals(0.0f, 0.0f, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2411 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2412 break;
2413 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
2414 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
2415 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2416 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2417 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2418 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2419 }
2420 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
2421 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2422 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2423 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2424 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2425 if(no_plus_testing) {
2426 // update act_m because it is actually another test case!
2427 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2428 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2429 }
2430 }
2431 else {
2432 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M2,
2433 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2434 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2435 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2436 }
2437 break;
2438 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_NOTHING:
2439 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2440 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2441 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2442 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2443 }
2444 else {
2445 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2446 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2447 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2448 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2449 }
2450 break;
2451 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
2452 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2453 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2454 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2455 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2456 }
2457 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
2458 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2459 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2460 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2461 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2462 }
2463 else {
2464 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P2,
2465 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2466 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val - x_p, y_val - y_p, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF2,
2467 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2468 }
2469 break;
2470 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
2471 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
2472 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
2473 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
2474 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2475 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2476 }
2477 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
2478 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P,
2479 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2480 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF,
2481 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2482 }
2483 else if(net->phase_no == 2) {
2484 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_P2,
2485 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2486 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val - x_p, y_val - y_p, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF2,
2487 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2488 }
2489 else {
2490 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_val, y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M2,
2491 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2492 lay->SetTwoDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_DIF2,
2493 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2494 }
2495 break;
2496 }
2497 }
2498}
2499
2500float TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_SSE_ugp(LeabraLayer* ly,
2501 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2502 int& n_vals) {
2503 TwoDValLeabraLayer* lay = (TwoDValLeabraLayer*)ly;
2504 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(gpidx);
2505 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->GetUnitSpec();
2506 float rval = 0.0f;
2507 for(int k=0;k<twod.n_vals;k++) { // first loop over and find potential target values
2508 float x_targ, y_targ;
2509 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_targ, y_targ, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_TARG, k,
2510 gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2511 // only count if target value is within range -- otherwise considered a non-target
2512 if(x_val_range.RangeTestEq(x_targ) && y_val_range.RangeTestEq(y_targ)) {
2513 n_vals++;
2514 // now find minimum dist actual activations
2515 float mn_dist = taMath::flt_max;
2516 for(int j=0;j<twod.n_vals;j++) {
2517 float x_act_m, y_act_m;
2518 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_act_m, y_act_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2519 j, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2520 float dx = x_targ - x_act_m;
2521 float dy = y_targ - y_act_m;
2522 if(fabsf(dx) < us->sse_tol) dx = 0.0f;
2523 if(fabsf(dy) < us->sse_tol) dy = 0.0f;
2524 float dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
2525 if(dist < mn_dist) {
2526 mn_dist = dist;
2527 lay->SetTwoDVals(dx, dy, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ERR,
2528 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2529 lay->SetTwoDVals(dx*dx, dy*dy, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_SQERR,
2530 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2531 }
2532 }
2533 rval += mn_dist;
2534 }
2535 }
2536 return rval;
2537}
2538
2539float TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_SSE(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*,
2540 int& n_vals, bool unit_avg, bool sqrt) {
2541 n_vals = 0;
2542 if(!(lay->ext_flag & (Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP))) return 0.0f;
2543 lay->sse = 0.0f;
2544 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay,if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals);
} } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx
= 0; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals
); }
2545 lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals);if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals);
} } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx
= 0; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals
); }
2546 )if(lay->unit_groups) { for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->
gp_geom.n; gpidx++) { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_GP
; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals);
} } else { Layer::AccessMode acc_md = Layer::ACC_LAY; int gpidx
= 0; lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, n_vals
); };
2547 float rval = lay->sse;
2548 if(unit_avg && n_vals > 0)
2549 lay->sse /= (float)n_vals;
2550 if(sqrt)
2551 lay->sse = sqrtf(lay->sse);
2552 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
2553 ((lay->ext_flag & Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE))) {
2554 rval = 0.0f;
2555 n_vals = 0;
2556 }
2557 return rval;
2558}
2559
2560float TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr_ugp(LeabraLayer* ly,
2561 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2562 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2563 TwoDValLeabraLayer* lay = (TwoDValLeabraLayer*)ly;
2564 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(gpidx);
2565 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->GetUnitSpec();
2566 float rval = 0.0f;
2567 for(int k=0;k<twod.n_vals;k++) { // first loop over and find potential target values
2568 float x_targ, y_targ;
2569 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_targ, y_targ, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_TARG, k,
2570 gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2571 // only count if target value is within range -- otherwise considered a non-target
2572 if(x_val_range.RangeTestEq(x_targ) && y_val_range.RangeTestEq(y_targ)) {
2573 // now find minimum dist actual activations
2574 float mn_dist = taMath::flt_max;
2575 for(int j=0;j<twod.n_vals;j++) {
2576 float x_act_m, y_act_m;
2577 lay->GetTwoDVals(x_act_m, y_act_m, TwoDValLeabraLayer::TWOD_ACT_M,
2578 j, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
2579 float dx = x_targ - x_act_m;
2580 float dy = y_targ - y_act_m;
2581 if(fabsf(dx) < us->sse_tol) dx = 0.0f;
2582 if(fabsf(dy) < us->sse_tol) dy = 0.0f;
2583 float dist = fabsf(dx) + fabsf(dy); // only diff from sse!
2584 if(dist < mn_dist)
2585 mn_dist = dist;
2586 }
2587 rval += mn_dist;
2588 }
2589 }
2590 return rval;
2591}
2592
2593float TwoDValLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
2594 lay->norm_err = -1.0f; // assume not contributing
2595 if(!(lay->ext_flag & (Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP))) return -1.0f; // indicates not applicable
2596
2597 float nerr = 0.0f;
2598 float ntot = 0;
2599 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && lay->unit_groups) {
2600 for(int g=0; g < lay->gp_geom.n; g++) {
2601 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(g);
2602 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_GP, g, (LeabraInhib*)gpd, net);
2603 ntot += x_range.range + y_range.range;
2604 }
2605 }
2606 else {
2607 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, Layer::ACC_LAY, 0, (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
2608 ntot += x_range.range + y_range.range;
2609 }
2610 if(ntot == 0.0f) return -1.0f;
2611
2612 lay->norm_err = nerr / ntot;
2613 if(lay->norm_err > 1.0f) lay->norm_err = 1.0f;
2614
2615 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
2616 ((lay->ext_flag & Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE)))
2617 return -1.0f; // no contributarse
2618
2619 return lay->norm_err;
2620}

2626}

2630}
2631
2632void DecodeTwoDValLayerSpec::ReadValue_ugp(TwoDValLeabraLayer* lay,
2633 Layer::AccessMode acc_md, int gpidx,
2634 LeabraNetwork* net) {
2635 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(acc_md);
2636 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
2637 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAccess(acc_md, i, gpidx);
2638 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
2639 if(u->recv.size == 0) continue;
2640 LeabraRecvCons* cg = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv[0];
2641 if(cg->size == 0) continue;
2642 LeabraUnit* su = (LeabraUnit*)cg->Un(0);
2643 u->net = su->net;
2644 u->act = su->act;
2645 u->act_eq = su->act_eq;
2646 u->act_nd = su->act_nd;
2647 }
2648 inherited::ReadValue_ugp(lay, acc_md, gpidx, net);
2649}

2656
2657void FourDValLeabraLayer::Initialize() {
2658}

2660void FourDValLeabraLayer::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
2661 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
2662 UpdateFourDValsGeom();
2663}
2664
2665void FourDValLeabraLayer::UpdateFourDValsGeom() {
2666 FourDValLayerSpec* ls = (FourDValLayerSpec*)GetLayerSpec();
2667 if(!ls) return;
2668 if(ls->InheritsFrom(&TA_FourDValLayerSpec)) {
2669 if(unit_groups)
2670 fourd_vals.SetGeom(5, 2, FOURD_N, ls->fourd.n_vals, gp_geom.x, gp_geom.y);
2671 else
2672 fourd_vals.SetGeom(5, 2, FOURD_N, ls->fourd.n_vals, 1, 1);
2673 }
2674}
2675
2676void FourDValLeabraLayer::ApplyInputData_2d(taMatrix* data, Unit::ExtType ext_flags,
2677 Random* ran, const TwoDCoord& offs, bool na_by_range) {
2678 // only no unit_group supported!
2679 if(TestError(unit_groups, "ApplyInputData_2d",
2680 "input data must be 4d for layers with unit_groups: outer 2 are group dims, inner 2 are x,y vals and n_vals")) {
2681 return;
2682 }
2683 for(int d_y = 0; d_y < data->dim(1); d_y++) {
2684 int val_idx = offs.y + d_y;
2685 for(int d_x = 0; d_x < data->dim(0); d_x++) {
2686 int xy_idx = offs.x + d_x;
2687 Variant val = data->SafeElAsVar(d_x, d_y);
2688 if(ext_flags & Unit::EXT)
2689 fourd_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, FOURD_EXT, val_idx, 0, 0);
2690 else
2691 fourd_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, FOURD_TARG, val_idx, 0, 0);
2692 }
2693 }
2694}
2695
2696void FourDValLeabraLayer::ApplyInputData_Flat4d(taMatrix* data, Unit::ExtType ext_flags,
2697 Random* ran, const TwoDCoord& offs, bool na_by_range) {
2698 // outer-loop is data-group (groups of x-y data items)
2699 if(TestError(!unit_groups, "ApplyInputData_Flat4d",
2700 "input data must be 2d for layers without unit_groups: x,y vals and n_vals")) {
2701 return;
2702 }
2703 for(int dg_y = 0; dg_y < data->dim(3); dg_y++) {
2704 for(int dg_x = 0; dg_x < data->dim(2); dg_x++) {
2705
2706 for(int d_y = 0; d_y < data->dim(1); d_y++) {
2707 int u_y = offs.y + dg_y * data->dim(1) + d_y; // multiply out data indicies
2708 for(int d_x = 0; d_x < data->dim(0); d_x++) {
2709 int u_x = offs.x + dg_x * data->dim(0) + d_x; // multiply out data indicies
2710 Unit* un = UnitAtCoord(u_x, u_y);
2711 if(un) {
2712 float val = data->SafeElAsVar(d_x, d_y, dg_x, dg_y).toFloat();
2713 un->ApplyInputData(val, ext_flags, ran, na_by_range);
2714 }
2715 }
2716 }
2717 }
2718 }
2719}
2720
2721void FourDValLeabraLayer::ApplyInputData_Gp4d(taMatrix* data, Unit::ExtType ext_flags, Random* ran,
2722 bool na_by_range) {
2723 // outer-loop is data-group (groups of x-y data items)
2724 for(int dg_y = 0; dg_y < data->dim(3); dg_y++) {
2725 for(int dg_x = 0; dg_x < data->dim(2); dg_x++) {
2726
2727 for(int d_y = 0; d_y < data->dim(1); d_y++) {
2728 int val_idx = d_y;
2729 for(int d_x = 0; d_x < data->dim(0); d_x++) {
2730 int xy_idx = d_x;
2731 Variant val = data->SafeElAsVar(d_x, d_y, dg_x, dg_y);
2732 if(ext_flags & Unit::EXT)
2733 fourd_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, FOURD_EXT, val_idx, dg_x, dg_y);
2734 else
2735 fourd_vals.SetFmVar(val, xy_idx, FOURD_TARG, val_idx, dg_x, dg_y);
2736 }
2737 }
2738 }
2739 }
2740}

2742///////////////////////////////////////////////////////
2743// FourDValLayerSpec
2744
2745void FourDValSpec::Initialize() {
2746 rep = GAUSSIAN;
2747 n_vals = 1;
2748 un_width = .3f;
2749 norm_width = false;
2750 clamp_pat = false;
2751 min_sum_act = 0.2f;
2752 mn_dst = 0.5f;
2753 clip_val = true;
2754
2755 x_min = x_val = y_min = y_val = 0.0f;
2756 x_range = x_incr = y_range = y_incr = 1.0f;
2757 x_size = y_size = 1;
2758 un_width_x = un_width_y = un_width;
2759}
2760
2761void FourDValSpec::InitRange(float xmin, float xrng, float ymin, float yrng) {
2762 x_min = xmin; x_range = xrng; y_min = ymin; y_range = yrng;
2763 un_width_x = un_width;
2764 un_width_y = un_width;
2765 if(norm_width) {
2766 un_width_x *= x_range;
2767 un_width_y *= y_range;
2768 }
2769}
2770
2771void FourDValSpec::InitVal(float xval, float yval, int xsize, int ysize, float xmin, float xrng, float ymin, float yrng) {
2772 InitRange(xmin, xrng, ymin, yrng);
2773 x_val = xval; y_val = yval;
2774 x_size = xsize; y_size = ysize;
2775 x_incr = x_range / (float)(x_size - 1); // DON'T skip 1st row, and count end..
2776 y_incr = y_range / (float)(y_size - 1); // DON'T skip 1st row, and count end..
2777 // incr -= .000001f; // round-off tolerance..
2778}
2779
2780float FourDValSpec::GetUnitAct(int unit_idx) {
2781 int x_idx = unit_idx % x_size;
2782 int y_idx = (unit_idx / x_size);
2783 if(rep == GAUSSIAN) {
2784 float x_cur = x_min + x_incr * (float)x_idx;
2785 float x_dist = (x_cur - x_val) / un_width_x;
2786 float y_cur = y_min + y_incr * (float)y_idx;
2787 float y_dist = (y_cur - y_val) / un_width_y;
2788 float dist = x_dist * x_dist + y_dist * y_dist;
2789 return expf(-dist);
2790 }
2791 else if(rep == LOCALIST) {
2792 float x_cur = x_min + x_incr * (float)x_idx;
2793 float y_cur = y_min + y_incr * (float)y_idx;
2794 float x_dist = fabs(x_val - x_cur);
2795 float y_dist = fabs(y_val - y_cur);
2796 if((x_dist > x_incr) && (y_dist > y_incr)) return 0.0f;
2797
2798 return 1.0f - .5 * ((x_dist / x_incr) + (y_dist / y_incr)); // todo: no idea if this is right.
2799 }
2800 return 0.0f;
2801}
2802
2803void FourDValSpec::GetUnitVal(int unit_idx, float& x_cur, float& y_cur) {
2804 int x_idx = unit_idx % x_size;
2805 int y_idx = (unit_idx / x_size);
2806 x_cur = x_min + x_incr * (float)x_idx;
2807 y_cur = y_min + y_incr * (float)y_idx;
2808}
2809
2810void FourDValBias::Initialize() {
2811 un = NO_UN;
2812 un_gain = 1.0f;
2813 wt = NO_WT;
2814 wt_gain = 1.0f;
2815 x_val = 0.0f;
2816 y_val = 0.0f;
2817}

2819void FourDValLayerSpec::Initialize() {
2820 min_obj_type = &TA_FourDValLeabraLayer;
2821
2822 SetUnique("kwta", true);
2823 kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
2824 kwta.k = 9;
2825 gp_kwta.k_from = KWTASpec::USE_K;
2826 gp_kwta.k = 9;
2827 SetUnique("inhib_group", true);
2828 inhib_group = ENTIRE_LAYER;
2829 SetUnique("inhib", true);
2830 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
2831 inhib.kwta_pt = .6f;
2832
2833 if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
2834 x_range.min = -0.5f; x_range.max = 1.5f; x_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
2835 y_range.min = -0.5f; y_range.max = 1.5f; y_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
2836 fourd.InitRange(x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
2837 x_val_range.min = x_range.min + (.5f * fourd.un_width_x);
2838 x_val_range.max = x_range.max - (.5f * fourd.un_width_x);
2839 y_val_range.min = y_range.min + (.5f * fourd.un_width_y);
2840 y_val_range.max = y_range.max - (.5f * fourd.un_width_y);
2841 }
2842 else if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
2843 x_range.min = 0.0f; x_range.max = 1.0f; x_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
2844 y_range.min = 0.0f; y_range.max = 1.0f; y_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
2845 x_val_range.min = x_range.min; x_val_range.max = x_range.max;
2846 y_val_range.min = y_range.min; y_val_range.max = y_range.max;
2847 }
2848 x_val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui(); y_val_range.UpdateAfterEdit_NoGui();
2849}

2868
2869void FourDValLayerSpec::HelpConfig() {
2870 String help = "FourDValLayerSpec Computation:\n\
2871 Uses distributed coarse-coding units to represent two-dimensional values. Each unit\
2872 has a preferred value arranged evenly between the min-max range, and decoding\
2873 simply computes an activation-weighted average based on these preferred values. The\
2874 current fourd value is encoded in the fourd_vals member of the FourDValLeabraLayer (x1,y1, x2,y2, etc),\
2875 which are set by input data, and updated to reflect current values encoded over layer.\
2876 For no unit groups case, input data should be 2d with inner dim of size 2 (x,y) and outer dim\
2877 of n_vals size. For unit_groups, data should be 4d with two extra outer dims of gp_x, gp_y.\
2878 Provide the actual fourd values in input data and it will automatically establish the \
2879 appropriate distributed representation in the rest of the units.\n\
2880 \nFourDValLayerSpec Configuration:\n\
2881 - The bias_val settings allow you to specify a default initial and ongoing bias value\
2882 through a constant excitatory current (GC) or bias weights (BWT) to the unit, and initial\
2883 weight values. These establish a distributed representation that represents the given .val\n\
2884 - A self connection using the FourDValSelfPrjnSpec can be made, which provides a bias\
2885 for neighboring units to have similar values. It should usually have a fairly small wt_scale.rel\
2886 parameter (e.g., .1)";
2887 taMisc::Confirm(help);
2888}
2889
2890bool FourDValLayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
2891 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
2892 bool rval = inherited::CheckConfig_Layer(lay, quiet);
2893
2894 if(lay->CheckError(lay->un_geom.n < 3, quiet, rval,
2895 "coarse-coded fourd representation requires at least 3 units, I just set un_geom.n")) {
2896 if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
2897 lay->un_geom.n = 9;
2898 lay->un_geom.x = 3;
2899 lay->un_geom.y = 3;
2900 }
2901 else if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
2902 lay->un_geom.n = 121;
2903 lay->un_geom.x = 11;
2904 lay->un_geom.y = 11;
2905 }
2906 }
2907
2908 if(lay->InheritsFrom(&TA_FourDValLeabraLayer)) { // inh will be flagged above
2909 ((FourDValLeabraLayer*)lay)->UpdateFourDValsGeom();
2910 }
2911
2912 if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
2913 kwta.k = 1; // localist means 1 unit active!!
2914 gp_kwta.k = 1;
2915 }
2916
2917 if(bias_val.un == FourDValBias::GC) {
2918 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
2919 if(lay->CheckError(us->hyst.init, quiet, rval,
2920 "bias_val.un = GCH requires UnitSpec hyst.init = false, I just set it for you in spec:", us->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
2921 us->SetUnique("hyst", true);
2922 us->hyst.init = false;
2923 }
2924 if(lay->CheckError(us->acc.init, quiet, rval,
2925 "bias_val.un = GC requires UnitSpec acc.init = false, I just set it for you in spec:", us->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
2926 us->SetUnique("acc", true);
2927 us->acc.init = false;
2928 }
2929 }
2930
2931 // check for conspecs with correct params
2932 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
2933 if(lay->CheckError(u == NULL, quiet, rval,
2934 "fourd val layer doesn't have any units:", lay->name)) {
2935 return false; // fatal
2936 }
2937
2938 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
2939 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
2940 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL)) continue;
2941 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
2942 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec)) {
2943 if(lay->CheckError(cs->wt_scale.rel > 0.5f, quiet, rval,
2944 "fourd val self connections should have wt_scale < .5, I just set it to .1 for you (make sure this is appropriate for all connections that use this spec!)")) {
2945 cs->SetUnique("wt_scale", true);
2946 cs->wt_scale.rel = 0.1f;
2947 }
2948 if(lay->CheckError(cs->lrate > 0.0f, quiet, rval,
2949 "fourd val self connections should have lrate = 0, I just set it for you in spec:", cs->name, "(make sure this is appropriate for all layers that use this spec!)")) {
2950 cs->SetUnique("lrate", true);
2951 cs->lrate = 0.0f;
2952 }
2953 }
2954 else if(cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
2955 continue;
2956 }
2957 }
2958 return rval;
2959}
2960
2961void FourDValLayerSpec::ReConfig(Network* net, int n_units) {
2962 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, net->layers) {
2963 if(lay->spec.SPtr() != this) continue;
2964
2965 if(n_units > 0) {
2966 lay->SetNUnits(n_units);
2967 }
2968
2969 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)lay->unit_spec.SPtr();
2970 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->units.Leaf(0); // taking 1st unit as representative
2971
2972 if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::LOCALIST) {
2973 fourd.min_sum_act = .2f;
2974 kwta.k = 1;
2975 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_AVG_INHIB;
2976 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.9f;
2977 us->g_bar.h = .03f; us->g_bar.a = .09f;
2978 us->act_fun = LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_LINEAR;
2979 us->act.thr = .17f;
2980 us->act.gain = 220.0f;
2981 us->act.nvar = .01f;
2982 us->dt.vm = .05f;
2983 bias_val.un = FourDValBias::GC; bias_val.wt = FourDValBias::NO_WT;
2984 x_range.min = 0.0f; x_range.max = 1.0f;
2985 y_range.min = 0.0f; y_range.max = 1.0f;
2986
2987 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
2988 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
2989 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL)) continue;
2990 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
2991 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
2992 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
2993 continue;
2994 }
2995 cs->lmix.err_sb = false; // false: this is critical for linear mapping of vals..
2996 cs->rnd.mean = 0.1f;
2997 cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
2998 cs->wt_sig.gain = 1.0; cs->wt_sig.off = 1.0;
2999 }
3000 }
3001 else if(fourd.rep == FourDValSpec::GAUSSIAN) {
3002 inhib.type = LeabraInhibSpec::KWTA_INHIB;
3003 inhib.kwta_pt = 0.25f;
3004 us->g_bar.h = .015f; us->g_bar.a = .045f;
3005 us->act_fun = LeabraUnitSpec::NOISY_XX1;
3006 us->act.thr = .25f;
3007 us->act.gain = 600.0f;
3008 us->act.nvar = .005f;
3009 us->dt.vm = .2f;
3010 bias_val.un = FourDValBias::GC; bias_val.wt = FourDValBias::NO_WT;
3011 x_range.min = -.5f; x_range.max = 1.5f;
3012 y_range.min = -.5f; y_range.max = 1.5f;
3013
3014 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
3015 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
3016 if((recv_gp->prjn == NULL) || (recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr() == NULL)) continue;
3017 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
3018 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
3019 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) {
3020 continue;
3021 }
3022 cs->lmix.err_sb = true;
3023 cs->rnd.mean = 0.1f;
3024 cs->rnd.var = 0.0f;
3025 cs->wt_sig.gain = 1.0; cs->wt_sig.off = 1.0;
3026 }
3027 }
3028 us->UpdateAfterEdit();
3029 }
3030 UpdateAfterEdit();
3031}

3033// todo: deal with lesion flag in lots of special purpose code like this!!!
3034
3035void FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_WtBias_Val(Unit_Group* ugp, float x_val, float y_val) {
3036 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
3037 Layer* lay = ugp->own_lay;
3038 fourd.InitVal(x_val, y_val, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
3039 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3040 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(i);
3041 float act = .03f * bias_val.wt_gain * fourd.GetUnitAct(i);
3042 for(int g=0; g<u->recv.size; g++) {
3043 LeabraRecvCons* recv_gp = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(g);
3044 LeabraConSpec* cs = (LeabraConSpec*)recv_gp->GetConSpec();
3045 if(recv_gp->prjn->spec.SPtr()->InheritsFrom(TA_ScalarValSelfPrjnSpec) ||
3046 cs->InheritsFrom(TA_MarkerConSpec)) continue;
3047 for(int ci=0;ci<recv_gp->size;ci++) {
3048 LeabraCon* cn = (LeabraCon*)recv_gp->Cn(ci);
3049 cn->wt += act;
3050 if(cn->wt < cs->wt_limits.min) cn->wt = cs->wt_limits.min;
3051 if(cn->wt > cs->wt_limits.max) cn->wt = cs->wt_limits.max;
3052 }
3053 recv_gp->Init_Weights_post(u);
3054 }
3055 }
3056}
3057
3058void FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_UnBias_Val(Unit_Group* ugp, float x_val, float y_val) {
3059 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
3060 Layer* lay = ugp->own_lay;
3061 fourd.InitVal(x_val, y_val, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
3062 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3063 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(i);
3064 float act = bias_val.un_gain * fourd.GetUnitAct(i);
3065 if(bias_val.un == FourDValBias::GC)
3066 u->vcb.g_h = act;
3067 else if(bias_val.un == FourDValBias::BWT)
3068 u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt = act;
3069 }
3070}
3071
3072void FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_BiasVal(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3073 if(bias_val.un != FourDValBias::NO_UN) {
3074 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Compute_UnBias_Val(ugp, bias_val.x_val, bias_val.y_val););
3075 }
3076 if(bias_val.wt == FourDValBias::WT) {
3077 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, Compute_WtBias_Val(ugp, bias_val.x_val, bias_val.y_val););
3078 }
3079}
3080
3081void FourDValLayerSpec::Init_Weights(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3082 inherited::Init_Weights(lay, net);
3083 Compute_BiasVal(lay, net);
3084}
3085
3086void FourDValLayerSpec::ClampValue_ugp(Unit_Group* ugp, LeabraNetwork*, float rescale) {
3087 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
3088 FourDValLeabraLayer* lay = (FourDValLeabraLayer*)ugp->own_lay;
3089 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = ugp->GpLogPos();
3090 // first initialize to zero
3091 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)ugp->FastEl(0)->GetUnitSpec();
3092 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3093 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(i);
3094 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
3095 u->ext = 0.0;
3096 }
3097 for(int k=0;k<fourd.n_vals;k++) {
3098 float x_val = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_EXT,
3099 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3100 float y_val = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_EXT,
3101 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3102 if(fourd.clip_val) {
3103 x_val = x_val_range.Clip(x_val);
3104 y_val = y_val_range.Clip(y_val);
3105 }
3106 fourd.InitVal(x_val, y_val, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
3107 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3108 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(i);
3109 float act = rescale * fourd.GetUnitAct(i);
3110 if(act < us->opt_thresh.send)
3111 act = 0.0f;
3112 u->ext += act;
3113 }
3114 }
3115}
3116
3117void FourDValLayerSpec::ReadValue(FourDValLeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3118 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, ReadValue_ugp(lay, ugp, net); );
3119}
3120
3121void FourDValLayerSpec::ReadValue_ugp(FourDValLeabraLayer* lay, Unit_Group* ugp, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3122 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
3123 fourd.InitVal(0.0f, 0.0f, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
3124 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = ugp->GpLogPos();
3125 if(fourd.n_vals == 1) { // special case
3126 float x_avg = 0.0f; float y_avg = 0.0f;
3127 float sum_act = 0.0f;
3128 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3129 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(i);
3130 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
3131 float x_cur, y_cur; fourd.GetUnitVal(i, x_cur, y_cur);
3132 float act_val = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->act_eq) / us->clamp_range.max; // clipped & normalized!
3133 x_avg += x_cur * act_val;
3134 y_avg += y_cur * act_val;
3135 sum_act += act_val;
3136 }
3137 sum_act = MAX(sum_act, fourd.min_sum_act);
3138 if(sum_act > 0.0f) {
3139 x_avg /= sum_act; y_avg /= sum_act;
3140 }
3141 // encode the value
3142 lay->SetFourDVal(x_avg, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT,
3143 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3144 lay->SetFourDVal(y_avg, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT,
3145 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3146 }
3147 else { // multiple items
3148 // first find the max values, using sum of -1..+1 region
3149 static ValIdx_Array sort_ary;
3150 sort_ary.Reset();
3151 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3152 float sum = 0.0f;
3153 float nsum = 0.0f;
3154 for(int x=-1;x<=1;x++) {
3155 for(int y=-1;y<=1;y++) {
3156 int idx = i + y * lay->un_geom.x + x;
3157 if(idx < 0 || idx >= nunits) continue;
3158 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(idx);
3159 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec();
3160 float act_val = us->clamp_range.Clip(u->act_eq) / us->clamp_range.max; // clipped & normalized!
3161 nsum += 1.0f;
3162 sum += act_val;
3163 }
3164 }
3165 if(nsum > 0.0f) sum /= nsum;
3166 ValIdx vi(sum, i);
3167 sort_ary.Add(vi);
3168 }
3169 sort_ary.Sort();
3170 float mn_x = fourd.mn_dst * fourd.un_width_x * x_range.Range();
3171 float mn_y = fourd.mn_dst * fourd.un_width_y * y_range.Range();
3172 float mn_dist = mn_x * mn_x + mn_y * mn_y;
3173 int outi = 0; int j = 0;
3174 while((outi < fourd.n_vals) && (j < sort_ary.size)) {
3175 ValIdx& vi = sort_ary[sort_ary.size - j - 1]; // going backward through sort_ary
3176 float x_cur, y_cur; fourd.GetUnitVal(vi.idx, x_cur, y_cur);
3177 // check distance from all previous!
3178 float my_mn = x_range.Range() + y_range.Range();
3179 for(int k=0; k<j; k++) {
3180 ValIdx& vo = sort_ary[sort_ary.size - k - 1];
3181 if(vo.val == -1.0f) continue; // guy we skipped over before
3182 float x_prv, y_prv; fourd.GetUnitVal(vo.idx, x_prv, y_prv);
3183 float x_d = x_cur - x_prv; float y_d = y_cur - y_prv;
3184 float dist = x_d * x_d + y_d * y_d;
3185 my_mn = MIN(dist, my_mn);
3186 }
3187 if(my_mn < mn_dist) { vi.val = -1.0f; j++; continue; } // mark with -1 so we know we skipped it
3188
3189 // encode the value
3190 lay->SetFourDVal(x_cur, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT,
3191 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3192 lay->SetFourDVal(y_cur, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT,
3193 0, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3194 j++; outi++;
3195 }
3196 }
3197}
3198
3199void FourDValLayerSpec::LabelUnits_ugp(Unit_Group* ugp) {
3200 if(nunits < 3) return; // must be at least a few units..
3201 Layer* lay = ugp->own_lay;
3202 fourd.InitVal(0.0f, 0.0f, lay->un_geom.x, lay->un_geom.y, x_range.min, x_range.range, y_range.min, y_range.range);
3203 for(int i=0;i<nunits;i++) {
3204 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)ugp->FastEl(i);
3205 float x_cur, y_cur; fourd.GetUnitVal(i, x_cur, y_cur);
3206 u->name = (String)x_cur + "," + String(y_cur);
3207 }

3210void FourDValLayerSpec::LabelUnits(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3211 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, LabelUnits_ugp(ugp); );
3212}
3213
3214void FourDValLayerSpec::LabelUnitsNet(LeabraNetwork* net) {
3215 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, l, net->layers) {
3216 if(l->spec.SPtr() == this)
3217 LabelUnits(l, net);
3218 }
3219}

3225void FourDValLayerSpec::Settle_Init_TargFlags_Layer(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3226 inherited::Settle_Init_TargFlags_Layer(lay, net);
3227 // need to actually copy over targ to ext vals!
3228 FourDValLeabraLayer* tdlay = (FourDValLeabraLayer*)lay;
3229 if(lay->ext_flag & Unit::TARG) { // only process target layers..
3230 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::PLUS_PHASE) {
3231 UNIT_GP_ITR(tdlay,
3232 for(int k=0;k<fourd.n_vals;k++) {
3233 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = ugp->GpLogPos();
3234 float x_val = tdlay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X,
3235 FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_TARG,
3236 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3237 float y_val = tdlay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y,
3238 FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_TARG,
3239 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3240 tdlay->SetFourDVal(x_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X,
3241 FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_EXT,
3242 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3243 tdlay->SetFourDVal(y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y,
3244 FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_EXT,
3245 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3246 }
3247 );
3248 }
3249 }

3253void FourDValLayerSpec::Settle_Init_Layer(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3254 inherited::Settle_Init_Layer(lay, net);
3255
3256 FourDValLeabraLayer* tdlay = (FourDValLeabraLayer*)lay;
3257 tdlay->UpdateFourDValsGeom(); // quick, make sure no mismatch
3258
3259 if(bias_val.un == ScalarValBias::BWT) {
3260 // if using bias-weight bias, keep a constant scaling (independent of layer size)
3261 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units) {
3262 LeabraConSpec* bspec = (LeabraConSpec*)u->GetUnitSpec()->bias_spec.SPtr();
3263 u->bias_scale = bspec->wt_scale.abs; // still have absolute scaling if wanted..
3264 u->bias_scale /= 100.0f; // keep a constant scaling so it doesn't depend on network size!
3265 }
3266 }

3269void FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_HardClamp(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3270 if(fourd.clamp_pat) {
3271 inherited::Compute_HardClamp(lay, net);
3272 return;
3273 }
3274 if(!(lay->ext_flag & Unit::EXT)) {
3275 lay->hard_clamped = false;
3276 return;
3277 }
3278 // allow for soft-clamping: translates pattern into exts first
3279 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay, if(nunits > 2) { ClampValue_ugp(ugp, net); } );
3280 // now check for actual hard clamping
3281 if(!clamp.hard) {
3282 lay->hard_clamped = false;
3283 return;
3284 }
3285 HardClampExt(lay, net);
3286}

3298
3299void FourDValLayerSpec::PostSettle_ugp(FourDValLeabraLayer* lay, Unit_Group* ugp, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3300 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = ugp->GpLogPos();
3301
3302 bool no_plus_testing = false;
3303 if(net->no_plus_test && (net->train_mode == LeabraNetwork::TEST)) {
3304 no_plus_testing = true;
3305 }
3306
3307 for(int k=0;k<fourd.n_vals;k++) {
3308 float x_val, y_val, x_m, y_m, x_p, y_p;
3309 lay->GetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT,
3310 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3311 lay->GetFourDVals(x_m, y_m, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3312 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3313 lay->GetFourDVals(x_p, y_p, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3314 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3315
3316 switch(net->phase_order) {
3317 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS:
3318 if(no_plus_testing) {
3319 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3320 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3321 lay->SetFourDVals(0.0f, 0.0f, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3322 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3323 }
3324 else {
3325 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
3326 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3327 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3328 }
3329 else {
3330 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3331 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3332 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3333 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3334 }
3335 }
3336 break;
3337 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_MINUS:
3338 if(no_plus_testing) {
3339 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3340 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3341 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3342 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3343 lay->SetFourDVals(0.0f, 0.0f, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3344 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3345 }
3346 else {
3347 if(net->phase == LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PHASE) {
3348 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3349 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3350 lay->SetFourDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3351 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3352 }
3353 else {
3354 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3355 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3356 }
3357 }
3358 break;
3359 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_ONLY:
3360 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3361 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3362 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3363 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3364 lay->SetFourDVals(0.0f, 0.0f, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3365 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3366 break;
3367 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
3368 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_MINUS:
3369 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
3370 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
3371 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3372 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3373 }
3374 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
3375 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3376 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3377 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3378 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3379 if(no_plus_testing) {
3380 // update act_m because it is actually another test case!
3381 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3382 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3383 }
3384 }
3385 else {
3386 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M2,
3387 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3388 lay->SetFourDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3389 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3390 }
3391 break;
3392 case LeabraNetwork::PLUS_NOTHING:
3393 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
3394 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
3395 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3396 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3397 }
3398 else {
3399 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3400 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3401 lay->SetFourDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3402 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3403 }
3404 break;
3405 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS:
3406 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
3407 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
3408 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3409 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3410 }
3411 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
3412 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3413 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3414 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3415 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3416 }
3417 else {
3418 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P2,
3419 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3420 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val - x_p, y_val - y_p, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF2,
3421 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3422 }
3423 break;
3424 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_NOTHING:
3425 case LeabraNetwork::MINUS_PLUS_PLUS_MINUS:
3426 // don't use actual phase values because pluses might be minuses with testing
3427 if(net->phase_no == 0) {
3428 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3429 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3430 }
3431 else if(net->phase_no == 1) {
3432 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P,
3433 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3434 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val - x_m, y_val - y_m, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF,
3435 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3436 }
3437 else if(net->phase_no == 2) {
3438 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_P2,
3439 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3440 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val - x_p, y_val - y_p, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF2,
3441 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3442 }
3443 else {
3444 lay->SetFourDVals(x_val, y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M2,
3445 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3446 lay->SetFourDVals(x_p - x_val, y_p - y_val, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_DIF2,
3447 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3448 }
3449 break;
3450 }
3451 }

3453
3454float FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_SSE_ugp(Unit_Group* ugp, LeabraLayer* ly, int& n_vals) {
3455 FourDValLeabraLayer* lay = (FourDValLeabraLayer*)ly;
3456 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = ugp->GpLogPos();
3457 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)ugp->FastEl(0)->GetUnitSpec();
3458 float rval = 0.0f;
3459 for(int k=0;k<fourd.n_vals;k++) { // first loop over and find potential target values
3460 float x_targ = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_TARG, k,
3461 gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3462 float y_targ = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_TARG, k,
3463 gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3464 // only count if target value is within range -- otherwise considered a non-target
3465 if(x_val_range.RangeTestEq(x_targ) && y_val_range.RangeTestEq(y_targ)) {
3466 n_vals++;
3467 // now find minimum dist actual activations
3468 float mn_dist = taMath::flt_max;
3469 for(int j=0;j<fourd.n_vals;j++) {
3470 float x_act_m = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3471 j, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3472 float y_act_m = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3473 j, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3474 float dx = x_targ - x_act_m;
3475 float dy = y_targ - y_act_m;
3476 if(fabsf(dx) < us->sse_tol) dx = 0.0f;
3477 if(fabsf(dy) < us->sse_tol) dy = 0.0f;
3478 float dist = dx * dx + dy * dy;
3479 if(dist < mn_dist) {
3480 mn_dist = dist;
3481 lay->SetFourDVal(dx, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ERR,
3482 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3483 lay->SetFourDVal(dy, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ERR,
3484 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3485 lay->SetFourDVal(dx*dx, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_SQERR,
3486 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3487 lay->SetFourDVal(dy*dy, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_SQERR,
3488 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3489 }
3490 }
3491 rval += mn_dist;
3492 }
3493 }
3494 return rval;
3495}
3496
3497float FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_SSE(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork*,
3498 int& n_vals, bool unit_avg, bool sqrt) {
3499 n_vals = 0;
3500 if(!(lay->ext_flag & (Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP))) return 0.0f;
3501 lay->sse = 0.0f;
3502 UNIT_GP_ITR(lay,
3503 lay->sse += Compute_SSE_ugp(ugp, lay, n_vals);
3504 );
3505 float rval = lay->sse;
3506 if(unit_avg && n_vals > 0)
3507 lay->sse /= (float)n_vals;
3508 if(sqrt)
3509 lay->sse = sqrtf(lay->sse);
3510 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
3511 ((lay->ext_flag & Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE))) {
3512 rval = 0.0f;
3513 n_vals = 0;
3514 }
3515 return rval;
3516}
3517
3518float FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr_ugp(LeabraLayer* ly, Unit_Group* ugp,
3519 LeabraInhib* thr, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3520 FourDValLeabraLayer* lay = (FourDValLeabraLayer*)ly;
3521 TwoDCoord gp_geom_pos = ugp->GpLogPos();
3522 LeabraUnitSpec* us = (LeabraUnitSpec*)ugp->FastEl(0)->GetUnitSpec();
3523 float rval = 0.0f;
3524 for(int k=0;k<fourd.n_vals;k++) { // first loop over and find potential target values
3525 float x_targ = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_TARG,
3526 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3527 float y_targ = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_TARG,
3528 k, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3529 // only count if target value is within range -- otherwise considered a non-target
3530 if(x_val_range.RangeTestEq(x_targ) && y_val_range.RangeTestEq(y_targ)) {
3531 // now find minimum dist actual activations
3532 float mn_dist = taMath::flt_max;
3533 for(int j=0;j<fourd.n_vals;j++) {
3534 float x_act_m = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_X, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3535 j, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3536 float y_act_m = lay->GetFourDVal(FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_Y, FourDValLeabraLayer::FOURD_ACT_M,
3537 j, gp_geom_pos.x, gp_geom_pos.y);
3538 float dx = x_targ - x_act_m;
3539 float dy = y_targ - y_act_m;
3540 if(fabsf(dx) < us->sse_tol) dx = 0.0f;
3541 if(fabsf(dy) < us->sse_tol) dy = 0.0f;
3542 float dist = fabsf(dx) + fabsf(dy); // only diff from sse!
3543 if(dist < mn_dist)
3544 mn_dist = dist;
3545 }
3546 rval += mn_dist;
3547 }
3548 }
3549 return rval;
3550}
3551
3552float FourDValLayerSpec::Compute_NormErr(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
3553 lay->norm_err = -1.0f; // assume not contributing
3554 if(!(lay->ext_flag & (Unit::TARG | Unit::COMP))) return -1.0f; // indicates not applicable
3555
3556 float nerr = 0.0f;
3557 float ntot = 0;
3558 if((inhib_group != ENTIRE_LAYER) && (lay->unit_groups)) {
3559 for(int g=0; g<lay->units.gp.size; g++) {
3560 LeabraUnit_Group* rugp = (LeabraUnit_Group*)lay->units.gp[g];
3561 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, rugp, (LeabraInhib*)rugp, net);
3562 ntot += x_range.range + y_range.range;
3563 }
3564 }
3565 else {
3566 nerr += Compute_NormErr_ugp(lay, &(lay->units), (LeabraInhib*)lay, net);
3567 ntot += x_range.range + y_range.range;
3568 }
3569 if(ntot == 0.0f) return -1.0f;
3570
3571 lay->norm_err = nerr / ntot;
3572 if(lay->norm_err > 1.0f) lay->norm_err = 1.0f;
3573
3574 if(lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_SSE) ||
3575 ((lay->ext_flag & Unit::COMP) && lay->HasLayerFlag(Layer::NO_ADD_COMP_SSE)))
3576 return -1.0f; // no contributarse
3577
3578 return lay->norm_err;
3579}
3580
3581*/

3796
3797void LeabraExtOnlyUnitSpec::Initialize() {
3798
3799}
3800
3801void LeabraExtOnlyUnitSpec::Compute_NetinInteg(LeabraUnit* u, LeabraNetwork* net, int thread_no) {
3802 LeabraLayer* lay = u->own_lay();
3803 if(lay->hard_clamped) return;
3804
3805 if(net->inhib_cons_used) {
3806 u->g_i_raw += u->g_i_delta;
3807 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
3808 u->gc.i = MAX(u->g_i_raw, 0.0f)(((u->g_i_raw) > (0.0f)) ? (u->g_i_raw) : (0.0f));
3809 Compute_NetinInteg_Spike_i(u, net);
3810 }
3811 else {
3812 u->gc.i = u->prv_g_i + dt.net * (u->g_i_raw - u->prv_g_i);
3813 u->prv_g_i = u->gc.i;
3814 }
3815 }
3816
3817 u->net_raw += u->net_delta;
3818 float tot_net = (u->bias_scale * u->bias.OwnCn(0)->wt) + u->net_raw;
3819
3820 if(u->HasExtFlag(Unit::EXT)) {
3821 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->GetLayerSpec();
3822 float extin = u->ext * ls->clamp.gain;
3823 if(extin < opt_thresh.send)
3824 tot_net = 0.0f; // not allowed to activate
3825 else
3826 tot_net += extin;
3827 }
3828 else {
3829 // get first projection, first connection
3830 LeabraRecvCons* cg = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.SafeEl(0);
3831 if(TestError(!cg, "Compute_NetinInteg", "requires one recv projection!")) {
3832 return;
3833 }
3834 LeabraUnit* su = (LeabraUnit*)cg->Un(0);
3835 if(TestError(!su, "Compute_NetinInteg", "requires one unit in recv projection!")) {
3836 return;
3837 }
3838 float extin = su->act_eq;
3839 if(extin < opt_thresh.send)
3840 tot_net = 0.0f; // veto
3841 }
3842
3843 u->net_delta = 0.0f; // clear for next use
3844 u->g_i_delta = 0.0f; // clear for next use
3845
3846 if(act_fun == SPIKE) {
3847 // todo: need a mech for inhib spiking
3848 u->net = MAX(tot_net, 0.0f)(((tot_net) > (0.0f)) ? (tot_net) : (0.0f)); // store directly for integration
3849 Compute_NetinInteg_Spike_e(u,net);
3850 }
3851 else {
3852 float dnet = dt.net * (tot_net - u->prv_net);
3853 u->net = u->prv_net + dnet;
3854 u->prv_net = u->net;
3855 u->net = MAX(u->net, 0.0f)(((u->net) > (0.0f)) ? (u->net) : (0.0f)); // negative netin doesn't make any sense
3856 }
3857
3858 // add just before computing i_thr -- after all the other stuff is done..
3859 if((noise_type == NETIN_NOISE) && (noise.type != Random::NONE) && (net->cycle >= 0)) {
3860 u->net += Compute_Noise(u, net);
3861 }
3862 u->i_thr = Compute_IThresh(u, net);
3863}

3868
3869void SaliencyPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
3870 // init_wts = true;
3871 convergence = 1;
3872 reciprocal = false;
3873 feat_only = true;
3874 feat_gps = 2;
3875 dog_wts.filter_width = 3;
3876 dog_wts.filter_size = 7;
3877 dog_wts.on_sigma = 1;
3878 dog_wts.off_sigma = 2;
3879 wt_mult = 1.0f;
3880 surr_mult = 1.0f;
3881 units_per_feat_gp = 4;
3882}
3883
3884void SaliencyPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
3885 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
3886 if(prjn->layer->units.leaves == 0) // an empty layer!
3887 return;
3888 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
3889 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
3890 return;
3891 }
3892 if(TestWarning(!prjn->from->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
3893 "requires sending layer to have unit groups!")) {
3894 return;
3895 }
3896 if(feat_only)
3897 Connect_feat_only(prjn);
3898 else
3899 Connect_full_dog(prjn);
3900}
3901
3902void SaliencyPrjnSpec::Connect_feat_only(Projection* prjn) {
3903 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
3904 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
3905
3906 if(reciprocal) {
3907 recv_lay = prjn->from;
3908 send_lay = prjn->layer;
3909
3910 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(Unit, su, send_lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (Unit *su = (Unit*)
(send_lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); su; su = (Unit*) (
send_lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
3911 su->RecvConsPreAlloc(1, prjn); // only ever have 1!
3912 }
3913 }
3914
3915 TwoDCoord rug_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
3916 TwoDCoord ruu_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
3917 TwoDCoord su_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
3918
3919 int fltsz = convergence;
3920 int sg_sz_tot = fltsz * fltsz;
3921
3922 int feat_no = 0;
3923 TwoDCoord rug;
3924 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
3925 for(rug.y = 0; rug.y < rug_geo.y; rug.y++) {
3926 for(rug.x = 0; rug.x < rug_geo.x; rug.x++, feat_no++) {
3927 Unit_Group* ru_gp = recv_lay->UnitGpAtCoord(rug);
3928 if(!ru_gp) continue;
3929
3930 int rui = 0;
3931 TwoDCoord ruc;
3932 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < ruu_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
3933 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < ruu_geo.x; ruc.x++, rui++) {
3934
3935 TwoDCoord su_st = ruc*convergence;
3936
3937 Unit* ru_u = (Unit*)ru_gp->SafeEl(rui);
3938 if(!ru_u) break;
3939 if(!reciprocal && !alloc_loop)
3940 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(sg_sz_tot, prjn);
3941
3942 TwoDCoord suc;
3943 for(suc.y = 0; suc.y < fltsz; suc.y++) {
3944 for(suc.x = 0; suc.x < fltsz; suc.x++) {
3945 TwoDCoord sugc = su_st + suc;
3946 Unit_Group* su_gp = send_lay->UnitGpAtCoord(sugc);
3947 if(!su_gp) continue;
3948
3949 Unit* su_u = (Unit*)su_gp->SafeEl(feat_no);
3950 if(su_u) {
3951 if(reciprocal)
3952 su_u->ConnectFrom(ru_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
3953 else
3954 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
3955 }
3956 }
3957 }
3958 }
3959 }
3960 }
3961 }
3962 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
3963 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
3964 }
3965 }
3966}
3967
3968void SaliencyPrjnSpec::Connect_full_dog(Projection* prjn) {
3969 dog_wts.UpdateFilter();
3970 taMath_float::vec_norm_abs_max(&(dog_wts.net_filter)); // renorm to abs max = 1
3971
3972 if(TestError(reciprocal, "Connect_full_dog", "full DoG connection not supported in reciprocal mode!!!")) return;
3973
3974 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
3975 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
3976 TwoDCoord rug_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
3977 TwoDCoord ruu_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
3978 TwoDCoord su_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
3979
3980 int fltwd = dog_wts.filter_width; // no convergence..
3981 int fltsz = dog_wts.filter_size * convergence;
3982
3983 int sg_sz_tot = fltsz * fltsz;
3984 Unit_Group* su_gp0 = (Unit_Group*)send_lay->units.gp[0];
3985 int alloc_no = sg_sz_tot * su_gp0->size;
3986
3987 units_per_feat_gp = su_gp0->size / feat_gps;
3988
3989 int feat_no = 0;
3990 TwoDCoord rug;
3991 for(rug.y = 0; rug.y < rug_geo.y; rug.y++) {
3992 for(rug.x = 0; rug.x < rug_geo.x; rug.x++, feat_no++) {
3993 Unit_Group* ru_gp = recv_lay->UnitGpAtCoord(rug);
3994 if(!ru_gp) continue;
3995
3996 int rui = 0;
3997 TwoDCoord ruc;
3998 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < ruu_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
3999 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < ruu_geo.x; ruc.x++, rui++) {
4000
4001 TwoDCoord su_st = ruc*convergence - convergence*fltwd;
4002
4003 Unit* ru_u = (Unit*)ru_gp->SafeEl(rui);
4004 if(!ru_u) break;
4005 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(alloc_no, prjn);
4006
4007 TwoDCoord suc;
4008 for(suc.y = 0; suc.y < fltsz; suc.y++) {
4009 for(suc.x = 0; suc.x < fltsz; suc.x++) {
4010 TwoDCoord sugc = su_st + suc;
4011 Unit_Group* su_gp = send_lay->UnitGpAtCoord(sugc);
4012 if(!su_gp) continue;
4013
4014 for(int sui=0;sui<su_gp->size;sui++) {
4015 Unit* su_u = (Unit*)su_gp->FastEl(sui);
4016 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
4017 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn);
4018 }
4019 }
4020 }
4021 }
4022 }
4023 }
4024 }
4025}
4026
4027void SaliencyPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
4028 if(feat_only) { // just use regular..
4029 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru);
4030 return;
4031 }
4032 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
4033 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
4034
4035 int fltwd = dog_wts.filter_width; // no convergence.
4036 int fltsz = dog_wts.filter_size * convergence;
4037
4038 Unit_Group* su_gp0 = (Unit_Group*)send_lay->units.gp[0];
4039 units_per_feat_gp = su_gp0->size / feat_gps;
4040
4041 Unit_Group* rugp = (Unit_Group*)ru->GetOwner();
4042
4043 TwoDCoord rug_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
4044 TwoDCoord rgp_pos = rugp->GpLogPos();
4045
4046 int feat_no = rgp_pos.y * rug_geo.x + rgp_pos.x; // unit group index
4047 int my_feat_gp = feat_no / units_per_feat_gp;
4048 int fg_st = my_feat_gp * units_per_feat_gp;
4049 int fg_ed = fg_st + units_per_feat_gp;
4050
4051 TwoDCoord ruu_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
4052 TwoDCoord su_st; // su starting (left)
4053 su_st.x = (ru->idx % ruu_geo.x)*convergence - convergence*fltwd;
4054 su_st.y = (ru->idx / ruu_geo.x)*convergence - convergence*fltwd;
4055
4056 TwoDCoord su_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
4057
4058 int su_idx = 0;
4059 TwoDCoord suc;
4060 for(suc.y = 0; suc.y < fltsz; suc.y++) {
4061 for(suc.x = 0; suc.x < fltsz; suc.x++) {
4062 TwoDCoord sugc = su_st + suc;
4063 Unit_Group* su_gp = send_lay->UnitGpAtCoord(sugc);
4064 if(!su_gp) continue;
4065
4066 float wt = wt_mult * dog_wts.net_filter.FastEl(suc.x/convergence,
4067 suc.y/convergence);
4068
4069 if(wt > 0) {
4070 for(int sui=0;sui<su_gp->size;sui++) {
4071 if(sui == feat_no)
4072 cg->Cn(su_idx++)->wt = wt; // target feature
4073 else
4074 cg->Cn(su_idx++)->wt = 0.0f; // everyone else
4075 }
4076 }
4077 else {
4078 for(int sui=0;sui<su_gp->size;sui++) {
4079 if(sui != feat_no && sui >= fg_st && sui < fg_ed)
4080 cg->Cn(su_idx++)->wt = -surr_mult * wt;
4081 else
4082 cg->Cn(su_idx++)->wt = 0.0f; // not in our group or is guy itself
4083 }
4084 }
4085 }
4086 }
4087}
4088
4089void SaliencyPrjnSpec::GraphFilter(DataTable* graph_data) {
4090 dog_wts.GraphFilter(graph_data);
4091}
4092
4093void SaliencyPrjnSpec::GridFilter(DataTable* graph_data) {
4094 dog_wts.GridFilter(graph_data);
4095}

4100
4101void V1LateralContourPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
4102 radius = 4;
4103 wrap = true;
4104 ang_pow = 4.0f;
4105 dist_sigma = 1.0f;
4106 con_thr = 0.2f;
4107 oth_feat_wt = 0.5f;
4108 init_wts = true;
4109
4110}
4111
4112void V1LateralContourPrjnSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
4113 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
4114}
4115
4116void V1LateralContourPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
4117 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
4118
4119 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
4120 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
4121 return;
4122 }
4123 if(TestWarning(!prjn->from->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
4124 "requires send layer to have unit groups!")) {
4125 return;
4126 }
4127 if(TestWarning(prjn->from != prjn->layer, "Connect_impl",
4128 "requires send and recv to be the same layer -- lateral projection!")) {
4129 return;
4130 }
4131 if(TestWarning(prjn->con_spec->wt_limits.sym, "Connect_impl",
4132 "cannot have wt_limits.sym on in conspec -- turning off in spec:",
4133 prjn->con_spec->name,
4134 "This might affect children of this spec.")) {
4135 prjn->con_spec->SetUnique("wt_limits", true);
4136 prjn->con_spec->wt_limits.sym = false;
4137 prjn->con_spec->UpdateAfterEdit();
4138 }
4139
4140 Layer* lay = prjn->from;
4141 TwoDCoord gp_geo = lay->gp_geom;
4142 TwoDCoord un_geo = lay->un_geom;
4143 float n_angles = (float)un_geo.x;
4144
4145 TwoDCoord ruc;
4146 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
4147 int rgpidx = 0;
4148 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < gp_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
4149 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < gp_geo.x; ruc.x++, rgpidx++) {
4150
4151 TwoDCoord suc;
4152 TwoDCoord suc_wrp;
4153 for(suc.y = ruc.y-radius; suc.y <= ruc.y+radius; suc.y++) {
4154 for(suc.x = ruc.x-radius; suc.x <= ruc.x+radius; suc.x++) {
4155 suc_wrp = suc;
4156 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, gp_geo) && !wrap)
4157 continue;
4158 int sgpidx = lay->UnitGpIdxFmPos(suc_wrp);
4159 if(!lay->UnitGpIdxIsValid(sgpidx)) continue;
4160
4161 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc; // don't use wrap!
4162 float dst = del.Mag();
4163 if(dst > (float)radius) continue; // out of bounds
4164 if(dst == 0.0f) continue; // no selfs
4165
4166 float nrmdst = dst / (float)radius;
4167 float gang = atan2f(del.y, del.x); // group angle
4168 if(gang >= taMath_float::pi) gang -= taMath_float::pi;
4169 if(gang < 0.0f) gang += taMath_float::pi;
4170
4171 float gauswt = taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(nrmdst, dist_sigma);
4172
4173 TwoDCoord run;
4174 for(run.x = 0; run.x < un_geo.x; run.x++) {
4175 float rang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)run.x / n_angles);
4176 float gangwt = powf(fabsf(cosf(gang-rang)), ang_pow);
4177
4178 TwoDCoord sun;
4179 for(sun.x = 0; sun.x < un_geo.x; sun.x++) {
4180 float sang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)sun.x / n_angles);
4181 float sangwt = powf(fabsf(cosf(sang-rang)), ang_pow);
4182 float wt = sangwt * gangwt * gauswt;
4183 if(wt < con_thr) continue;
4184
4185 for(run.y = 0; run.y < un_geo.y; run.y++) {
4186 for(sun.y = 0; sun.y < un_geo.y; sun.y++) {
4187 int rui = run.y * un_geo.x + run.x;
4188 int sui = sun.y * un_geo.x + sun.x;
4189
4190 float feat_wt = 1.0f;
4191 if(run.y != sun.y)
4192 feat_wt = oth_feat_wt;
4193 float eff_wt = wt * feat_wt;
4194 if(eff_wt < con_thr) continue;
4195
4196 Unit* ru_u = lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
4197 if(!ru_u) continue;
4198 Unit* su_u = lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
4199 if(!su_u) continue;
4200 if(alloc_loop) {
4201 ru_u->RecvConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4202 su_u->SendConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4203 }
4204 else {
4205 Connection* cn = ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
4206 cn->wt = eff_wt;
4207 }
4208 }
4209 }
4210 }
4211 }
4212 }
4213 }
4214 }
4215 }
4216 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do allocations
4217 prjn->layer->RecvConsPostAlloc(prjn);
4218 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
4219 }
4220 }
4221}
4222
4223void V1LateralContourPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
4224 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
4225 Layer* lay = prjn->from;
4226 TwoDCoord gp_geo = lay->gp_geom;
4227 TwoDCoord un_geo = lay->un_geom;
4228 float n_angles = (float)un_geo.x;
4229
4230 TwoDCoord gp_geo_half = gp_geo / 2;
4231
4232 int rgpidx;
4233 int rui;
4234 lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
4235 TwoDCoord ruc = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(rgpidx);
4236 TwoDCoord run;
4237 run.SetFmIndex(rui, un_geo.x);
4238 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
4239 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
4240 int sgpidx;
4241 int sui;
4242 lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, sui, sgpidx);
4243 TwoDCoord suc = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(sgpidx);
4244 TwoDCoord sun;
4245 sun.SetFmIndex(sui, un_geo.x);
4246
4247 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc; // don't use wrap!
4248 if(wrap) { // dist may be closer in wrapped case..
4249 suc.WrapMinDist(del, gp_geo, ruc, gp_geo_half);
4250 }
4251
4252 float dst = del.Mag();
4253 float nrmdst = dst / (float)radius;
4254 float gang = atan2f((float)del.y, (float)del.x); // group angle
4255 if(gang >= taMath_float::pi) gang -= taMath_float::pi;
4256 if(gang < 0.0f) gang += taMath_float::pi;
4257 float rang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)run.x / n_angles);
4258 float sang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)sun.x / n_angles);
4259 float sangwt = powf(fabsf(cosf(sang-rang)), ang_pow);
4260 float gangwt = powf(fabsf(cosf(gang-rang)), ang_pow);
4261 float gauswt = taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(nrmdst, dist_sigma);
4262 float feat_wt = 1.0f;
4263 if(run.y != sun.y)
4264 feat_wt = oth_feat_wt;
4265 float wt = feat_wt * sangwt * gangwt * gauswt;
4266 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
4267 }
4268}

4271//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4272// V2BoLateralPrjnSpec
4273
4274void V2BoLateralPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
4275 init_wts = true;
4276
4277 radius = 8;
4278 wrap = true;
4279 t_on = true;
4280 opp_on = true;
4281 ang_sig = 0.5f;
4282 dist_sig_line = 0.8f;
4283 dist_sig_oth = 0.5f;
4284 line_mag = 0.8f;
4285 weak_mag = 0.5f;
4286 con_thr = 0.2f;
4287 test_ang = -1;
4288}
4289
4290void V2BoLateralPrjnSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
4291 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
4292}
4293
4294// static int dbg_hit_cnt = 0;
4295
4296void V2BoLateralPrjnSpec::CreateStencils() {
4297 int n_angles = 4;
4298 int max_cnt = (2 * radius + 1);
4299 v2ffbo_weights.SetGeom(6, max_cnt, max_cnt, 2, n_angles, 2, n_angles);
4300 TwoDCoord suc; // send coords
4301 for(int rang_dx = 0; rang_dx < n_angles; rang_dx++) {
4302 for(int rdir = 0; rdir < 2; rdir++) {
4303 for(int sang_dx = 0; sang_dx < n_angles; sang_dx++) {
4304 for(suc.y = -radius; suc.y <= radius; suc.y++) {
4305 int ysuc_dx = suc.y + radius;
4306 for(suc.x = -radius; suc.x <= radius; suc.x++) {
4307 int xsuc_dx = suc.x + radius;
4308 for(int sdir = 0; sdir < 2; sdir++) { // integrate over sending directions
4309 float wt = ConWt(suc, rang_dx, sang_dx, rdir, sdir);
4310 v2ffbo_weights.FastEl(xsuc_dx, ysuc_dx, sdir, sang_dx, rdir, rang_dx) = wt;
4311 }
4312 }
4313 }
4314 }
4315 }
4316 }
4317}
4318
4319float V2BoLateralPrjnSpec::ConWt(TwoDCoord& suc, int rang_dx, int sang_dx, int rdir, int sdir) {
4320 float n_angles = 4.0f;
4321 // integer angles -- useful for precise conditionals..
4322 int rang_n = rang_dx + rdir * 4;
4323 int sang_n = sang_dx + sdir * 4;
4324 int dang_n;
4325 if(sang_n < rang_n)
4326 dang_n = (8 + sang_n) - rang_n;
4327 else
4328 dang_n = sang_n - rang_n;
4329 int dang_n_pi = dang_n;
4330 if(dang_n >= 4) dang_n_pi = 8 - dang_n;
4331 int abs_dang_n_pi = dang_n_pi < 0 ? -dang_n_pi : dang_n_pi;
4332
4333 if(!opp_on && dang_n == 4) return 0.0f; // no opposite angle cons
4334
4335 if((test_ang >= 0) && (dang_n != test_ang))
4336 return 0.0f; // don't continue
4337
4338 TwoDCoord del = suc;
4339 float dst = del.Mag();
4340 if(dst > (float)radius) return 0.0f;
4341 if(dst == 0.0f) return 0.0f; // no self con
4342 float nrmdst = dst / (float)radius;
4343
4344 float gang = atan2f(del.y, del.x); // group angle -- 0..pi or -pi
4345 if(gang < 0.0f) gang += 2.0f * taMath_float::pi; // keep it positive
4346
4347 // dir 0 = 0..pi, dir 1 = pi..2pi
4348 float rang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)rang_dx / n_angles) + taMath_float::pi * (float)rdir;
4349 float sang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)sang_dx / n_angles) + taMath_float::pi * (float)sdir;
4350
4351 float dang; // delta-angle -- keep this positive too
4352 if(sang < rang)
4353 dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi + sang) - rang;
4354 else
4355 dang = sang - rang;
4356 float dang_pi = dang; // this determines type of projection -- equal fabs(dang_pi) are same type
4357 if(dang >= taMath_float::pi) dang_pi = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi) - dang;
4358 float abs_dang_pi = fabs(dang_pi);
4359
4360 float op_mag = 0.0f;
4361 if(abs_dang_pi < 0.499f * taMath_float::pi)
4362 op_mag = ((0.5f * taMath_float::pi - abs_dang_pi) / (0.5f * taMath_float::pi)); // 1 for 0, .5 for 45
4363
4364 float tang = rang + 0.5f * dang; // target angle
4365
4366 float gtang = gang - tang;
4367 if(gtang > taMath_float::pi) gtang -= 2.0f * taMath_float::pi;
4368 if(gtang < -taMath_float::pi) gtang += 2.0f * taMath_float::pi;
4369
4370 // make symmetric around half sphere
4371 bool op_side = false;
4372 if(gtang > taMath_float::pi * 0.5f) { gtang -= taMath_float::pi; op_side = true; }
4373 if(gtang < -taMath_float::pi * 0.5f){ gtang += taMath_float::pi; op_side = true; }
4374
4375 float eff_mag = 1.0f;
4376 if(abs_dang_pi > 0.501f * taMath_float::pi) eff_mag = weak_mag;
4377
4378 float netwt = eff_mag * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(gtang, ang_sig);
4379 if(abs_dang_n_pi == 0)
4380 netwt *= line_mag * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(nrmdst, dist_sig_line);
4381 else
4382 netwt *= taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(nrmdst, dist_sig_oth);
4383
4384 if(op_side)
4385 netwt *= op_mag;
4386
4387 if(t_on && abs_dang_n_pi == 2 && dst <= 2.9f) {
4388 float grang = gang - rang;
4389// if(dbg_hit_cnt++ <= 100) {
4390// taMisc::Info("rang_n: " + String(rang_n), " sang_n: " + String(sang_n),
4391// " dang_n: " + String(dang_n), " dang_n_pi: " + String(dang_n_pi),
4392// "gang: " + String(gang), " grang:" + String(grang));
4393// }
4394 if(fabsf(grang - (1.5f * taMath_float::pi)) < .1f ||
4395 fabsf(grang - (-0.5f * taMath_float::pi)) < .1f) {
4396 netwt = 1.0f;
4397 }
4398 }
4399
4400 return netwt;
4401}
4402
4403void V2BoLateralPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
4404// dbg_hit_cnt = 0; // debugging
4405
4406 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
4407
4408 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
4409 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
4410 return;
4411 }
4412 if(TestWarning(!prjn->from->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
4413 "requires send layer to have unit groups!")) {
4414 return;
4415 }
4416 if(TestWarning(prjn->from != prjn->layer, "Connect_impl",
4417 "requires send and recv to be the same layer -- lateral projection!")) {
4418 return;
4419 }
4420 if(TestWarning(prjn->con_spec->wt_limits.sym, "Connect_impl",
4421 "cannot have wt_limits.sym on in conspec -- turning off in spec:",
4422 prjn->con_spec->name,
4423 "This might affect children of this spec.")) {
4424 prjn->con_spec->SetUnique("wt_limits", true);
4425 prjn->con_spec->wt_limits.sym = false;
4426 prjn->con_spec->UpdateAfterEdit();
4427 }
4428
4429 CreateStencils();
4430
4431 Layer* lay = prjn->from;
4432 TwoDCoord gp_geo = lay->gp_geom;
4433 TwoDCoord un_geo = lay->un_geom;
4434 float n_angles = (float)un_geo.x;
4435
4436 TwoDCoord ruc;
4437 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
4438 int rgpidx = 0;
4439 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < gp_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
4440 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < gp_geo.x; ruc.x++, rgpidx++) {
4441 TwoDCoord suc;
4442 TwoDCoord suc_wrp;
4443 for(suc.y = ruc.y-radius; suc.y <= ruc.y+radius; suc.y++) {
4444 for(suc.x = ruc.x-radius; suc.x <= ruc.x+radius; suc.x++) {
4445 suc_wrp = suc;
4446 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, gp_geo) && !wrap)
4447 continue;
4448 int sgpidx = lay->UnitGpIdxFmPos(suc_wrp);
4449 if(!lay->UnitGpIdxIsValid(sgpidx)) continue;
4450
4451 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc; // don't use wrap!
4452 float dst = del.Mag();
4453 if(dst > (float)radius) continue; // out of bounds
4454 if(dst == 0.0f) continue; // no selfs
4455
4456 TwoDCoord run;
4457 TwoDCoord sun;
4458
4459 for(run.x = 0; run.x < un_geo.x; run.x++) {
4460 for(sun.x = 0; sun.x < un_geo.x; sun.x++) {
4461 for(run.y = 0; run.y < un_geo.y; run.y++) {
4462 int syst = (run.y / 2) * 2;
4463 int syed = syst+2;
4464 for(sun.y = syst; sun.y < syed; sun.y++) {
4465 // mod 2 on y allows for multiple depths to be replicated
4466 float wt = v2ffbo_weights.FastEl(del.x +radius, del.y+radius,
4467 sun.y % 2, sun.x, run.y % 2, run.x);
4468 if(wt <= con_thr) continue;
4469
4470 int rui = run.y * un_geo.x + run.x;
4471 int sui = sun.y * un_geo.x + sun.x;
4472
4473 Unit* ru_u = lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
4474 if(!ru_u) continue;
4475 Unit* su_u = lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
4476 if(!su_u) continue;
4477 if(alloc_loop) {
4478 ru_u->RecvConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4479 su_u->SendConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4480 }
4481 else {
4482 Connection* cn = ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
4483 cn->wt = wt;
4484 }
4485 }
4486 }
4487 }
4488 }
4489 }
4490 }
4491 }
4492 }
4493 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do allocations
4494 prjn->layer->RecvConsPostAlloc(prjn);
4495 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
4496 }
4497 }
4498}
4499
4500void V2BoLateralPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
4501 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
4502 Layer* lay = prjn->from;
4503 TwoDCoord gp_geo = lay->gp_geom;
4504 TwoDCoord un_geo = lay->un_geom;
4505 float n_angles = (float)un_geo.x;
4506
4507 TwoDCoord gp_geo_half = gp_geo / 2;
4508
4509 int rgpidx;
4510 int rui;
4511 lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
4512 TwoDCoord ruc = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(rgpidx);
4513 TwoDCoord run;
4514 run.SetFmIndex(rui, un_geo.x);
4515 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
4516 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
4517 int sgpidx;
4518 int sui;
4519 lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, sui, sgpidx);
4520 TwoDCoord suc = lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(sgpidx);
4521 TwoDCoord sun;
4522 sun.SetFmIndex(sui, un_geo.x);
4523
4524 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc;
4525 if(wrap) { // dist may be closer in wrapped case..
4526 suc.WrapMinDist(del, gp_geo, ruc, gp_geo_half);
4527 }
4528
4529 float wt = v2ffbo_weights.FastEl(del.x + radius, del.y + radius,
4530 sun.y % 2, sun.x, run.y % 2, run.x);
4531 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
4532 }
4533}

4539
4540void FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl::Initialize() {
4541 con_radius = 14;
4542 wt_radius = 0.7f;
4543 dist_sig = 0.3f;
4544 ang_sig = 1.0f;
4545 ellipse_ratio = 1.0f;
4546 ellipse_angle = 0.0f;
4547 max_wt = 1.0f;
4548 min_wt = 0.1f;
4549 con_thr = 0.2f;
4550}
4551
4552void FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
4553 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
4554 CreateStencil();
4555}
4556
4557void FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl::CreateStencil() {
4558 int n_angles = 4;
4559 int max_cnt = (2 * con_radius + 1);
4560 fgbo_weights.SetGeom(4, max_cnt, max_cnt, 2, n_angles);
4561 TwoDCoord suc; // send coords
4562 int cnt = 0;
4563 for(suc.y = -con_radius; suc.y <= con_radius; suc.y++) {
4564 int ysuc_dx = suc.y + con_radius;
4565 for(suc.x = -con_radius; suc.x <= con_radius; suc.x++) {
4566 int xsuc_dx = suc.x + con_radius;
4567 for(int sang_dx = 0; sang_dx < n_angles; sang_dx++) {
4568 for(int sdir = 0; sdir < 2; sdir++) { // integrate over sending directions
4569 float wt = ConWt(suc, sang_dx, sdir);
4570 fgbo_weights.FastEl(xsuc_dx, ysuc_dx, sdir, sang_dx) = wt;
4571 }
4572 }
4573 }
4574 }
4575}
4576
4577float FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl::ConWt(TwoDCoord& suc, int sang_dx, int sdir) {
4578 float n_angles = 4.0f;
4579
4580 TwoDCoord del = suc;
4581 float dst = del.Mag();
4582 if(dst > (float)con_radius) return 0.0f;
4583 if(dst == 0.0f) return 0.0f; // no self con
4584 float nrmdst = dst / (float)con_radius;
4585
4586 float gang = atan2f(del.y, del.x); // group angle -- 0..pi or -pi
4587 if(gang < 0.0f) gang += 2.0f * taMath_float::pi; // keep it positive
4588
4589 float pang = gang + 0.5f * taMath_float::pi; // perpendicular angle
4590 if(pang > 2.0f * taMath_float::pi) pang -= 2.0f * taMath_float::pi;
4591
4592 // dir 0 = 0..pi, dir 1 = pi..2pi
4593 float sang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)sang_dx / n_angles) + taMath_float::pi * (float)sdir;
4594
4595 float dang; // delta-angle -- keep this positive too
4596 if(sang < pang)
4597 dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi + sang) - pang;
4598 else
4599 dang = sang - pang;
4600 if(dang >= taMath_float::pi) dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi) - dang;
4601
4602 if(ellipse_ratio < 1.0f) {
4603 float a = (float)con_radius;
4604 float b = ellipse_ratio * a;
4605 float elang = ellipse_angle * taMath_float::rad_per_deg;
4606 float R = (b*b - a*a) * cosf(2.0f * gang - 2.0f * elang) + a*a + b*b;
4607 float Q = sqrtf(2) * a * b * sqrtf(R);
4608 float r = Q / R;
4609 nrmdst = dst / r; // normalize relative to outer radius!
4610 }
4611
4612 float netwt = max_wt * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(dang, ang_sig)
4613 * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm((nrmdst-wt_radius), dist_sig);
4614
4615 return netwt;
4616}

4623}

4640 }
