4642
4643void FgBoEllipseGpPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
4644// dbg_hit_cnt = 0; // debugging
4645
4646 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
4647
4648 if(TestWarning(group_specs.size == 0, "Connect_impl",
4649 "group_specs must have at least one item!")) {
4650 return;
4651 }
4652 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
4653 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
4654 return;
4655 }
4656 if(TestWarning(!prjn->from->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
4657 "requires send layer to have unit groups!")) {
4658 return;
4659 }
4660// if(TestWarning(prjn->con_spec->wt_limits.sym, "Connect_impl",
4661// "cannot have wt_limits.sym on in conspec -- turning off in spec:",
4662// prjn->con_spec->name,
4663// "This might affect children of this spec.")) {
4664// prjn->con_spec->SetUnique("wt_limits", true);
4665// prjn->con_spec->wt_limits.sym = false;
4666// prjn->con_spec->UpdateAfterEdit();
4667// }
4668
4669 CreateStencils();
4670
4671 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
4672 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
4673 if(reciprocal) { // switch!
4674 recv_lay = prjn->from;
4675 send_lay = prjn->layer;
4676 }
4677 TwoDCoord rgp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
4678 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
4679 TwoDCoord sgp_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
4680 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
4681
4682 int n_depth = sun_geo.y / 2; // number of different depths represented
4683 int ruy_per_depth = run_geo.y / n_depth;
4684 int run_per_depth = recv_lay->un_geom.n / n_depth;
4685 if(TestWarning(ruy_per_depth * n_depth != run_geo.y, "Connect_impl",
4686 "recv layer un_geom.y must be even multiple of number of depths represented in the input:", StringtaString(n_depth))) {
4687 return;
4688 }
4689
4690 float n_angles = (float)sun_geo.x;
4691
4692 if(TestWarning(run_per_depth != group_specs.size, "Connect_impl",
4693 "recv layer units per depth is not same as number of group specs -- should be -- redundant or incomplete connections will be created")) {
4694 }
4695
4696 TwoDCoord rgp_sc = sgp_geo / rgp_geo;
4697 TwoDCoord rgp_chk = rgp_geo * rgp_sc;
4698
4699 if(TestWarning(rgp_chk != sgp_geo, "Connect_impl",
4700 "recv layer gp_geom is not an even multiple of send layer gp_geom -- should be! Some units will not be connected", rgp_sc.GetStr(), rgp_chk.GetStr())) {
4701 }
4702
4703
4704 TwoDCoord ruc;
4705 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
4706 int rcnt = 0;
4707 TwoDCoord run;
4708 for(run.y = 0; run.y < run_geo.y; run.y++) {
4709 int depth = run.y / ruy_per_depth;
4710 int suy_st = depth * 2;
4711 for(run.x = 0; run.x < run_geo.x; run.x++, rcnt++) {
4712 FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl* el = group_specs.FastEl(rcnt % group_specs.size);
4713
4714 float wt_renorm = (1.0f - el->min_wt);
4715
4716 int rgpidx = 0;
4717 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < rgp_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
4718 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < rgp_geo.x; ruc.x++, rgpidx++) {
4719 TwoDCoord ruc_s = ruc * rgp_sc; // project ruc into s coords
4720
4721 TwoDCoord suc;
4722 TwoDCoord suc_wrp;
4723 for(suc.y = ruc_s.y-el->con_radius; suc.y <= ruc_s.y+el->con_radius; suc.y++) {
4724 for(suc.x = ruc_s.x-el->con_radius; suc.x <= ruc_s.x+el->con_radius; suc.x++) {
4725 suc_wrp = suc;
4726 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, sgp_geo) && !wrap)
4727 continue;
4728 int sgpidx = send_lay->UnitGpIdxFmPos(suc_wrp);
4729 if(!send_lay->UnitGpIdxIsValid(sgpidx)) continue;
4730
4731 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc_s; // don't use wrap!
4732 float dst = del.Mag();
4733 if(dst > (float)el->con_radius) continue; // out of bounds
4734 if(dst == 0.0f) continue; // no selfs
4735
4736 TwoDCoord sun;
4737
4738 for(sun.x = 0; sun.x < sun_geo.x; sun.x++) {
4739 for(sun.y = suy_st; sun.y < suy_st+2; sun.y++) {
4740 float wt = el->fgbo_weights.FastEl(del.x +el->con_radius,
4741 del.y+el->con_radius, sun.y-suy_st, sun.x);
4742 if(wt <= el->con_thr) continue;
4743 wt = wt * wt_renorm + el->min_wt; // renorm to min wt range
4744
4745 int rui = run.y * run_geo.x + run.x;
4746 int sui = sun.y * sun_geo.x + sun.x;
4747
4748 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
4749 if(!ru_u) continue;
4750 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
4751 if(!su_u) continue;
4752 if(alloc_loop) {
4753 if(reciprocal) {
4754 su_u->RecvConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4755 ru_u->SendConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4756 }
4757 else {
4758 ru_u->RecvConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4759 su_u->SendConsAllocInc(1, prjn);
4760 }
4761 }
4762 else {
4763 if(reciprocal) {
4764 Connection* cn = su_u->ConnectFrom(ru_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
4765 if(cn) cn->wt = wt;
4766 }
4767 else {
4768 Connection* cn = ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
4769 if(cn) cn->wt = wt;
4770 }
4771 }
4772 }
4773 }
4774 }
4775 }
4776 }
4777 }
4778 }
4779 }
4780 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do allocations
4781 prjn->layer->RecvConsPostAlloc(prjn);
4782 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
4783 }
4784 }
4785}
4786
4787void FgBoEllipseGpPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
4788 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
4789 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
4790 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
4791 if(reciprocal) { // switch!
4792 recv_lay = prjn->from;
4793 send_lay = prjn->layer;
4794 }
4795 TwoDCoord rgp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
4796 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
4797 TwoDCoord sgp_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
4798 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
4799 float n_angles = (float)sun_geo.x;
4800 int n_depth = sun_geo.y / 2; // number of different depths represented
4801 int ruy_per_depth = run_geo.y / n_depth;
4802
4803 TwoDCoord rgp_sc = sgp_geo / rgp_geo;
4804 TwoDCoord sgp_geo_half = sgp_geo / 2;
4805
4806 if(reciprocal) {
4807 int sgpidx;
4808 int sui;
4809 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, sui, sgpidx); // send = recv!
4810 TwoDCoord suc = send_lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(sgpidx);
4811 TwoDCoord sun;
4812 sun.SetFmIndex(sui, sun_geo.x);
4813 int depth = sun.y / 2;
4814 int suy_st = depth * 2;
4815
4816 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
4817 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
4818 int rgpidx;
4819 int rui;
4820 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, rui, rgpidx); // recv = send!
4821 TwoDCoord ruc = recv_lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(rgpidx);
4822 TwoDCoord ruc_s = ruc * rgp_sc; // project ruc into s coords
4823 TwoDCoord run;
4824 run.SetFmIndex(rui, run_geo.x);
4825 FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl* el = group_specs.FastEl(rui % group_specs.size);
4826 float wt_renorm = (1.0f - el->min_wt);
4827
4828 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc_s;
4829 if(wrap) { // dist may be closer in wrapped case..
4830 suc.WrapMinDist(del, sgp_geo, ruc_s, sgp_geo_half);
4831 }
4832
4833 float wt = el->fgbo_weights.FastEl(del.x + el->con_radius, del.y + el->con_radius,
4834 sun.y-suy_st, sun.x);
4835 wt = wt * wt_renorm + el->min_wt; // renorm to min wt range
4836 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
4837 }
4838 }
4839 else {
4840 int rgpidx;
4841 int rui;
4842 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
4843 TwoDCoord ruc = recv_lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(rgpidx);
4844 TwoDCoord ruc_s = ruc * rgp_sc; // project ruc into s coords
4845 TwoDCoord run;
4846 run.SetFmIndex(rui, run_geo.x);
4847 int depth = run.y / ruy_per_depth;
4848 int suy_st = depth * 2;
4849
4850 FgBoEllipseGpPrjnEl* el = group_specs.FastEl(rui % group_specs.size);
4851 float wt_renorm = (1.0f - el->min_wt);
4852
4853 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
4854 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
4855 int sgpidx;
4856 int sui;
4857 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, sui, sgpidx);
4858 TwoDCoord suc = send_lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(sgpidx);
4859 TwoDCoord sun;
4860 sun.SetFmIndex(sui, sun_geo.x);
4861
4862 TwoDCoord del = suc - ruc_s;
4863 if(wrap) { // dist may be closer in wrapped case..
4864 suc.WrapMinDist(del, sgp_geo, ruc_s, sgp_geo_half);
4865 }
4866
4867 float wt = el->fgbo_weights.FastEl(del.x + el->con_radius, del.y + el->con_radius,
4868 sun.y-suy_st, sun.x);
4869 wt = wt * wt_renorm + el->min_wt; // renorm to min wt range
4870 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
4871 }
4872 }
4873}
4874

4877//////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
4878// FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec
4879
4880void FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
4881 wrap = true;
4882 init_wts = true;
4883 dist_sigma = 0.8f;
4884 ang_sigma = 1.0f;
4885 wt_base = 0.25f;
4886 wt_range = 0.5f;
4887}
4888
4889void FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
4890 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
4891 CreateStencil();
4892}
4893
4894void FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::CreateStencil() {
4895 int n_angles = 4;
4896 int n_wedges = 8;
4897 fgbo_weights.SetGeom(5, send_gp_size.x, send_gp_size.y, 2, n_angles, n_wedges);
4898 TwoDCoord suc; // send coords
4899 for(int wedge=0; wedge < n_wedges; wedge++) {
4900 for(suc.y = 0; suc.y < send_gp_size.y; suc.y++) {
4901 for(suc.x = 0; suc.x < send_gp_size.x; suc.x++) {
4902 for(int sang_dx = 0; sang_dx < n_angles; sang_dx++) {
4903 for(int sdir = 0; sdir < 2; sdir++) { // integrate over sending directions
4904 float wt;
4905 if(wedge < 4)
4906 wt = ConWt_Wedge(wedge, suc, send_gp_size, sang_dx, sdir);
4907 else
4908 wt = ConWt_Line(wedge-4, suc, send_gp_size, sang_dx, sdir);
4909 fgbo_weights.FastEl(suc.x, suc.y, sdir, sang_dx, wedge) = wt;
4910 }
4911 }
4912 }
4913 }
4914 }
4915}
4916
4917float FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::ConWt_Wedge(int wedge, TwoDCoord& suc, TwoDCoord& su_geo, int sang_dx, int sdir) {
4918 float n_angles = 4.0f;
4919
4920 TwoDCoord ctr;
4921 switch(wedge) {
4922 case 0:
4923 ctr.SetXY(0,0);
4924 break;
4925 case 1:
4926 ctr.SetXY(su_geo.x-1,0);
4927 break;
4928 case 2:
4929 ctr.SetXY(su_geo.x-1,su_geo.y-1);
4930 break;
4931 case 3:
4932 ctr.SetXY(0,su_geo.y-1);
4933 break;
4934 }
4935
4936 TwoDCoord del = suc - ctr;
4937 float dst = del.Mag();
4938 float nrmdst = dst / (float)su_geo.x; // assume square
4939
4940 float gang = atan2f(del.y, del.x); // group angle -- 0..pi or -pi
4941 if(gang < 0.0f) gang += 2.0f * taMath_float::pi; // keep it positive
4942
4943 float pang = gang + 0.5f * taMath_float::pi; // perpendicular angle
4944 if(pang > 2.0f * taMath_float::pi) pang -= 2.0f * taMath_float::pi;
4945
4946 // dir 0 = 0..pi, dir 1 = pi..2pi
4947 float sang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)sang_dx / n_angles) + taMath_float::pi * (float)sdir;
4948
4949 float dang; // delta-angle -- keep this positive too
4950 if(sang < pang)
4951 dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi + sang) - pang;
4952 else
4953 dang = sang - pang;
4954 if(dang >= taMath_float::pi) dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi) - dang;
4955
4956 float netwt = wt_base + wt_range * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(dang, ang_sigma)
4957 * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm((nrmdst-1.0f), dist_sigma);
4958
4959 return netwt;
4960}
4961
4962float FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::ConWt_Line(int line, TwoDCoord& suc, TwoDCoord& su_geo, int sang_dx, int sdir) {
4963 float n_angles = 4.0f;
4964
4965 TwoDCoord su_geo_half = su_geo / 2;
4966
4967 float dst;
4968 switch(line) {
4969 case 0:
4970 case 2:
4971 dst = (float)(suc.y - su_geo_half.y);
4972 break;
4973 case 1:
4974 case 3:
4975 dst = (float)(suc.x - su_geo_half.x);
4976 break;
4977 }
4978
4979 float pang = (float)(line) * 0.5f * taMath_float::pi;
4980 float nrmdst = dst / (float)su_geo.x; // assume square
4981
4982 // dir 0 = 0..pi, dir 1 = pi..2pi
4983 float sang = taMath_float::pi * ((float)sang_dx / n_angles) + taMath_float::pi * (float)sdir;
4984
4985 float dang; // delta-angle -- keep this positive too
4986 if(sang < pang)
4987 dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi + sang) - pang;
4988 else
4989 dang = sang - pang;
4990 if(dang >= taMath_float::pi) dang = (2.0f * taMath_float::pi) - dang;
4991
4992 float netwt = wt_base + wt_range * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(dang, ang_sigma)
4993 * taMath_float::gauss_den_nonorm(nrmdst, dist_sigma);
4994
4995 return netwt;
4996}
4997
4998void FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
4999 CreateStencil();
5000 inherited::Connect_impl(prjn);
5001}
5002
5003void FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::Connect_UnitGroup(Projection* prjn, Layer* recv_lay,
5004 Layer* send_lay, int rgpidx, int sgpidx, int alloc_loop) {
5005 int ru_nunits = recv_lay->un_geom.n;
5006 int su_nunits = send_lay->un_geom.n;
5007 int n_wedges = 8;
5008
5009 TwoDCoord sug;
5010 if(reciprocal) { // reciprocal is backwards!
5011 for(int sui=0; sui < su_nunits; sui++) {
5012 sug.SetFmIndex(sui, send_lay->un_geom.x);
5013 int cur_depth = sug.y / 2; // v2bo has 2 per depth always
5014 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
5015 for(int rui=0; rui < ru_nunits; rui++) {
5016 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5017 int ru_depth = rui / n_wedges;
5018 if(cur_depth != ru_depth) continue;
5019 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
5020 su_u->ConnectFrom(ru_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // recip!
5021 }
5022 }
5023 }
5024 else {
5025 for(int rui=0; rui < ru_nunits; rui++) {
5026 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5027 int ru_depth = rui / n_wedges;
5028 for(int sui=0; sui < su_nunits; sui++) {
5029 sug.SetFmIndex(sui, send_lay->un_geom.x);
5030 int cur_depth = sug.y / 2; // v2bo has 2 per depth always
5031 if(cur_depth != ru_depth) continue;
5032 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
5033 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
5034 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // recip!
5035 }
5036 }
5037 }
5038}
5039
5040void FgBoWedgeGpPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
5041 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
5042 if(cg->size == 0) return;
5043 int n_wedges = 8;
5044
5045 if(reciprocal) {
5046 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->from;
5047 Layer* send_lay = prjn->layer;
5048 TwoDCoord sgp_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
5049 TwoDCoord sgp_geo_half = sgp_geo / 2;
5050
5051 int sgpidx;
5052 int sui;
5053 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, sui, sgpidx); // recv = send!
5054 TwoDCoord suc;
5055 suc.SetFmIndex(sui, send_lay->un_geom.x);
5056 TwoDCoord sgpc;
5057 sgpc.SetFmIndex(sgpidx, send_lay->gp_geom.x);
5058 int sdir = suc.y % 2;
5059 int sang_dx = suc.x;
5060
5061 for(int i=0; i < cg->size; i++) {
5062 Unit* su = cg->Un(i); // this is actually ru
5063 int rgpidx;
5064 int rui;
5065 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, rui, rgpidx); // recv = send!
5066 int wedge = rui % n_wedges;
5067
5068 RecvCons* rucg = su->recv.FindFrom(send_lay); // recip prjn
5069 if(!rucg) continue;
5070 Unit* ssu = rucg->Un(0); // first sending unit in that guy's prjn
5071 int ssgpidx;
5072 int ssui;
5073 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ssu->idx, ssui, ssgpidx);
5074 TwoDCoord ssgpc;
5075 ssgpc.SetFmIndex(ssgpidx, send_lay->gp_geom.x);
5076
5077 TwoDCoord del = sgpc - ssgpc;
5078 sgpc.WrapMinDist(del, sgp_geo, ssgpc, sgp_geo_half);
5079
5080 float wt = fgbo_weights.FastEl(del.x, del.y, sdir, sang_dx, wedge);
5081 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
5082 }
5083 }
5084 else {
5085 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5086 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5087 TwoDCoord sgp_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
5088 TwoDCoord sgp_geo_half = sgp_geo / 2;
5089
5090 int rgpidx;
5091 int rui;
5092 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
5093 int wedge = rui % n_wedges;
5094
5095 Unit* ssu = cg->Un(0);
5096 int ssgpidx;
5097 int ssui;
5098 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ssu->idx, ssui, ssgpidx);
5099 TwoDCoord ssgpc;
5100 ssgpc.SetFmIndex(ssgpidx, send_lay->gp_geom.x);
5101
5102 for(int i=0; i < cg->size; i++) {
5103 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
5104 int sgpidx;
5105 int sui;
5106 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, sui, sgpidx);
5107 TwoDCoord suc;
5108 suc.SetFmIndex(sui, send_lay->un_geom.x);
5109 TwoDCoord sgpc;
5110 sgpc.SetFmIndex(sgpidx, send_lay->gp_geom.x);
5111
5112 TwoDCoord del = sgpc - ssgpc;
5113 sgpc.WrapMinDist(del, sgp_geo, ssgpc, sgp_geo_half);
5114
5115 int sdir = suc.y % 2;
5116 int sang_dx = suc.x;
5117 float wt = fgbo_weights.FastEl(del.x, del.y, sdir, sang_dx, wedge);
5118 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
5119 }
5120 }
5121}

5126void V1EndStopPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
5127 n_angles = 4;
5128 end_stop_dist = 2;
5129 adjang_wt = 0.2f;
5130 wrap = true;
5131 init_wts = true;
5132}

5134void V1EndStopPrjnSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
5135 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
5136 wrap = true;
5137}
5138
5139static void es_get_angles(float angf, float& cosx, float& siny) {
5140 cosx = taMath_float::cos(angf);
5141 siny = taMath_float::sin(angf);
5142 // always normalize by the largest value so that it is equal to 1
5143 // not for these guys!!
5144// if(fabsf(cosx) > fabsf(siny)) {
5145// siny = siny / fabsf(cosx); // must come first!
5146// cosx = cosx / fabsf(cosx);
5147// }
5148// else {
5149// cosx = cosx / fabsf(siny);
5150// siny = siny / fabsf(siny);
5151// }
5152}
5153
5154void V1EndStopPrjnSpec::InitStencils(Projection* prjn) {
5155 v1s_ang_slopes.SetGeom(3,2,2,n_angles);
5156 float ang_inc = taMath_float::pi / (float)n_angles;
5157 for(int ang=0; ang<n_angles; ang++) {
5158 float cosx, siny;
5159 float angf = (float)ang * ang_inc;
5160 es_get_angles(angf, cosx, siny);
5161 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, LINE, ang) = cosx;
5162 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, LINE, ang) = siny;
5163
5164 es_get_angles(angf + taMath_float::pi * .5f, cosx, siny);
5165 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, ORTHO, ang) = cosx;
5166 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, ORTHO, ang) = siny;
5167 }
5168
5169 v1c_es_stencils.SetGeom(4, 2, 2, 2, n_angles);
5170
5171 if(n_angles == 4) {
5172 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 0, 0) = -end_stop_dist;
5173 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 0, 0) = -end_stop_dist;
5174 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 0, 0) = -end_stop_dist;
5175 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 0, 0) = end_stop_dist;
5176 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 1, 0) = end_stop_dist;
5177 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 1, 0) = -end_stop_dist;
5178 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 1, 0) = end_stop_dist;
5179 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 1, 0) = end_stop_dist;
5180
5181 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 0, 2) = -end_stop_dist;
5182 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 0, 2) = -end_stop_dist;
5183 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 0, 2) = -end_stop_dist;
5184 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 0, 2) = end_stop_dist;
5185 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 1, 2) = end_stop_dist;
5186 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 1, 2) = -end_stop_dist;
5187 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 1, 2) = end_stop_dist;
5188 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 1, 2) = end_stop_dist;
5189
5190 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 0, 1) = -end_stop_dist;
5191 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 0, 1) = 0;
5192 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 0, 1) = end_stop_dist;
5193 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 0, 1) = 0;
5194 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 1, 1) = 0;
5195 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 1, 1) = -end_stop_dist;
5196 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 1, 1) = 0;
5197 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 1, 1) = end_stop_dist;
5198
5199 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 0, 3) = -end_stop_dist;
5200 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 0, 3) = 0;
5201 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 0, 3) = end_stop_dist;
5202 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 0, 3) = 0;
5203 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 0, 1, 3) = 0;
5204 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 0, 1, 3) = -end_stop_dist;
5205 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, 1, 1, 3) = 0;
5206 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, 1, 1, 3) = end_stop_dist;
5207 }
5208 else {
5209 for(int ang=0; ang < n_angles; ang++) {
5210 for(int sidx=0; sidx < 2; sidx++) {
5211 int side = (sidx == 0) ? -1 : 1;
5212
5213 int sx = (int)(end_stop_dist * (float)side * v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, LINE, ang));
5214 int sy = (int)(end_stop_dist * (float)side * v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, LINE, ang));
5215 for(int lpdx=0; lpdx < 2; lpdx++) {
5216 int lpt = (lpdx == 0) ? -1 : 1;
5217 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X, lpdx, sidx, ang) = sx +
5218 (int)(end_stop_dist *(float)lpt * v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, ORTHO, ang));
5219 v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y, lpdx, sidx, ang) = sy +
5220 (int)(end_stop_dist * (float)lpt * v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, ORTHO, ang));
5221 }
5222 }
5223 }
5224 }
5225
5226 v1c_es_angwts.SetGeom(2, n_angles, n_angles);
5227 for(int ang1=0; ang1 < n_angles; ang1++) {
5228 for(int ang2=0; ang2 < n_angles; ang2++) {
5229 int ang_dst = ABS(ang1-ang2)((ang1-ang2) >= 0 ? (ang1-ang2) : -(ang1-ang2));
5230 {
5231 int wrap_dst = ABS(ang1 - (ang2 + n_angles))((ang1 - (ang2 + n_angles)) >= 0 ? (ang1 - (ang2 + n_angles
)) : -(ang1 - (ang2 + n_angles)));
5232 if(wrap_dst < ang_dst) ang_dst = wrap_dst;
5233 }
5234 {
5235 int wrap_dst = ABS(ang1 - (ang2 - n_angles))((ang1 - (ang2 - n_angles)) >= 0 ? (ang1 - (ang2 - n_angles
)) : -(ang1 - (ang2 - n_angles)));
5236 if(wrap_dst < ang_dst) ang_dst = wrap_dst;
5237 }
5238 float wt;
5239 if(ang_dst == 0)
5240 wt = 0.0f;
5241 else if(ang_dst == 1)
5242 wt = adjang_wt;
5243 else
5244 wt = 1.0f;
5245 v1c_es_angwts.FastEl(ang1, ang2) = wt;
5246 }
5247 }
5248}
5249
5250void V1EndStopPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
5251 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
5252
5253 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
5254 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
5255 return;
5256 }
5257 if(TestWarning(!prjn->from->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
5258 "requires send layer to have unit groups!")) {
5259 return;
5260 }
5261
5262 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5263 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5264
5265 if(TestWarning(recv_lay->gp_geom != send_lay->gp_geom, "Connect_impl",
5266 "Recv layer does not have same gp geometry as sending layer -- cannot connect!")) {
5267 return;
5268 }
5269
5270 TwoDCoord gp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom; // same as sgp
5271
5272 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
5273 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
5274 int su_n = sun_geo.Product();
5275 int ru_n = run_geo.Product();
5276
5277 if(TestWarning(run_geo.x != sun_geo.x, "Connect_impl",
5278 "Recv layer does not have same x-dimension unit geometry within unit groups as sending layer -- cannot connect!")) {
5279 return;
5280 }
5281 if(TestWarning(run_geo.y != 1, "Connect_impl",
5282 "Recv layer should have a single y-dimension unit geometry within unit groups")) {
5283 return;
5284 }
5285
5286 InitStencils(prjn);
5287
5288 int n_cons = sun_geo.y + 2 * 2 * (n_angles-1) * sun_geo.y;
5289
5290 TwoDCoord ruc;
5291 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop >= 0; alloc_loop--) {
5292 int rgpidx = 0;
5293 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < gp_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
5294 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < gp_geo.x; ruc.x++, rgpidx++) {
5295
5296 for(int ang = 0; ang < n_angles; ang++) { // angles
5297 int rui = ang;
5298 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5299 if(!ru_u) continue;
5300 if(!alloc_loop)
5301 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(n_cons, prjn);
5302
5303 TwoDCoord sun;
5304 for(sun.y = 0; sun.y < sun_geo.y; sun.y++) {
5305 // central point (same as ruc -- use rgpidx)
5306 int sui = sun.y * n_angles + ang;
5307 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, rgpidx);
5308 if(!su_u) continue;
5309 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
5310
5311 for(int sidx=0; sidx < 2; sidx++) {
5312 for(int lpdx=0; lpdx < 2; lpdx++) {
5313 int xp = v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(X,lpdx,sidx,ang);
5314 int yp = v1c_es_stencils.FastEl(Y,lpdx,sidx,ang);
5315
5316 TwoDCoord suc = ruc;
5317 suc.x += xp; suc.y += yp;
5318 TwoDCoord suc_wrp = suc;
5319 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, gp_geo) && !wrap)
5320 continue;
5321 int sgpidx = send_lay->UnitGpIdxFmPos(suc_wrp);
5322 if(!send_lay->UnitGpIdxIsValid(sgpidx)) continue;
5323
5324 for(int opang=0; opang<n_angles; opang++) {
5325 float angwt = v1c_es_angwts.FastEl(ang, opang);
5326 if(angwt == 0.0f) continue;
5327
5328 int sui = sun.y * n_angles + opang;
5329 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
5330 if(!su_u) continue;
5331 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
5332 }
5333 }
5334 }
5335 }
5336 } // for ang
5337 }
5338 }
5339 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
5340 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
5341 }
5342 }
5343}
5344
5345void V1EndStopPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
5346 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
5347 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5348 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5349 TwoDCoord gp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom; // same as sgp
5350
5351 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
5352 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
5353 int su_n = sun_geo.Product();
5354 int ru_n = run_geo.Product();
5355
5356 int n_cons = sun_geo.y + 2 * 2 * (n_angles-1) * sun_geo.y;
5357 if(cg->size != n_cons) return; // no can do
5358
5359 int rgpidx;
5360 int rui;
5361 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
5362
5363 int ang = rui;
5364
5365 int cnidx = 0;
5366 TwoDCoord sun;
5367 for(sun.y = 0; sun.y < sun_geo.y; sun.y++) {
5368 cg->Cn(cnidx++)->wt = 1.0f; // center point
5369 for(int sidx=0; sidx < 2; sidx++) {
5370 for(int lpdx=0; lpdx < 2; lpdx++) {
5371 for(int opang=0; opang<n_angles; opang++) {
5372 float angwt = v1c_es_angwts.FastEl(rui, opang);
5373 if(angwt == 0.0f) continue;
5374 cg->Cn(cnidx++)->wt = angwt;
5375 }
5376 }
5377 }
5378 }
5379}

5383
5384void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
5385 n_disps = 1;
5386 disp_range_pct = 0.05f;
5387 gauss_sig = 0.7f;
5388 disp_spacing = 2.0f;
5389 end_extra = 2;
5390 wrap = true;
5391
5392 init_wts = true;
5393
5394 tot_disps = 1 + 2 * n_disps;
5395 UpdateFmV1sSize(24);
5396}
5397
5398void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::UpdateAfterEdit_impl() {
5399 inherited::UpdateAfterEdit_impl();
5400 tot_disps = 1 + 2 * n_disps;
5401}
5402
5403
5404void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
5405 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
5406 if(prjn->layer->units.leaves == 0) // an empty layer!
5407 return;
5408 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
5409 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
5410 return;
5411 }
5412 if(TestWarning(!prjn->from->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
5413 "requires sending layer to have unit groups!")) {
5414 return;
5415 }
5416
5417 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5418 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5419 TwoDCoord rgp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
5420 TwoDCoord sgp_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
5421
5422 if(TestWarning(rgp_geo != sgp_geo, "Connect_Gps",
5423 "Recv layer does not have same gp geometry as sending layer -- cannot connect!")) {
5424 return;
5425 }
5426 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
5427 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
5428
5429 int su_n = sun_geo.Product();
5430 int ru_n = run_geo.Product();
5431
5432 if(TestWarning(ru_n != su_n * tot_disps, "Connect_Gps",
5433 "Recv layer unit groups must have n_disps * 2 + 1=",
5434 StringtaString(tot_disps),"times number of units in send layer unit group=",
5435 StringtaString(su_n)," should be:", StringtaString(su_n * tot_disps), "is:",
5436 StringtaString(ru_n))) {
5437 return;
5438 }
5439
5440 if(prjn->recv_idx == 0) // right eye
5441 Connect_RightEye(prjn);
5442 else
5443 Connect_LeftEye(prjn);
5444}
5445
5446void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::Connect_RightEye(Projection* prjn) {
5447 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5448 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5449 TwoDCoord gp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
5450
5451 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
5452 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
5453 int su_n = sun_geo.Product();
5454 int ru_n = run_geo.Product();
5455
5456 // note: could optimize this code b/c sender alloc = tot_disps so could be pre-alloc entirely
5457 TwoDCoord ruc;
5458 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop >= 0; alloc_loop--) {
5459 int rgpidx = 0;
5460 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < gp_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
5461 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < gp_geo.x; ruc.x++, rgpidx++) {
5462 for(int rui=0; rui<ru_n; rui++) {
5463 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5464 if(!ru_u) continue;
5465 if(!alloc_loop)
5466 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(1, prjn); // just one prjn!
5467
5468 int sui = rui % su_n; // just modulus -- recv from same features tot_disps times
5469 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, rgpidx); // rgp = sgp
5470 if(!su_u) continue;
5471 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
5472 }
5473 }
5474 }
5475 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
5476 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
5477 }
5478 }
5479}
5480
5481void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::InitStencils(Projection* prjn) {
5482 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5483 TwoDCoord gp_geo = send_lay->gp_geom;
5484
5485 UpdateFmV1sSize(gp_geo.x);
5486
5487 v1b_widths.SetGeom(1, tot_disps);
5488 v1b_weights.SetGeom(2, max_width, tot_disps);
5489 v1b_stencils.SetGeom(2, max_width, tot_disps);
5490
5491 v1b_weights.InitVals(0.0f); // could have some lurkers in there from other settings, which can affect normalization
5492
5493 int twe = disp_range + end_ext;
5494
5495 // everything is conditional on the disparity
5496 for(int disp=-n_disps; disp <= n_disps; disp++) {
5497 int didx = disp + n_disps;
5498 int doff = disp * disp_spc;
5499 if(disp == 0) { // focal
5500 v1b_widths.FastEl(didx) = 1 + 2 * disp_range;
5501 for(int tw=-disp_range; tw<=disp_range; tw++) {
5502 int twidx = tw + disp_range;
5503 float fx = (float)tw / (float)disp_range;
5504 v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx) = taMath_float::gauss_den_sig(fx, gauss_sig);
5505 v1b_stencils.FastEl(twidx, didx) = doff + tw;
5506 }
5507 }
5508 else if(disp == -n_disps) {
5509 v1b_widths.FastEl(didx) = 1 + 2 * disp_range + end_ext;
5510 for(int tw=-twe; tw<=disp_range; tw++) {
5511 int twidx = tw + twe;
5512 if(tw < 0)
5513 v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx) = taMath_float::gauss_den_sig(0.0f, gauss_sig);
5514 else {
5515 float fx = (float)tw / (float)disp_range;
5516 v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx) = taMath_float::gauss_den_sig(fx, gauss_sig);
5517 }
5518 v1b_stencils.FastEl(twidx, didx) = doff + tw;
5519 }
5520 }
5521 else if(disp == n_disps) {
5522 v1b_widths.FastEl(didx) = 1 + 2 * disp_range + end_ext;
5523 for(int tw=-disp_range; tw<=twe; tw++) {
5524 int twidx = tw + disp_range;
5525 if(tw > 0)
5526 v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx) = taMath_float::gauss_den_sig(0.0f, gauss_sig);
5527 else {
5528 float fx = (float)tw / (float)disp_range;
5529 v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx) = taMath_float::gauss_den_sig(fx, gauss_sig);
5530 }
5531 v1b_stencils.FastEl(twidx, didx) = doff + tw;
5532 }
5533 }
5534 else {
5535 v1b_widths.FastEl(didx) = 1 + 2 * disp_range;
5536 for(int tw=-disp_range; tw<=disp_range; tw++) {
5537 int twidx = tw + disp_range;
5538 float fx = (float)tw / (float)disp_range;
5539 v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx) = taMath_float::gauss_den_sig(fx, gauss_sig);
5540 v1b_stencils.FastEl(twidx, didx) = doff + tw;
5541 }
5542 }
5543 }
5544
5545 taMath_float::vec_norm_max(&v1b_weights); // max norm to 1
5546}
5547
5548void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::Connect_LeftEye(Projection* prjn) {
5549 InitStencils(prjn);
5550
5551 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5552 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5553 TwoDCoord gp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom; // same as sgp
5554
5555 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
5556 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
5557 int su_n = sun_geo.Product();
5558 int ru_n = run_geo.Product();
5559
5560 TwoDCoord ruc;
5561 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop >= 0; alloc_loop--) {
5562 int rgpidx = 0;
5563 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < gp_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
5564 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < gp_geo.x; ruc.x++, rgpidx++) {
5565 for(int didx=0; didx < tot_disps; didx++) {
5566 int dwd = v1b_widths.FastEl(didx);
5567
5568 int strui = didx * su_n; // starting index
5569 for(int sui=0; sui<su_n; sui++) {
5570 int rui = strui + sui;
5571 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5572 if(!ru_u) continue;
5573 if(!alloc_loop)
5574 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(dwd, prjn);
5575
5576 for(int twidx = 0; twidx < dwd; twidx++) {
5577 int off = v1b_stencils.FastEl(twidx, didx);
5578 // float wt = v1b_weights.FastEl(twidx, didx);
5579
5580 TwoDCoord suc = ruc;
5581 suc.x += off; // offset
5582 TwoDCoord suc_wrp = suc;
5583 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, gp_geo) && !wrap)
5584 continue;
5585 int sgpidx = send_lay->UnitGpIdxFmPos(suc_wrp);
5586 if(!send_lay->UnitGpIdxIsValid(sgpidx)) continue;
5587
5588 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
5589 if(!su_u) continue;
5590 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop);
5591 }
5592 }
5593 }
5594 }
5595 }
5596 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
5597 prjn->from->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
5598 }
5599 }
5600}
5601
5602void VisDisparityPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
5603 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
5604 if(cg->size == 1) { // right eye
5605 cg->Cn(0)->wt = 1.0f;
5606 return;
5607 }
5608
5609 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5610 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5611 TwoDCoord gp_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom; // same as sgp
5612
5613 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
5614 TwoDCoord sun_geo = send_lay->un_geom;
5615 int su_n = sun_geo.Product();
5616 int ru_n = run_geo.Product();
5617
5618 int rgpidx;
5619 int rui;
5620 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
5621 int didx = rui / su_n; // disparity index
5622
5623 int dwd = v1b_widths.SafeEl(didx);
5624 if(cg->size == dwd) {
5625 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
5626 float wt = v1b_weights.SafeEl(i, didx);
5627 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
5628 }
5629 }
5630 else {
5631 TwoDCoord ruc = recv_lay->UnitGpPosFmIdx(rgpidx);
5632 if(ruc.x < gp_geo.x / 2) {
5633 int st = dwd - cg->size;
5634 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
5635 float wt = v1b_weights.SafeEl(st + i, didx);
5636 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
5637 }
5638 }
5639 else {
5640 // actually just straight up
5641 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
5642 float wt = v1b_weights.SafeEl(i, didx);
5643 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
5644 }
5645 }
5646 }
5647}

5694
5695void VisDisparityLayerSpec::ComputeDispToExt(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
5696 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
5697 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
5698 float right = 0.0f;
5699 float left = 0.0f;
5700
5701 LeabraRecvCons* cg_r = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.SafeEl(0);
5702 if(!cg_r || cg_r->size <= 0) return;
5703 LeabraUnit* su_r = (LeabraUnit*)cg_r->Un(0);
5704 right = su_r->act_eq;
5705
5706 LeabraRecvCons* cg_l = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.SafeEl(1);
5707 if(!cg_l || cg_l->size <= 0) return;
5708 for(int i=0; i < cg_l->size; i++) {
5709 LeabraUnit* su_l = (LeabraUnit*)cg_l->Un(i);
5710 LeabraCon* cn = (LeabraCon*)cg_l->PtrCn(i); // recv mode
5711 float itm = cn->wt * su_l->act_eq;
5712 if(disp.max_l)
5713 left = MAX(left, itm)(((left) > (itm)) ? (left) : (itm));
5714 else
5715 left += itm;
5716 }
5717 if(!disp.max_l) {
5718 left /= (float)cg_l->size;
5719 }
5720
5721 float prod = MIN(left, right)(((left) < (right)) ? (left) : (right)); // min = product!
5722 u->misc_1 = prod;
5723
5724 if(disp.incl_other_res && net->cycle > 1) {
5725 for(int j=2; j<u->recv.size; j++) {
5726 LeabraRecvCons* cg = (LeabraRecvCons*)u->recv.FastEl(j);
5727 LeabraLayer* fm = (LeabraLayer*)cg->prjn->from.ptr();
5728 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)fm->spec.SPtr();
5729 if(!ls->InheritsFrom(&TA_VisDisparityLayerSpec)) continue;
5730 float netin = 0.0f;
5731 for(int i=0; i < cg->size; i++) {
5732 LeabraUnit* su = (LeabraUnit*)cg->Un(i);
5733// LeabraCon* cn = (LeabraCon*)cg->PtrCn(i); // recv mode
5734// float itm = cn->wt * su->misc_1; // note: using misc_1 prod val!
5735 float itm = su->misc_1; // no need for weight!
5736 if(disp.max_l)
5737 netin = MAX(netin, itm)(((netin) > (itm)) ? (netin) : (itm));
5738 else
5739 netin += itm;
5740 }
5741 if(!disp.max_l) {
5742 if(cg->size > 0)
5743 netin /= (float)cg->size;
5744 }
5745 prod = MIN(netin, prod)(((netin) < (prod)) ? (netin) : (prod));
5746 }
5747 }
5748
5749 u->SetExtFlag(Unit::EXT);
5750 u->ext = prod;
5751 }
5752 // todo: deal with horiz apeture prob
5753}
5754
5755void VisDisparityLayerSpec::Compute_ExtraNetin(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
5756 if(disp.updt_cycles < 0 || net->cycle <= disp.updt_cycles)
5757 ComputeDispToExt(lay, net); // always do it here -- avail for softclamp
5758}
5759
5760void VisDisparityLayerSpec::Compute_CycleStats(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
5761 if(!clamp.hard) {
5762 inherited::Compute_CycleStats(lay, net);
5763 return;
5764 }
5765 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraUnit, u, lay->units)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraUnit *u = (LeabraUnit
*) (lay->units).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); u; u = (LeabraUnit*)
(lay->units).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
5766 if(u->lesioned()) continue;
5767 u->act = u->ext;
5768 u->act_eq = u->act_nd = u->act;
5769 u->da = 0.0f; // I'm fully settled!
5770 }
5771 inherited::Compute_CycleStats(lay, net);
5772}

5774///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
5775// TiledGpRFOneToOnePrjnSpec
5776
5777void TiledGpRFOneToOnePrjnSpec::Initialize() {
5778 gauss_sigma = 1.0f;
5779 su_idx_st = 0;
5780 ru_idx_st = 0;
5781 gp_n_cons = -1;
5782}
5783
5784void TiledGpRFOneToOnePrjnSpec::Connect_UnitGroup(Projection* prjn, Layer* recv_lay,
5785 Layer* send_lay, int rgpidx, int sgpidx, int alloc_loop) {
5786 int ru_nunits = recv_lay->un_geom.n - ru_idx_st;
5787 int su_nunits = send_lay->un_geom.n - su_idx_st;
5788 int maxn = MIN(ru_nunits, su_nunits)(((ru_nunits) < (su_nunits)) ? (ru_nunits) : (su_nunits));
5789 if(gp_n_cons > 0)
5790 maxn = MIN(gp_n_cons, maxn)(((gp_n_cons) < (maxn)) ? (gp_n_cons) : (maxn));
5791
5792 if(reciprocal) { // reciprocal is backwards!
5793 for(int ui=0; ui < maxn; ui++) {
5794 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(su_idx_st + ui, sgpidx);
5795 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(ru_idx_st + ui, rgpidx);
5796 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
5797 su_u->ConnectFrom(ru_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // recip!
5798 }
5799 }
5800 else {
5801 for(int ui=0; ui < maxn; ui++) {
5802 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(ru_idx_st + ui, rgpidx);
5803 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(su_idx_st + ui, sgpidx);
5804 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
5805 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // recip!
5806 }
5807 }
5808}
5809
5810void TiledGpRFOneToOnePrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
5811 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
5812
5813 TwoDCoord rf_half_wd = send_gp_size / 2;
5814 FloatTwoDCoord rf_ctr = rf_half_wd;
5815 if(rf_half_wd * 2 == send_gp_size) // even
5816 rf_ctr -= .5f;
5817
5818 float sig_sq = (float)(rf_half_wd.x * rf_half_wd.x) * gauss_sigma * gauss_sigma;
5819
5820 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
5821 int su_x = i % send_gp_size.x;
5822 int su_y = i / send_gp_size.x;
5823
5824 float dst = taMath_float::euc_dist_sq(su_x, su_y, rf_ctr.x, rf_ctr.y);
5825 float wt = expf(-0.5 * dst / sig_sq);
5826
5827 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
5828 }
5829}

5832// TiledGpRFOneToOneWtsPrjnSpec
5833
5834void TiledGpRFOneToOneWtsPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
5835 one_to_one_wt = 0.8f;
5836 other_wt = 0.2f;
5837 init_wts = true;
5838}
5839
5840void TiledGpRFOneToOneWtsPrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
5841 inherited::C_Init_Weights(prjn, cg, ru); // always do regular init
5842 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
5843 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
5844
5845 int rgpidx;
5846 int rui;
5847 recv_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(ru->idx, rui, rgpidx);
5848 for(int i=0; i < cg->size; i++) {
5849 Unit* su = cg->Un(i);
5850 int sgpidx;
5851 int sui;
5852 send_lay->UnGpIdxFmUnitIdx(su->idx, sui, sgpidx);
5853 if(sui == rui)
5854 cg->Cn(i)->wt = one_to_one_wt;
5855 else
5856 cg->Cn(i)->wt = other_wt;
5857 }
5858}

5861///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
5862// V2toV4DepthPrjnSpec
5863
5864void V2toV4DepthPrjnSpec::Initialize() {
5865 depth_idx = 0;
5866}
5867
5868void V2toV4DepthPrjnSpec::Connect_UnitGroup(Projection* prjn, Layer* recv_lay,
5869 Layer* send_lay, int rgpidx, int sgpidx, int alloc_loop) {
5870 int ru_nunits = recv_lay->un_geom.n;
5871 int su_nunits = send_lay->un_geom.n;
5872 TwoDCoord sug;
5873
5874 if(reciprocal) { // reciprocal is backwards!
5875 for(int sui=0; sui < su_nunits; sui++) {
5876 sug.SetFmIndex(sui, send_lay->un_geom.x);
5877 int cur_depth = sug.y / 2; // v2bo has 2 per depth always
5878 if(cur_depth != depth_idx) continue;
5879 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
5880 for(int rui=0; rui < ru_nunits; rui++) {
5881 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5882 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
5883 su_u->ConnectFrom(ru_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // recip!
5884 }
5885 }
5886 }
5887 else {
5888 for(int rui=0; rui < ru_nunits; rui++) {
5889 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
5890 for(int sui=0; sui < su_nunits; sui++) {
5891 sug.SetFmIndex(sui, send_lay->un_geom.x);
5892 int cur_depth = sug.y / 2; // v2bo has 2 per depth always
5893 if(cur_depth != depth_idx) continue;
5894 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(sui, sgpidx);
5895 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
5896 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // recip!
5897 }
5898 }
5899 }
5900}

5934
5935bool LeabraV1LayerSpec::CheckConfig_Layer(Layer* ly, bool quiet) {
5936 LeabraLayer* lay = (LeabraLayer*)ly;
5937 if(!inherited::CheckConfig_Layer(lay, quiet)) return false;
5938
5939 if(!feat_inhib.on) return true;
5940
5941 bool rval = true;
5942 lay->CheckError(!lay->unit_groups, quiet, rval,
5943 "does not have unit groups -- MUST have unit groups!");
5944
5945 lay->CheckError(lay->un_geom.x != feat_inhib.n_angles, quiet, rval,
5946 "un_geom.x must be = to feat_inhib.n_angles -- is not!");
5947 return rval;
5948}
5949
5950static void v1_get_angles(float angf, float& cosx, float& siny) {
5951 cosx = taMath_float::cos(angf);
5952 siny = taMath_float::sin(angf);
5953 // always normalize by the largest value so that it is equal to 1
5954 if(fabsf(cosx) > fabsf(siny)) {
5955 siny = siny / fabsf(cosx); // must come first!
5956 cosx = cosx / fabsf(cosx);
5957 }
5958 else {
5959 cosx = cosx / fabsf(siny);
5960 siny = siny / fabsf(siny);
5961 }
5962}
5963
5964void LeabraV1LayerSpec::UpdateStencils() {
5965 v1s_ang_slopes.SetGeom(3,2,2,feat_inhib.n_angles);
5966 float ang_inc = taMath_float::pi / (float)feat_inhib.n_angles;
5967 for(int ang=0; ang<feat_inhib.n_angles; ang++) {
5968 float cosx, siny;
5969 float angf = (float)ang * ang_inc;
5970 v1_get_angles(angf, cosx, siny);
5971 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, LINE, ang) = cosx;
5972 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, LINE, ang) = siny;
5973
5974 v1_get_angles(angf + taMath_float::pi * .5f, cosx, siny);
5975 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, ORTHO, ang) = cosx;
5976 v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, ORTHO, ang) = siny;
5977 }
5978 // config: x,y coords by tot_ni_len, by angles
5979 v1s_ni_stencils.SetGeom(3, 2, feat_inhib.tot_ni_len, feat_inhib.n_angles);
5980
5981 for(int ang = 0; ang < feat_inhib.n_angles; ang++) { // angles
5982 for(int lpt=-feat_inhib.inhib_d; lpt <= feat_inhib.inhib_d; lpt++) {
5983 int lpdx = lpt + feat_inhib.inhib_d;
5984 v1s_ni_stencils.FastEl(X, lpdx, ang) =
5985 taMath_float::rint((float)lpt * v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(X, ORTHO, ang)); // ortho
5986 v1s_ni_stencils.FastEl(Y, lpdx, ang) =
5987 taMath_float::rint((float)lpt * v1s_ang_slopes.FastEl(Y, ORTHO, ang));
5988 }
5989 }
5990}

5992
5993void LeabraV1LayerSpec::Compute_FeatGpActive(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraUnit_Group* fugp,
5994 LeabraNetwork* net) {
5995// fugp->active_buf.size = 0;
5996// for(int ui=0; ui<fugp->size; ui++) {
5997// LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)fugp->FastEl(ui);
5998// LeabraUnit_Group* u_own = (LeabraUnit_Group*)u->owner; // NOT fugp!
5999// if(u->i_thr >= u_own->i_val.g_i) // compare to their own group's inhib val!
6000// fugp->active_buf.Add(u);
6001// }
6002}
6003
6004
6005void LeabraV1LayerSpec::Compute_ApplyInhib(LeabraLayer* lay, LeabraNetwork* net) {
6006 if(!feat_inhib.on) { // do the normal
6007 inherited::Compute_ApplyInhib(lay, net);
6008 return;
6009 }
6010 if((net->cycle >= 0) && lay->hard_clamped)
6011 return; // don't do this during normal processing
6012 if(inhib.type == LeabraInhibSpec::UNIT_INHIB) return; // otherwise overwrites!
6013
6014 for(int gpidx=0; gpidx < lay->gp_geom.n; gpidx++) {
6015 LeabraUnGpData* gpd = lay->ungp_data.FastEl(gpidx);
6016 LeabraInhib* thr = (LeabraInhib*)gpd;
6017 TwoDCoord sc; // simple coords
6018 sc.SetFmIndex(gpidx, lay->gp_geom.x);
6019
6020 int nunits = lay->UnitAccess_NUnits(Layer::ACC_GP);
6021 float inhib_val = thr->i_val.g_i;
6022 // note: not doing tie break!
6023
6024 TwoDCoord fc; // v1s feature coords
6025 TwoDCoord oc; // other coord
6026 float uidx = 0;
6027 for(int polclr = 0; polclr < lay->un_geom.y; polclr++) { // polclr features
6028 fc.y = polclr;
6029 for(int ang = 0; ang < feat_inhib.n_angles; ang++, uidx++) { // angles
6030 fc.x = ang;
6031 float feat_inhib_max = 0.0f;
6032 for(int lpdx=0; lpdx < feat_inhib.tot_ni_len; lpdx++) { // go out to neighs
6033 if(lpdx == feat_inhib.inhib_d) continue; // skip self
6034 int xp = v1s_ni_stencils.FastEl(X,lpdx,ang);
6035 int yp = v1s_ni_stencils.FastEl(Y,lpdx,ang);
6036 oc.x = sc.x + xp;
6037 oc.y = sc.y + yp;
6038 if(oc.WrapClip(feat_inhib.wrap, lay->gp_geom)) {
6039 if(!feat_inhib.wrap) continue; // bail on clipping only
6040 }
6041 LeabraUnit* oth_unit = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAtGpCoord(oc, fc);
6042 float oth_ithr = oth_unit->i_thr;
6043 float ogi = feat_inhib.inhib_g * oth_ithr; // note: directly on ithr!
6044 feat_inhib_max = MAX(feat_inhib_max, ogi)(((feat_inhib_max) > (ogi)) ? (feat_inhib_max) : (ogi));
6045 }
6046
6047 float gi_eff = MAX(inhib_val, feat_inhib_max)(((inhib_val) > (feat_inhib_max)) ? (inhib_val) : (feat_inhib_max
));
6048 LeabraUnit* u = (LeabraUnit*)lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx((int)uidx, gpidx);
6049 u->Compute_ApplyInhib(net, gi_eff);
6050 }
6051 }
6052 }
6053}

6056///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6057// Cerebellum-related special guys
6058
6059void CerebConj2PrjnSpec::Initialize() {
6060 init_wts = true;
6061 rf_width = 6;
6062 rf_move = 3.0f;
6063 wrap = false;
6064 gauss_sigma = 1.0f;
6065}
6066
6067void CerebConj2PrjnSpec::Connect_impl(Projection* prjn) {
6068 if(!(bool)prjn->from) return;
6069 if(prjn->layer->units.leaves == 0) // an empty layer!
6070 return;
6071 if(TestWarning(!prjn->layer->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
6072 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
6073 return;
6074 }
6075 if(prjn->recv_idx == 0)
6076 Connect_Outer(prjn);
6077 else
6078 Connect_Inner(prjn);
6079}
6080
6081void CerebConj2PrjnSpec::Connect_Outer(Projection* prjn) {
6082 int n_cons = rf_width.Product();
6083 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
6084 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
6085
6086 TwoDCoord rf_half_wd = rf_width / 2;
6087 TwoDCoord rug_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
6088 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
6089 TwoDCoord su_geo = send_lay->flat_geom;
6090
6091 TwoDCoord ruc;
6092 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
6093 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < rug_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
6094 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < rug_geo.x; ruc.x++) {
6095 int rgpidx = recv_lay->UnitGpIdxFmPos(ruc);
6096 if(!recv_lay->UnitGpIdxIsValid(rgpidx)) continue;
6097
6098 TwoDCoord su_st;
6099 if(wrap) {
6100 su_st.x = (int)floor((float)ruc.x * rf_move.x) - rf_half_wd.x;
6101 su_st.y = (int)floor((float)ruc.y * rf_move.y) - rf_half_wd.y;
6102 }
6103 else {
6104 su_st.x = (int)floor((float)ruc.x * rf_move.x);
6105 su_st.y = (int)floor((float)ruc.y * rf_move.y);
6106 }
6107
6108 su_st.WrapClip(wrap, su_geo);
6109 TwoDCoord su_ed = su_st + rf_width;
6110 if(wrap) {
6111 su_ed.WrapClip(wrap, su_geo); // just wrap ends too
6112 }
6113 else {
6114 if(su_ed.x > su_geo.x) {
6115 su_ed.x = su_geo.x; su_st.x = su_ed.x - rf_width.x;
6116 }
6117 if(su_ed.y > su_geo.y) {
6118 su_ed.y = su_geo.y; su_st.y = su_ed.y - rf_width.y;
6119 }
6120 }
6121
6122 for(int rui=0; rui<recv_lay->un_geom.n; rui++) {
6123 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rgpidx);
6124 if(!alloc_loop)
6125 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(n_cons, prjn);
6126
6127 TwoDCoord suc;
6128 TwoDCoord suc_wrp;
6129 for(suc.y = 0; suc.y < rf_width.y; suc.y++) {
6130 for(suc.x = 0; suc.x < rf_width.x; suc.x++) {
6131 suc_wrp = su_st + suc;
6132 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, su_geo) && !wrap)
6133 continue;
6134 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtCoord(suc_wrp);
6135 if(!su_u) continue;
6136 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
6137
6138 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // don't check: saves lots of time!
6139 }
6140 }
6141 }
6142 }
6143 }
6144 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
6145 send_lay->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
6146 }
6147 }
6148}
6149
6150void CerebConj2PrjnSpec::Connect_Inner(Projection* prjn) {
6151 Layer* recv_lay = prjn->layer;
6152 Layer* send_lay = prjn->from;
6153
6154 if(!(bool)send_lay) return;
6155 if(recv_lay->units.leaves == 0) // an empty layer!
6156 return;
6157 if(TestWarning(!recv_lay->unit_groups, "Connect_impl",
6158 "requires recv layer to have unit groups!")) {
6159 return;
6160 }
6161
6162 int n_cons = rf_width.Product();
6163 TwoDCoord rf_half_wd = rf_width / 2;
6164 TwoDCoord rug_geo = recv_lay->gp_geom;
6165 TwoDCoord run_geo = recv_lay->un_geom;
6166 TwoDCoord su_geo = send_lay->flat_geom;
6167
6168 for(int alloc_loop=1; alloc_loop>=0; alloc_loop--) {
6169 for(int rug=0;rug<recv_lay->gp_geom.n;rug++) {
6170 TwoDCoord ruc;
6171 for(ruc.y = 0; ruc.y < run_geo.y; ruc.y++) {
6172 for(ruc.x = 0; ruc.x < run_geo.x; ruc.x++) {
6173 int rui = ruc.y * run_geo.x + ruc.x;
6174 Unit* ru_u = recv_lay->UnitAtUnGpIdx(rui, rug);
6175 if(!ru_u) continue;
6176 if(!alloc_loop)
6177 ru_u->RecvConsPreAlloc(n_cons, prjn);
6178
6179 TwoDCoord su_st;
6180 if(wrap) {
6181 su_st.x = (int)floor((float)ruc.x * rf_move.x) - rf_half_wd.x;
6182 su_st.y = (int)floor((float)ruc.y * rf_move.y) - rf_half_wd.y;
6183 }
6184 else {
6185 su_st.x = (int)floor((float)ruc.x * rf_move.x);
6186 su_st.y = (int)floor((float)ruc.y * rf_move.y);
6187 }
6188
6189 su_st.WrapClip(wrap, su_geo);
6190 TwoDCoord su_ed = su_st + rf_width;
6191 if(wrap) {
6192 su_ed.WrapClip(wrap, su_geo); // just wrap ends too
6193 }
6194 else {
6195 if(su_ed.x > su_geo.x) {
6196 su_ed.x = su_geo.x; su_st.x = su_ed.x - rf_width.x;
6197 }
6198 if(su_ed.y > su_geo.y) {
6199 su_ed.y = su_geo.y; su_st.y = su_ed.y - rf_width.y;
6200 }
6201 }
6202
6203 TwoDCoord suc;
6204 TwoDCoord suc_wrp;
6205 for(suc.y = 0; suc.y < rf_width.y; suc.y++) {
6206 for(suc.x = 0; suc.x < rf_width.x; suc.x++) {
6207 suc_wrp = su_st + suc;
6208 if(suc_wrp.WrapClip(wrap, su_geo) && !wrap)
6209 continue;
6210 Unit* su_u = send_lay->UnitAtCoord(suc_wrp);
6211 if(su_u == NULL__null) continue;
6212 if(!self_con && (su_u == ru_u)) continue;
6213 ru_u->ConnectFrom(su_u, prjn, alloc_loop); // don't check: saves lots of time!
6214 }
6215 }
6216 }
6217 }
6218 }
6219 if(alloc_loop) { // on first pass through alloc loop, do sending allocations
6220 send_lay->SendConsPostAlloc(prjn);
6221 }
6222 }
6223}
6224
6225void CerebConj2PrjnSpec::C_Init_Weights(Projection* prjn, RecvCons* cg, Unit* ru) {
6226 TwoDCoord rf_half_wd = rf_width / 2;
6227 FloatTwoDCoord rf_ctr = rf_half_wd;
6228 if(rf_half_wd * 2 == rf_width) // even
6229 rf_ctr -= .5f;
6230
6231 for(int i=0; i<cg->size; i++) {
6232 int su_x = i % rf_width.x;
6233 int su_y = i / rf_width.x;
6234
6235 float dst = taMath_float::euc_dist_sq(su_x, su_y, rf_ctr.x, rf_ctr.y);
6236 float wt = expf(-0.5 * dst / (gauss_sigma * gauss_sigma));
6237
6238 cg->Cn(i)->wt = wt;
6239 }
6240}
6241
6242bool CerebConj2PrjnSpec::TrgRecvFmSend(int send_x, int send_y) {
6243 trg_send_geom.x = send_x;
6244 trg_send_geom.y = send_y;
6245
6246 if(wrap)
6247 trg_recv_geom = (trg_send_geom / rf_move);
6248 else
6249 trg_recv_geom = (trg_send_geom / rf_move) - 1;
6250
6251 // now fix it the other way
6252 if(wrap)
6253 trg_send_geom = (trg_recv_geom * rf_move);
6254 else
6255 trg_send_geom = ((trg_recv_geom +1) * rf_move);
6256
6257 DataChanged(DCR_ITEM_UPDATED);
6258 return (trg_send_geom.x == send_x && trg_send_geom.y == send_y);
6259}
6260
6261bool CerebConj2PrjnSpec::TrgSendFmRecv(int recv_x, int recv_y) {
6262 trg_recv_geom.x = recv_x;
6263 trg_recv_geom.y = recv_y;
6264
6265 if(wrap)
6266 trg_send_geom = (trg_recv_geom * rf_move);
6267 else
6268 trg_send_geom = ((trg_recv_geom+1) * rf_move);
6269
6270 // now fix it the other way
6271 if(wrap)
6272 trg_recv_geom = (trg_send_geom / rf_move);
6273 else
6274 trg_recv_geom = (trg_send_geom / rf_move) - 1;
6275
6276 DataChanged(DCR_ITEM_UPDATED);
6277 return (trg_recv_geom.x == recv_x && trg_recv_geom.y == recv_y);
6278}

6287
6288bool LeabraWizard::UpdateInputDataFmNet(Network* net, DataTable* data_table) {
6289 if(TestError(!data_table || !net, "UpdateInputDataFmNet",
6290 "must specify both a network and a data table")) return false;
6291 data_table->StructUpdate(true);
6292 FOREACH_ELEM_IN_GROUP(LeabraLayer, lay, net->layers)if (bool FOREACH_done = false) { } else for (taLeafItr FOREACH_itr
; !FOREACH_done; FOREACH_done = true) for (LeabraLayer *lay =
(LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).FirstEl(FOREACH_itr); lay; lay
= (LeabraLayer*) (net->layers).NextEl(FOREACH_itr)) {
6293 if(lay->layer_type == Layer::HIDDEN) continue;
6294 int lay_idx = 0;
6295
6296 LeabraLayerSpec* ls = (LeabraLayerSpec*)lay->GetLayerSpec();
6297 if(ls->InheritsFrom(&TA_ScalarValLayerSpec) && !((ScalarValLayerSpec*)ls)->scalar.clamp_pat) {
6298 if(lay->unit_groups) {
6299 data_table->FindMakeColName
6300 (lay->name, lay_idx, DataTable::VT_FLOAT, 4, 1, 1,
6301 MAX(lay->gp_geom.x,1)(((lay->gp_geom.x) > (1)) ? (lay->gp_geom.x) : (1)), MAX(lay->gp_geom.y,1)(((lay->gp_geom.y) > (1)) ? (lay->gp_geom.y) : (1)));
6302 }
6303 else {
6304 data_table->FindMakeColName
6305 (lay->name, lay_idx, DataTable::VT_FLOAT, 2, 1, 1);
6306 }
6307 }
6308 else if(ls->InheritsFrom(&TA_TwoDValLayerSpec) && !((TwoDValLayerSpec*)ls)->twod.clamp_pat) {
6309 TwoDValLayerSpec* tdls = (TwoDValLayerSpec*)ls;
6310 int nx = tdls->twod.n_vals * 2;
6311 if(lay->unit_groups) {
6312 data_table->FindMakeColName
6313 (lay->name, lay_idx, DataTable::VT_FLOAT, 4, nx, 1,
6314 MAX(lay->gp_geom.x,1)(((lay->gp_geom.x) > (1)) ? (lay->gp_geom.x) : (1)), MAX(lay->gp_geom.y,1)(((lay->gp_geom.y) > (1)) ? (lay->gp_geom.y) : (1)));
6315 }
6316 else {
6317 data_table->FindMakeColName
6318 (lay->name, lay_idx, DataTable::VT_FLOAT, 2, nx, 1);
6319 }
6320 }
6321 else {
6322 if(lay->unit_groups) {
6323 data_table->FindMakeColName
6324 (lay->name, lay_idx, DataTable::VT_FLOAT, 4,
6325 MAX(lay->un_geom.x,1)(((lay->un_geom.x) > (1)) ? (lay->un_geom.x) : (1)), MAX(lay->un_geom.y,1)(((lay->un_geom.y) > (1)) ? (lay->un_geom.y) : (1)),
6326 MAX(lay->gp_geom.x,1)(((lay->gp_geom.x) > (1)) ? (lay->gp_geom.x) : (1)), MAX(lay->gp_geom.y,1)(((lay->gp_geom.y) > (1)) ? (lay->gp_geom.y) : (1)));
6327 }
6328 else {
6329 data_table->FindMakeColName
6330 (lay->name, lay_idx, DataTable::VT_FLOAT, 2,
6331 MAX(lay->un_geom.x,1)(((lay->un_geom.x) > (1)) ? (lay->un_geom.x) : (1)), MAX(lay->un_geom.y,1)(((lay->un_geom.y) > (1)) ? (lay->un_geom.y) : (1)));
6332 }
6333 }
6334 }
6335 data_table->StructUpdate(false);
6336// if(taMisc::gui_active) {
6337// tabMisc::DelayedFunCall_gui(data_table, "BrowserSelectMe");
6338// }
6339
6340 UpdateLayerWriters(net, data_table);
6341
6342 return true;
6343}
6344
6345///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6346// SRN Context
6347///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
6348
6349bool LeabraWizard::SRNContext(LeabraNetwork* net) {
6350 if(TestError(!net, "SRNContext", "must have basic constructed network first")) {
6351 return false;
6352 }
6353 OneToOnePrjnSpec* otop = (OneToOnePrjnSpec*)net->FindMakeSpec("CtxtPrjn", &TA_OneToOnePrjnSpec);
6354 LeabraContextLayerSpec* ctxts = (LeabraContextLayerSpec*)net->FindMakeSpec("CtxtLayerSpec", &TA_LeabraContextLayerSpec);
6355
6356 if((otop == NULL__null) || (ctxts == NULL__null)) {
6357 return false;
6358 }
6359
6360 LeabraLayer* hidden = (LeabraLayer*)net->FindLayer("Hidden");
6361 LeabraLayer* ctxt = (LeabraLayer*)net->FindMakeLayer("Context");
6362
6363 if((hidden == NULL__null) || (ctxt == NULL__null)) return false;
6364
6365 ctxt->SetLayerSpec(ctxts);
6366 ctxt->un_geom = hidden->un_geom;
6367
6368 net->layers.MoveAfter(hidden, ctxt);
6369 net->FindMakePrjn(ctxt, hidden, otop); // one-to-one into the ctxt layer
6370 net->FindMakePrjn(hidden, ctxt); // std prjn back into the hidden from context
6371 net->Build();
6372 return true;
6373}
